The conference will open on the 19th and close on the 22nd. After the conference, all the delegates will be invited to visit the construction projects on the entire island. Jiang and Liu are scheduled to return to China in mid-January of next year. (Special dispatch on the 9th)

Zhang Zhen's Investigation of Overseas Chinese Affairs in Southeast Asia

(Nanjing) Zhang Zhen said that he went to Southeast Asia to investigate overseas Chinese affairs in the Philippines, Java, Sumatra, the Malay Peninsula, Burma, Siam, and other places. He investigated the overseas Chinese affairs in all the places he passed through. There are millions of overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia, with a history of over 700 years. They have diligently engaged in industry and commerce. After the European War, economic panic and national disasters increased. Countries such as the Philippines, Annam, and Burma revised their immigration regulations, restricting the import of overseas Chinese. The Malay Peninsula and other places restricted the number of immigrants, reducing the import of overseas Chinese. The Dutch East Indies and Siam increased the population tax, reducing the number of overseas Chinese imports. In other respects, as the scholars' knowledge gradually improves, the status of our overseas Chinese is also affected. However, although the situation of overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia is not as good as it used to be, it is still more comfortable than that of compatriots in the interior. Whether they will be able to return to their original state in the future depends on whether domestic politics can be rectified and whether diplomacy can be successful. I have no proposals for the Fifth Plenary Session. (Special dispatch on the 9th)

Crackdown on Traditional Chinese Medicine in the Philippines

(Nanjing) The Philippines has cracked down on traditional Chinese medicine, and three people have been arrested by secret agents. The Chinese Medicine Association sent a letter to Consul Deng Zongying, requesting him to negotiate with the Philippine government repeatedly, but without result. The overseas Chinese physicians in the Philippines have sent a representative, Lü Liping, back to China to petition. On the 9th, he visited Jiao Yitang, director of the Central National Medical Hall, and explained the situation, requesting the establishment of a branch of the National Medical Hall in the Philippines. Lü is scheduled to submit a petition to the Fifth Plenary Session, the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 10th, requesting negotiations with the Philippine government to release the Chinese medicine practitioners and provide them with protection. (Special dispatch on the 9th)

The Rumor of Re-discussion of the Adultery Case in the Criminal Law is Not True

(Nanjing) It has been reported that some members of the Legislative Yuan believe that Article 239 of the Criminal Law, as finally amended, is still inappropriate and have jointly requested the Central Committee to submit it to the Legislative Yuan for reconsideration. According to reliable sources, the members of the Legislative Yuan who also serve on the Central Committee not only have no such plan but have never discussed this matter. It is thought to be a rumor from the outside world. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 9th)

Taoist Associations Must Not Promote Superstition

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior requested the Central Committee to explain whether Taoist associations could be organized. The Central People's Movement 指委會 replied that Taoist associations are religious groups and may be permitted to organize according to law. However, Taoist priests who make a living by displaying signs similar to that of shamans must not use the organization to promote superstition. This should be clearly stipulated in the articles of association, and if there are any activities that promote superstition, they should be strictly prohibited according to law. The matter has been communicated to the provincial and municipal governments for investigation. (Special dispatch on the 9th)

Guarantee Money for Savings Deposits Must Be Implemented Throughout the Year

(Nanjing) Guarantee money for savings deposits must be implemented throughout the year except for Shanghai. The Ministry of Finance yesterday instructed local banking associations and chambers of commerce to formulate the following measures: 1. For head offices or general associations located in Shanghai, the guarantee reserves that all their branches in various locations should deposit for receiving savings deposits should be reviewed by the Savings Guarantee Reserve Management Committee established in Shanghai and kept by the Central Bank of China in Shanghai. 2. For head offices or general associations located outside Shanghai, the guarantee reserves that their head offices and branches (except for the Shanghai branch) should deposit for receiving savings deposits should be kept by the local Central Bank of China or the bank designated by the Ministry. However, regarding the types, amounts, and values of bonds to be deposited, a list should still be prepared in accordance with Article 20 of the Regulations of the Savings Deposit Guarantee Reserve Management Committee and Article 12 of the Detailed Rules of the Committee and submitted to the Committee for review and approval to ensure responsibility. These measures must be followed in their entirety after the end of the accounting year. (Special dispatch on the 9th)

Hunan and Guangxi Armies Join Forces to Block the Remnant Bandits

(Hong Kong) Chen Jitang telegraphed the Central Government requesting continued subsidies for military expenses of 600,000 yuan per month. The fleeing bandits are wandering in Wugang, Suining, Chengwu, and Longsheng. The Central Government and the Hunan and Guangxi armies have joined forces to pursue them in a large-scale attack. Chen Jitang appointed Li Zhenqiu as Deputy Commander of the First Army, and Mo Xide was appointed to succeed him as Commander of the First Division. Zhang Da was appointed as Deputy Commander of the Second Army. (Special dispatch on the 9th)

(Guangzhou) According to official reports received here today, the Communist bandits who invaded Guangxi Province have all been defeated and are retreating northwest. The main force of the Fourth Army Group is currently pursuing the defeated bandits in Meixikou, Suining, and other places. The Hunan Army is also assisting in the suppression. At the same time, the Guangxi Army is advancing towards the border of Guizhou to join forces with the Guizhou Army to intercept them. The Guilin Militia is currently searching for the remnants of the Communist bandits in the territory. (Reuters dispatch on the 9th)

Regulations on the Organization of the Fujian-Jiangxi Pacification Headquarters Promulgated

(Xiamen) The regulations on the organization of the Pacification Headquarters have been promulgated. The headquarters will have a Chief of Staff, a Commander of the Reserve Army, and eight department heads. The responsibilities of the department heads include suppressing remnant bandits, completing transportation, training the people, handling post-banditry affairs, and reorganizing and training local militias. The military and local militias within the jurisdiction of the provincial security team will be under their command. To implement pacification, they may command the administrative commissioners, regional security commanders, and county government military and political organs in the jurisdiction and neighboring border areas at any time. Party and government affairs in the pacification area will be handled in consultation with the provincial party headquarters and the provincial government, and they may handle matters expediently when necessary. The Fujian-Jiangxi Pacification Headquarters has the same organization. (Special dispatch on the 9th)

(Xiamen) Jiang Dingwen announced that the main tasks of pacification in the future are: 1. To eliminate remnant bandits and suppress local gentry. 2. To be lenient to the people's army, but to thoroughly annihilate those who are deluded. 3. To lift the blockade of the bandit areas recently. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 9th)

Eastern Luan Silver Dollars Flow Into Puppet Territory

(Tianjin) A large number of silver dollars from eastern Luan have flowed into the puppet territory, causing a shortage of cash in eastern Luan. The Tianjin Customs has been ordered to instruct the tax checkpoints at the Great Wall ports to restrict the export of silver. Each person is allowed to carry a maximum of 120 yuan; the excess will be confiscated. The puppet customs is also cracking down on large quantities of silver dollars coming in because the influx of our silver has caused the puppet silver to depreciate. An order was issued this month to strictly prohibit large amounts of imports at various customs checkpoints. (Special dispatch on the 9th)

A Tang Dynasty Ship Discovered in Yuncheng

(Jinan) Farmers in Liang Village, south of Yuncheng, dug up a Tang Dynasty ship while digging a vegetable cellar. The ship is over eight zhang long and contains more than a dozen ancient three-eared tile jars and some ancient coins from the Dachong and Tianyou reign periods of the Tang Dynasty, which are stored in the People's Education Hall. Digging is still in progress. (Special dispatch on the 9th)

(Kaifeng) The project of diverting the Yellow River into the Hui River through the Libian Gate has been completed. The gate was opened for testing on the 9th. The Construction Department invited important figures from the provincial capital to observe (9th dispatch).

Shangguan Yunxiang Passes Through Zhengzhou to Xuchang

(Zhengzhou) Shangguan Yunxiang passed through Zhengzhou from Bian at 4 PM on the 8th, heading to Xuchang. According to reports, the remnants of the pseudo-25th Army, numbering about 500, have repeatedly fled to the Lushi Guanzhuang area in western Henan. The general headquarters will move from Xuchang to Lingbao within days to facilitate command and suppression (8th dispatch from the Central News Agency).

Weng Wenhao Travels from Bian to Jiaozuo

(Zhengzhou) Weng Wenhao passed through Zhengzhou from Bian on the evening of the 8th, heading to Jiaozuo. According to reports, he had agreed with Zhang Jingyu in Bian on specific measures to reorganize the Zhongfu Company. He will officially take office after arriving in Jiaozuo. As for the overall plan, it will be formulated after detailed investigation (8th dispatch from the Central News Agency).

Huainan Railway Mine Newly Dug Coal Shaft

(Bengbu) The combined Huainan Railway Mine section has been completed, and coal sales have increased sharply. The mine recently dug a new coal shaft at Guanyin Temple and is actively mining it. The entire mine produces 800 tons of coal per day (9th dispatch).

Rinji Hayashi Concurrently Serves as President of the Manchurian Affairs Bureau

(Tokyo) The Manchurian Affairs Bureau, as its budget has been approved by the Diet, will soon be realized. The office will be located in the former Ministry of Home Affairs building. Army Minister Hayashi will concurrently serve as president, and Haruo Matsui, president of the Resources Bureau, will serve as vice-president (9th dispatch from the Japan United Press).

Commentary

The Significance of Celebrating the Victory Over the Communists - Chiang Kai-shek

The victory over the Communists is indeed the unified sentiment of all our people,

And the result of the joint efforts of comrades in the rear.

In recent days, compatriots from all over the country, celebrating the completion of the Communist suppression in Jiangxi Province, the Communist nests accumulated over the years, fundamentally destroyed, and the Communist-held areas of Fujian and Jiangxi gradually recovered, expectations of several years fulfilled in one day, have held grand celebrations of the victory over the Communists. They have also given warm慰問 to the Communist suppression soldiers. Today, the capital and Shanghai have also held grand gatherings. Telegrams of慰勉 arrive one after another. I, Chiang Kai-shek, am even more惶愧 about this. From the perspective of the Communist suppression soldiers, the Red bandits harm the country and the people, a common anger shared by all. They have long sought their destruction. Until now, I still feel guilty for not fulfilling my duty. How dare I accept such encouragement? From the perspective of the nation, eliminating violence and punishing evil is an execution of heavenly justice. As for eradicating the bandits, there is no real victory to speak of. Moreover, wherever the troops go, the people are affected, with casualties, disabilities, and scars everywhere. How can we bear to speak of victory? Thinking about the pain after it subsides, there is only sorrow. If we must speak of the victory over the Communists, is it not more accurate to say it is the victory of the people? Therefore, today's celebration is truly a celebration of the victory of our entire nation. I hope that our people will be united, continue their efforts, see it through to the end, and eliminate the evil influence, so as not to betray today's grand celebration. I, Chiang Kai-shek, have said that suppressing the Communists requires seven parts political power, and military force is only three parts. Today's success in suppressing the Communists, while the Party and the country cannot bear to forget the loyalty of the officers and soldiers who died and sacrificed at the front, is especially due to the comrades in the rear who worked hard and endured hardships, without fear of difficulties, consolidating politics, maintaining order, planning finances, and raising military supplies with perseverance and hard work. This enabled the officers and soldiers at the front to have no shortage of weapons and ammunition, and to have no lack of pay and provisions, eliminating worries about the rear, and encouraging them to advance bravely. In short, it is the result of the joint efforts of the front and rear. The support and encouragement of comrades and compatriots in the rear in various aspects of politics and society have been especially significant. I, Chiang Kai-shek, on behalf of the officers and soldiers at the front, would like to express my sincere gratitude to the comrades in the rear who are responsible for political, financial, security, transportation, and public opinion matters. I also confirm that the greatest force behind the success of this Communist suppression is the unified and unwavering sentiment of the people across the country who hate the Red bandits and vow not to coexist with them. The manifestation of this unified sentiment not only gave the soldiers fighting at the front infinite encouragement and comfort, but also gave those who had gone astray the determination to turn back and return. The trend of popular sentiment is enough to prove that the Communist bandits' hypocritical and cruel actions cannot exist in the world, and are especially intolerable to the Chinese people. From the experience of this Communist suppression, it can be seen that the power of a unified public sentiment is unparalleled. This kind of intangible power surpasses any tangible power and is enough to overcome any difficulty. If the unified sentiment used in the past for suppressing the Communists is used for saving the country, I believe that any crisis facing the nation can be averted by the unified sentiment of our people. And what demonstrates the unified sentiment of the whole country is the support of the government's domestic and foreign policies and the firm belief that the policies implemented by the government will surely reap the final results. I, Chiang Kai-shek, hope that my compatriots will think deeply about this. During the Communist suppression, if the people of the whole country had not regarded the success or failure of the Communist suppression as their own vital interest, and had not had a unified trust and expectation in the Communist suppression military, giving various spiritual and material encouragement, then how could this huge national disaster have been eliminated amidst such great difficulties? The previous example is clear. The national crisis is not over. I earnestly hope that my compatriots will cherish this valuable lesson and use the same sentiment for suppressing the Communists to unite in saving the country. Then the soldiers who sacrificed in suppressing the Communists will be able to rest in peace, and the honors, rewards, and benefits will be even greater. As for the remnant Communists in Jiangxi Province, although there are still remnants who have escaped westward, we firmly believe that the deep-rooted Communist nests in southern Jiangxi, which have been entrenched for many years, have been eradicated. The remaining fleeing bandits are like frightened animals running in disarray, having lost their foothold, and are scattered and weak. In the future, their complete elimination will certainly not be as difficult as when we attacked their main nests. The goal of the roving bandits is Sichuan and Guizhou. Although the land of Sichuan and Guizhou is vast and the products are abundant, surpassing those of southern Jiangxi, the people of Sichuan and Guizhou are inherently strong, have strong self-defense capabilities, and deeply hate the Red bandits. They will certainly not be as easily coerced or tempted as the people of southern Jiangxi. The westward fleeing of the bandits will have no foothold in Sichuan and Guizhou. Observing the notorious bandit chiefs of past dynasties, none did not mark their demise and collapse with their entry into Sichuan and Guizhou. We can believe that future suppression will be easier. Our armed comrades must act with their greatest determination and make their last effort to eliminate this national disaster, so as to comfort the expectations of the elders and compatriots across the country. I further hope that the whole country will be united, sincere, and unremitting, and work together to eliminate this obstacle to revival, so as to lay a new foundation for the nation.

Yugoslavia's Hostility Towards Hungary Increases Tension in Central Europe

3,000 Hungarian僑민 Expelled Back Home

Serbs Repeatedly Invade Hungarian Territory

France and Italy Side with Each Side, Britain Acts Cautiously

(London) The Yugoslavian authorities' campaign of hostility against Hungarian 僑민 shows no signs of abating, hence the situation in Central Europe is more tense than before. Last night, a number of Hungarians returned to Hungary from Yugoslavia. Up to now, 3,000 Hungarian僑민 have been expelled from Yugoslavia. These people, young and old, knelt beside their hastily packed bags upon reaching the 四格特 station on the border, praying to God to protect them, to arrive safely in a place where their lives would no longer be endangered.

After the arrival of the most recent batch of refugees, Hungarian university students gathered to demonstrate against Yugoslavia. The Hungarian authorities quickly dispatched a large police force to prevent further incidents.

It has been reported that several invasions have occurred along the border. The most recent one involved a team of armed Serbians penetrating 300 yards into Hungarian territory. However, the Hungarian government has remained calm and focused on providing relief to the refugees, showing a desire to gradually calm public anger.

Yesterday, the trend in the Yugoslavian capital reduced the severity of the sudden conflict between the two countries. The authorities indicated that the process of expelling Hungarian僑민 would continue, but a more moderate policy would be adopted. It is rumored that the Hungarian army authorities have decided that if the Yugoslav army implements its policies, they would rather abandon the town of 四格特, because the area offers little defensibility. Last night, the Hungarian capital authorities denied reports that reinforcements had been sent to the border.

Yesterday, the Council of the League of Nations in Geneva reopened to discuss Yugoslavia's memorandum to Hungary for the bloodshed of Marseille. The representatives, especially British Lord Privy Seal Eden, tried hard not to involve politics, but to discuss purely from a legal point of view. This effort clearly did not have any effect, because French Foreign Minister Laval announced with eloquent words that France supported Yugoslavia on all counts raised in the Marseille bloodshed case, while Italian representative Aloisi spoke in defense of Hungary. However, both politicians agreed to propose to the Council of the League of Nations to take international action to deal with terrorism. Laval announced France's support for Yugoslavia, saying, "France stands on the side of Yugoslavia on this serious matter. Those who shot King Alexander were trying to destroy peace. They were trying to destroy King Alexander's work. It is up to us, the Council of the League of Nations, to ensure that peace is not endangered." Britain's view was that the whole case was judicial in nature, and that the League of Nations should consider Yugoslavia's memorandum as a court. Russian representative Litvinov also gave a brief speech, denouncing terrorism. British representative Eden strongly urged the representatives to separate facts from will and policy. Eden said that the responsibility for the Marseille bloodshed case is difficult to determine at this time, because those allegedly responsible have not yet been tried. The current discussion should therefore continue to the next meeting of the Executive Yuan at 10:30 AM on Monday, and the Executive Yuan announced that it would adjourn until the meeting.

Hungary has sent a memorandum to the League of Nations regarding the assassination of King Alexander of Yugoslavia, denying that the Hungarian government or Hungarian authorities lacked enthusiasm in controlling Yugoslavian fugitives, and defending that the Hungarian authorities had issued passports to a Yugoslavian terrorist party. It further stated that anyone who illegally crossed the border would be handed over to civil and military authorities for trial in accordance with the regulations for preventing espionage in various countries.

The Yugoslavian Minister to Geneva commented on yesterday's meeting of the Council of the League of Nations, saying, "Can we expect our people to be satisfied if you consider the resolution with a magnifying glass, hoping to find the guilt of the mastermind who murdered our monarch?" His meaning was that he felt the Council of the League of Nations' attitude towards Hungary was too lenient. From the current situation, it seems that the Council of the League of Nations will, on the one hand, pass a resolution condemning the Marseille bloodshed case, and, on the other hand, conclude an international convention stipulating the treatment of political fugitives.

The Paris newspapers commented on yesterday's declaration by Czech Foreign Minister Beneš that the Little Entente countries were prepared to defend their territorial integrity with war, also believing that the activities of those advocating revision of the peace treaty had endangered the peace of Europe. One newspaper said that in the event of war, even the League of Nations would not be able to maintain peace. Another newspaper said that Beneš's declaration was timely and would deal a fatal blow to those advocating revision of the treaty (8th Reuters dispatch).

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull solemnly announced today that the United States will take a bystander attitude towards the dispute between Yugoslavia and Hungary (8th dispatch from the National News Agency).

Speeches by Various National Representatives

(Geneva) The Council of the League of Nations continued its meeting at 3:00 PM today to discuss the issue of political responsibility for the Marseille assassination, as requested by Yugoslavia. Representatives from France, Italy, Russia, Britain, and Spain all made important speeches. The Council then adjourned the meeting until Monday to continue the discussion. The following is a summary of the speeches of the representatives of major powers:

French Foreign Minister Laval spoke on behalf of the French government, saying that France and Yugoslavia shared the same fate in the Marseille bloodshed case. The French Foreign Minister and the Yugoslavian King were assassinated at the same time. Alexander I was the founder of Yugoslavian unity. The thugs wanted him to die, and their intention was to destroy peace. Now that the Yugoslavian King has passed away, his peace cause must continue to exist and must be protected. Recently, when discussing the Saar issue, the Council expressed that it could use material force to prevent order from being disturbed. Now, for this case, the League of Nations has the same responsibility. Acts that violate the law should not be used as political tools. Therefore, I advocate that the Council should take action and jointly discuss and agree on international sanctions before it can be said to be complete.

Italian representative Baron Aloisi spoke after Laval, first praising the achievements of Yugoslavian King Alexander and French Foreign Minister Barthou, and then quoting Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, inviting Italy to participate in the Geneva debate with the desire for cooperation and peace. At this critical moment, the International Union should assume the task of疏解. Now, before us, someone is severely reprimanding a country, and even hurting its national honor. Hungary's rebuttal of this kind of 伸訴 is out of 公道, and its request that the Council immediately handle this case and clarify the truth is Hungary's due right and obligation. As for the revision of the treaty mentioned by Hungarian representative Eckhart, its nature is peaceful and completely different from terrorism. The Council has already recorded this declaration, which is enough. Italy initially advocated that the treaty should be suitable for the new needs of the times, because only in this way can the peace be guaranteed. However, the revision of the treaty to suit the new needs must be done in a legal way. Italy will also consider the issue of taking international action to suppress terrorism proposed by the French Foreign Minister.

Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov spoke from the 壇, saying that he should reserve his opinion on the facts of this case, but he believed that Yugoslavia and France had the right to 伸訴 to the Council and request judgment. Litvinov then recounted his brief history of terrorism, saying that since the war, terrorism has emerged in layers. This kind of terrorist action is mostly reactionary in nature, and often prepared in foreign territories, and some of them are aimed at provoking conflicts between the two countries. No country should allow the existence of such actions. We hate individual terrorism even more. As for the Marseille bloodshed case, which is enough to endanger international peace, the League of Nations has the responsibility to maintain peace and should handle it well. In short, international unity is obviously necessary for this kind of problem.

Then British Lord Privy Seal Eden spoke, first mourning the national funeral of Yugoslavia, saying that it was unfortunate that these facts could now be calmly and calmly discussed on the议坛. The accomplices in this case are still in prison, and the investigation has not yet been completed, so it is extremely difficult to express an opinion at present. Eden then made a general statement on Yugoslavia's proposed prevention of terrorism, saying that the British people attach great importance to the right of asylum that political prisoners should enjoy, but freedom and indulgence should not be confused. The British government will never allow the preparation of violent actions that endanger the authorities of other countries within its borders. The most important thing at present is to ease the air, to prevent international hatred from continuing to grow, and to do our best to assist the Council to limit the scope of the problem and prevent it from expanding.

Then the Polish representative also rose to speak, saying that Poland, located between Hungary and Yugoslavia, two friendly countries, should maintain an impartial attitude. If the League of Nations stipulates a mutual assistance system for countries to prohibit such crimes, Poland is also prepared to cooperate.

Finally, Spanish representative Madariaga spoke, first praising the calm attitude of Yugoslavia, France, and Hungary, saying that the establishment of the Council of the League of Nations is not only to uphold justice, but also, and more importantly, to take action. The Council should now remain calm and wait for the arrival of a time when all parties can compromise. In addition, various remedial measures should be taken, such as banning the arms trade. There were also speeches by representatives of other countries, praising the Yugoslavian King and French Foreign Minister Barthou, which will not be recorded in detail (9th dispatch from Havas).

French Foreign Minister Seeks Compromise

(Geneva) The Council of the League of Nations has been discussing the dispute between Yugoslavia and Hungary over the Marseille assassination for days, but has not yet reached a decision. This issue is closely related to the peace of Europe, so French Foreign Minister Laval will spend all his time looking for a way to establish a resolution. This resolution must satisfy Yugoslavia, must not violate the will of other countries, and must obtain the unanimous approval of all countries attending the Council, including Hungary. Laval has consulted with the Greek representative and will hold talks with Italian representative Aloisi, British representative Eden, or other national representatives this afternoon. In addition, Laval met with Yugoslavian Foreign Minister Jevtić this morning, and Jevtić informed Laval of the maximum extent of the concessions made by Yugoslavia and its allies. The meeting of the Council on Saturday and Sunday created a situation that was not conducive to a friendly resolution of this issue. As a result, all parties related to Geneva and the capitals of the Little Entente and the Balkan League were greatly disappointed. The problem is that procedural issues have made the resolution of this problem even more complicated. According to Article 11 of the Covenant of the League of Nations, this problem is applicable to reconciliation procedures, and all resolutions must be passed unanimously. Yugoslavia and Hungary, the two parties involved, have equal voting rights with other countries attending the Council, so it is even more difficult to establish a resolution (9th dispatch from Havas).

British, Italian, Dutch, and Swiss Police Sent to Maintain Security in the Saar

Decision of the Council of the League of Nations

(Geneva) The Council of the League of Nations today passed a resolution inviting Britain, Italy, the Netherlands, and Sweden to jointly dispatch personnel to form an international police force to maintain security in the Saar during the plebiscite in mid-January next year (8th dispatch from the National News Agency).

(Geneva) The issue of international police entering the Saar to maintain security was discussed at the Council of the League of Nations meeting this afternoon. Baron Aloisi presented a report that all countries willing to join the international police force and Germany have already agreed, and the German government has officially replied in writing to the Tripartite Committee expressing its agreement, so the Tripartite Committee asked the General Assembly to pay attention to this point, and all necessary procedures were completed by Czech Foreign Minister Beneš who formally moved to pass, and it was resolved to appoint an international committee to facilitate the process (8th dispatch from the National News Agency).

(London) The Dutch government has accepted the invitation of the League of Nations to dispatch a team to participate in the international police force to maintain order during the Saar plebiscite, but a Reuters interviewer stationed in the Dutch capital asked the authorities whether the Netherlands would dispatch troops, and the authorities denied this, saying that such official consultations have not yet begun. The French government declared today that all international police officers going to the Saar to take responsibility for maintaining order would be exempt from transportation costs when passing through French territory (8th Reuters dispatch).

We now believe that Franco-German reconciliation is indeed possible. The visit of French veterans of the European War, their speeches, and the replies of veterans of other countries are all enough to prove our slogan of peace. Italy and Abyssinia Trade Accusations Over Responsibility for Conflict

Italian Bombers Quell Riots

It is said that when the British official and the commission arrived at维鲁亚鲁亚, they encountered 800 troops under the command of an Italian officer. The Italian officer refused to allow the Asopini Commission to set up tents on the Abyssinian border and summoned tanks, aircraft, and troops from Italian territory to prevent the commission from carrying out its work. Although the British official mediated, it had no effect, and the situation deteriorated, leading to conflict. According to the British government's report, it is confirmed that the personnel dispatched by British Somaliland were indeed frightened, but the British envoy stationed in Abyssinia did not mention the details. The Asopini Commission was ordered to discuss the rights of the indigenous pastures, and from time to time passed through the border, and has nothing to do with the dispute over the territory between Italy and Abyssinia. When the conflict between Italy and Abyssinia occurred, more than 60 Italians were killed and 400 were injured. It is believed that the Abyssinian casualties must be heavy. Singapore Police Investigate Japanese Espionage Case

Two Japanese Nationals Arrive from Europe with Suspicious Behavior

Nishihara Dies Suddenly While Searching for a Mysterious Leather Bag

London Sources Claim Involvement of Naval Personnel

Singapore - Singapore police authorities are currently investigating the activities of several Japanese nationals. This matter has caused alarm among the public. In recent days, the political intelligence unit of the local police station has been extremely busy, drawing close public attention. Although the authorities are being tight-lipped, it is widely believed to be related to espionage. Initially, it was suddenly reported last Thursday that Nishihara, the president of the Japanese Association of Singapore, died at the special branch office of the police station. Nishihara was summoned to the station for questioning about the whereabouts of a peculiar leather bag brought by a certain Japanese national who arrived in Singapore earlier in the week. Two minutes after Nishihara arrived at the station, he collapsed and died. An autopsy is currently underway, but the results are unknown. The full details of this case are currently unavailable. However, it is widely believed that the matter originated with two Japanese nationals who came here from Europe. One did not have a passport and claimed it was with Nishihara. It was later confirmed that it was indeed with Nishihara, but before the departure of the mail ship, a leather bag belonging to the Japanese national went missing, arousing the suspicion of the police. An investigation ensued. After the two individuals re-boarded the mail ship, Nishihara was summoned to the special branch office of the police station for further questioning. The following day, two other Japanese nationals, one a sculptor and the other the deputy editor of a Japanese newspaper in Singapore, were issued deportation orders by the authorities and placed under detention. This further alarmed the public. While the police station did not refuse to release all information, they thoroughly searched Japanese hotels and residences yesterday, interrogating many Japanese residents, but did not arrest anyone. It is reported that searches will continue at various places where Japanese residents live. The police station has not yet announced the date when the two detained Japanese nationals will be deported. It is widely believed that they will leave soon. As for Nishihara's sudden death, it will likely be thoroughly investigated within the next four days. The local Japanese residents have expressed great regret over the detention of the two nationals by the authorities. However, since the authorities have not provided a clear explanation for this action, the Japanese residents claim that they know nothing about the matter. (Reuters, 9th)

(London) The Singapore police are handling the activities of Japanese residents there with strict secrecy, leading to much speculation among people in London. According to reliable sources, the activities of some Japanese residents are related to espionage. It is said that some of them are naval personnel. After being interrogated by the police, they hastily returned to Japan. It is expected that some other Japanese nationals will be deported, as there is insufficient evidence to prosecute them. Some also claim that the British naval exercises to be held in Singapore will be conducted in secret due to these developments. However, this claim is not acknowledged by London political circles. (Reuters, 9th)

US Expands Air Force

Army Adds Fifty Pursuit Planes

US Still Responsible for Philippine Defense

Philippine Assembly's Defense Bill Returned by Governor-General

(Manila) Philippine Governor-General Murphy today returned the Philippine defense bill to the assembly for reconsideration, which is tantamount to the governor-general exercising his veto power. The accompanying note stated that the defense issue is not currently urgent, as the United States remains responsible for protecting the Philippines until the islands gain full independence. The issue of defense will be studied at leisure. However, the governor-general has already signed off on the expansion of the police force and the establishment of an air defense plan. (National Telegram, 9th)

(Manila) A US Senate investigative team, studying various economic issues and the future commercial relations between the Philippines and the United States, led by Senator Tydings, chairman of the Senate Territorial Committee, arrived in the Philippines today. Business and political leaders will try to make them understand that the economic provisions of the Philippine independence bill urgently need to be amended. This is because the bill limits the tax-free import of Philippine sugar, coconut oil, and rope into the United States, and stipulates that a progressive export tax will be levied five years after independence. Leaders from all sectors have stated that this progressive tax must be removed. As for the coconut oil tax, although it is particularly reduced for Philippine products, only five cents per pound, it is still widely criticized. Philippine leaders hope that there will be some guarantees for future US-Philippine trade. The business community supports the establishment of reciprocal relations after independence, as the United States is currently the most important market for Philippine products, and almost all sugar production is shipped to the United States. Senator Hayden came here earlier to conduct a preliminary investigation. He stated that Congress has already approved the principle of reciprocal treaties to maintain existing commercial relations, as US-Philippine trade is very beneficial to the Philippines. Political and business circles here are also aware of this and have suggested a bill to protect American products. This proposal has been endorsed by Philippine Governor-General Murphy and Senate President Quezon. However, Washington has stated that it is not appropriate to take any action because the reciprocal policy is still in its infancy. Therefore, the Tax Code Drafting Committee of the last legislature only drafted a bill to protect Philippine products and increase revenue, and did not pass the bill before the legislature adjourned on November 8. The legislature will hold a special session early next year, and the bill may be introduced at that time. (National Telegram, 9th)

British-Australian Scheduled Air Service

The scheduled weekly flight between Le Bourget (France), London, and Australia began today. A British four-engine aircraft flew out of London at 1:05 PM and arrived here at 3:30 PM. It will depart tomorrow for Singapore via Naples, Italy. The King and Queen have sent a letter to their third son, the Duke of Gloucester, which will be delivered by airmail. (Havas, 8th)

Japanese Diet Concludes Hasty Session

Dozens of Bills Passed in Fifteen Minutes

(Tokyo) Today's plenary session of the House of Representatives was like a whirlwind after a storm. Few members were present. The meeting opened at 11:15 AM, and 26 proposals and 25 petitions were collectively submitted and unanimously passed. Speaker Akita gave a speech and adjourned the meeting at 11:30 AM. (Dentsu, 9th)

(Tokyo) The following bills submitted by the government to the extraordinary session have been passed: (1) Amendment to the City Planning Law; (2) Law on Deferment of Tax Reductions for Victims of Wind and Flood Disasters; (3) Law on Temporary Transfer of Government-Owned Uncultivated Land; (4) Amendment to Law No. 5 of Showa 9; Budget Bills: (5) Supplementary General Budget for Revenues and Expenditures for the Ninth Fiscal Year; (6) Supplementary Budget for Special Account Expenditures for the Ninth Fiscal Year. The above bills will be deliberated at the regular cabinet meeting on the 11th and promulgated on the same day. (Dentsu, 9th)

(Tokyo) The House of Peers meeting of the 66th Extraordinary Session opened at 10:15 AM on the morning of the 9th to deliberate on the disaster relief budget. Prime Minister Okada and all other cabinet members attended, and almost all the seats for members were occupied. Chairman Yanagisawa of the Budget Committee first reported on the process and results of the committee, and then questioning began. First, Sakatani Yoshio took the floor and said that the problem of reforming the institutions stationed in Manchuria should be addressed reasonably in light of past actual circumstances. However, Japan and "Manchukuo" should avoid disputes over the South Manchuria Railway (SMR) in the future. It has always been stipulated that no one except China and Japan is allowed to own SMR shares. Japan and Manchukuo have the same interests. In the future, "Manchukuo" should be allowed to own SMR shares. Is the government paying attention to this point?

Prime Minister Okada replied that the government is currently considering the issue of "Manchukuo" owning SMR shares in the SMR Ordinance and it is open to consideration. Sakatani urged the government to implement the revision of the ordinance as soon as possible. Then, after beginning the discussion, Maeda Toshisada criticized the government for convening the extraordinary session too late, saying that the civil engineering expenses in the disaster budget are extremely small. He hoped that the government would study more thorough disaster relief measures in the future. Although the contents of this budget are not satisfactory, he supported its passage through the Diet because of the urgency of the relief effort.

As a result of the Speaker's vote, it passed, and the government's disaster budget was completely established. The meeting adjourned at 11:50 AM. (Japan United Press, 9th)

(Tokyo) The extraordinary session of the Diet convened for the first time by the Okada cabinet has concluded. Although its purpose was to deliberate on the disaster budget, each political party concentrated its attack on the government's rigorous criticism of the implementation of the budget. The government authorities tried their best to defend it, extending the session and passing the disaster budget of 210 million yen, deciding on the exemption of taxes for disaster victims, the government's temporary transfer of rice plan, and reforming important issues such as the institutions stationed in Manchuria. Although the Diet session was not long, the importance of its passage of each bill is quite remarkable. (Japan United Press, 9th)

(Tokyo) The House of Representatives experienced repeated turbulence and extended the session twice, passing the government budget bill and delivering it to the House of Peers. On the 8th, the House of Peers committee decided to pass it to the formal meeting on the 9th. The government's deficit bond bill, the law on temporary transfer of government-owned rice to disaster areas, the amendment to the city planning law, and the four proposals to exempt victims of wind and flood disasters from taxes have been passed by both houses. If the budget bill on the 9th can be successfully passed, then the extraordinary session can be concluded. The government side considered that the Okada cabinet's first Diet session was dangerous because its answers were inconsistent. However, it was successful in extending the session and passing all the proposals peacefully. However, the Seiyukai, which advocated the revival of party politics and the return of constitutional politics, teamed up with the Minseito, but unexpectedly submitted a bombshell motion in the Diet. It was unable to maintain it and succumbed to the weak cabinet, exposing its weakness. Not only did its first step in reviving party politics completely fail, but also the credibility and power of the party fell to the ground, which is truly regrettable for parliamentary politics. (Japan United Press, 9th)

US Also Implements Drug Prohibition

Eight Overseas Chinese Arrested

(Washington) The government's campaign to eradicate thugs and gangsters has achieved another success. Treasury Department secret agents were ordered to arrest drug traffickers, and simultaneous actions were taken nationwide. More than 500 people have been arrested, and countless drugs have been seized. The government is determined to eradicate organized gangs and believes that to achieve this goal, drug trafficking must be eliminated first. During the arrests in Baltimore, Treasury Secretary Morgenthau personally directed the operation, demonstrating the government's seriousness. After the arrests, Mr. Anslinger, head of the Treasury Department's Bureau of Narcotics, conducted detailed inquiries. Mr. Anslinger said, "The results of the inquiries are very satisfactory. Even if this arrest does not completely eradicate drug traffickers, it will at least make the leaders in this business think deeply." Among the arrested drug traffickers were eight overseas Chinese, allegedly seized for opium. It is estimated that the final number of arrests will reach 1,000. It is also worth noting that the National Crime Conference will soon be held in Washington. At that time, federal and state agents will design the best way to jointly eradicate thugs and gangsters, and this large-scale arrest of drug offenders took place just before the conference. (National Telegram, 8th)

Bolivia Mobilizes Nationally

Preparing for a Decisive Battle with Paraguayan Forces

La Paz - The Bolivian cabinet has ordered a national mobilization to prevent the complete defeat of the army. The mobilization will be implemented on Sunday or Monday. This mobilization includes all reservists and is the most widespread mobilization order since the outbreak of war one and a half years ago. The cabinet is now determined to repel the Paraguayan army and has been working closely with military leaders to ensure that the front-line troops have the full support of the nation. (National Telegram, 8th)

According to official reports from Asuncion, the capital of Argentina, the right wing of the Paraguayan army launched a surprise attack, and seven divisions of the Bolivian army have been completely disintegrated. General Estigarribia also stated that after several days of bloody fighting, his troops have occupied Villa Montes, the gateway to the Bermejo oil region, and the forts of Picuiba, Longvesta, and Irondha have also fallen. (National Telegram, 8th)

Pacific Defense and Naval Arms Race

Japanese Newspaper Discusses Trends After Failure of Naval Conference

The Tokyo Kokumin Shimbun reported on the 2nd that the failure of the London Naval Conference and Japan's abandonment of the Washington Treaty are already established facts. Britain and the United States blamed Japan for the failure, and the United States insisted on a 5:5:3 ratio, threatening to compete in shipbuilding. The following is an analysis of the impact of expanded defense preparations in the Pacific after the breakdown of the conference. The Washington Treaty stipulated: (1) islands in the Pacific currently held by the United States and those to be acquired in the future (excluding islands near Alaska and the Panama Canal Zone, and the Hawaiian Islands); (2) territories in the Pacific east of 110 degrees east longitude currently held by Britain and those to be acquired in the future (excluding islands near Canada, the Commonwealth of Australia, and New Zealand); (3) island territories and dependencies in the Pacific of Japan (i.e., the Kuril Islands, Ogasawara Islands, Amami Ōshima, Ryukyu Islands, Taiwan, Penghu Islands, and islands territories and dependencies that Japan may acquire in the Pacific in the future (stipulating that the status quo of defense facilities be maintained). However, these defense restrictions are actually centered on Japan and are limited to the defense of the Western Pacific, not involving the Eastern or Southern Pacific. After the treaty is abandoned, the defense restrictions will naturally be lifted. At that time, there will be opportunities to attack Japan, reducing Japan's defensive capabilities. On the other hand, Japan can also prepare for defense far from the islands. This is why Japan had no choice but to abandon the treaty. However, once the treaty is abandoned, what follows is an arms race. In other words, during the treaty's validity period, it should be strictly observed until the end of 1936. After the treaty is abandoned, each country can build ships at will. However, with today's industrial capacity, it takes four years for a battleship, three years for a 10,000-ton cruiser, and less than a year for a destroyer, regardless of the country. However, even if countries want to compete in shipbuilding, their national strength is limited, and it remains questionable whether they can actually do so. For example, the United States has been experiencing a severe domestic panic since 1929. The total income of the American people was 85 billion yuan before the war, but today it is only 35 billion yuan. The national debt of the central government and the states totals 48 billion yuan, and overseas investments amount to 30 billion yuan. Now, if the United States wants to establish the world's leading navy, all of its expenses are paid from civil engineering funds in the name of unemployment relief, so the deficit public debt is increasing, and the fiscal situation is becoming tight. Therefore, the US Congress cannot achieve the goal of becoming the world's leading naval power in accordance with the domestic situation with the ship-building expenses that are agreed upon. The same is true for the UK. In addition, the training of naval officers requires at least ten years per person, non-commissioned officers require six years, and other aviation soldiers require more than five years of training. However, the US and UK have always adopted a mercenary system and a voluntary military system. The United States has not yet reformed its military system, so it feels a particular lack of personnel. Judging from the current situation of shipbuilding in various countries, if the existing treaty continues until after 1936, the United States will have an aircraft carrier of 30,000 tons, a cruiser of 60,000 tons, a destroyer of 70,000 tons, and a submarine of more than 20,000 tons, totaling more than 190,000 tons, which is still less than the treaty's limit of more than 520,000 tons. Now, to supplement the construction, the annual construction volume must be 80,000 tons. By the end of 1936, the UK would still be less than 100,000 tons of the treaty amount. Such a large shipbuilding plan is unlikely to be implemented. Moreover, if the United States implements a three-year plan and a five-year plan for shipbuilding today, it would have to build two new ships every month until the end of 1939, for a total of 139 ships, which would be even more difficult. In summary, the so-called arms race is just speculative talk and is still extremely difficult in reality.

Saar Impressions

(National News Agency German Correspondent) Qiao Qisen, a graduate of the University of Berlin, traveled to the Saar and gained many impressions. He has returned to Germany and made the following remarks to reporters. This winter, the most difficult political problem in Europe to solve is the Saar problem. By January 13 next year, the people of the Saar must vote to decide whether to belong to Germany, France, or remain in the status quo. This is an event that all European countries are paying attention to. In all fairness, the Saar should originally belong to Germany. Not only is the language of the residents the same as German, but also the culture and life are no different. Therefore, the people of the Saar all want to return to Germany. The public opinion of the Saar is inclined to Germany, and there should be no other problems. But doesn't the fact that the Saar problem arises is because it is caused by European politics?

From this point of view, it is clear that the people of the Saar are inclined to Germany and all want to be Hitler's comrades. This is enough to prove that Hitler's policy of friendship and peace abroad is different from the hypocritical high-pressure tactics of other countries. During my trip to the Saar, it was the day when the new German government was just established, the national flag was restored, and Hitler's election was won. When I arrived in Saarbrucken and Saar Louis, I saw many National Socialist flags and black, white, and red German national flags hanging in those two places. According to what I heard, only French agencies in the Saar hang the black, white, and blue French flag. The people of the Saar hang the German flag as a symbol of the residents' sympathy for Hitler. This kind of sympathy will probably not be lost until the vote next year. Within a country, the current government of that country did not encourage the people to hang the flag of a certain country, but the people automatically hang the German flag. This is enough to show the future will of the people of that country, which no one can stop. Those who are good at observing things should value the will of the people. Today, the people of the Saar all want to be Hitler's comrades. This truly shows the people there have a fanatical infatuation, which is even more intense than that of the people in Berlin. Berlin also hangs party flags and national flags every Friday under the same circumstances.

During this trip, I first met a Saar woman at Mainz Station. At that time, I was waiting for a train at the station. The woman was very simple. She took a step towards a German woman and came to the platform to ask me, "Are you also going to Saarbrucken?" I gladly agreed, so this Saar woman generously told me about the situation in the Saar, because her son was studying at Mainz School and this trip was to take her son home. I gained another political understanding from this. She said, "I am originally the mother of a German child, so I don't want my children to study in France. The people of the Saar all want to belong to Germany. I am a farmer's wife, and especially we farmers are more inclined to Germany. We always want to abandon our homes and go to our German homeland, because we have no country in our home, as if we are stateless. We are German migrants. The living standards in the Saar are even higher than in Germany. We know very well that if we return to our homeland, the economic situation will be even more difficult, but we are not afraid to sacrifice for the country. As for the farmers in Rottlin, their situation is even worse, several times worse than ours, and they can only make ends meet, but they have been lacking clothes for a long time. When we go out and look at people, we see the French people's gorgeous clothes and the German people's clean and simple clothes."

When the train arrived in the Saar, I said goodbye to this Saar farmer and thanked her for telling me about the situation in the Saar. The border between Germany and the Saar is the Namborn station. After the end of the European War and the signing of the treaty, the Saar belonged to the French customs zone, so France set up a customs inspection office there. After I waited for the customs inspection to be released, I went to the station to buy food, but the French tax officer called to me in French, "Please don't go, wait on the train." I deliberately replied in German, "I'm going to buy food," and wanted to see if German could not be used in Germany.

Saarbrucken is the capital of the Saar, and I looked up and saw many bright and dazzling German flags.

After I passed the customs, I immediately paid attention to French shoes. I went to four shoe stores to inquire, but all I saw were German shoes, and the prices were higher than in Berlin. I was very surprised at the time, how could there be no French shoes for sale in the French territory, and the import tariff on French goods is free, and the price should be cheaper than German. While I was hesitating, the female shop assistant explained to me that although French shoes are cheap, the people of the Saar do not want to buy them. When asked why, she replied that German shoes are national shame souvenirs and are made by our compatriots, so the workmanship and materials must be more refined. From this, it can be inferred that German goods still dominate the Saar market.

Secondly, I saw the people of the Saar coming and going on the street, all with a very special German style.

On the street, I saw many newspaper sellers and asked which newspaper was the most popular. One of the female newspaper sellers replied, "The Saarbrücken People's Newspaper and the Evening News" are the most popular. These two newspapers have large characters printed at the top of the newspaper, titled "Organ of the German Vanguard." The German Vanguard has a non-partisan stance and is purely dedicated to the construction of national society, leading the way in saving modern Germany. As for the Evening News, it also has a clear slogan on the front page, "For Germany, Resist the Enemies of Germany." These phrases are no different from what people in Germany are saying today. - So I continued to ask, "Do you have any French newspapers?" The female newspaper seller replied, "This goes without saying." At this point, I said goodbye. After this, wherever I went in the Saar, I discovered that the nature and character of the people of the Saar were exactly the same as those of Germany, and the people of the Saar had no other wish but to hope to be reunited with Germany.

Nobel Prize

Stockholm, Sweden - This year's Nobel Prize certificates will be awarded by the King of Sweden in person on December 10, the anniversary of the death of Nobel Prize donor Alfred Nobel. Italian playwright Luigi Pirandello, who won this year's Nobel Prize in Literature, and the four Americans who won the Nobel Prize in Medicine and Physiology, George Whipple, George Richards Minot and William Parry Murphy, will come to receive the award in person. However, American chemist Harold Urey, who won the Nobel Prize in Chemistry, will not be able to attend. In addition, this year's Nobel Prize in Physics has been decided to be suspended. The amount of each prize is approximately 162,607 Swedish kronor. (Havas, 9th)

Oslo, Norway - Reports say that this year's Nobel Peace Prize will be awarded to Henderson, chairman of the Disarmament Conference. The official announcement will be made around Sunday. (Havas, 8th)

Official Telegram

The Central Antiquities Preservation Committee Sends a Telegram to All Central Ministries and Councils, the Peiping Military and Political Branch Council, All Provincial and Municipal Governments, All Pacification Commissioners, All Universities, and All Academic Organizations: Since recent years, the government's organizations for preserving national antiquities have not been unified, leading to the erosion and collapse of steles and buildings, the outflow of bronze vessels, books, and documents overseas, free excavation, and unscrupulous merchants cleverly seizing profits and destroying national treasures, which is extremely distressing. For the sake of unified preservation, the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee has been established, and Li Ji, Ye Gongchuo, Huang Wenbi, Fu Sinian, Zhu Xizu, Jiang Fuchong, Dong Zuobin, Teng Gu, Shu Chushi, Fu Rulin, Lu Xirong, Ma Heng, Xu Bingchang, etc., have been appointed as committee members by the Executive Yuan, and Fu Rulin, Teng Gu, Li Ji, Ye Gongchuo, and Jiang Fuchong have been designated as standing committee members, with Fu Rulin as chairman. The inaugural meeting was held at the Executive Yuan on July 12th of this year. Subsequently, a copper seal was issued by the National Government, inscribed with "Seal of the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee," and a small copper stamp, inscribed with "Central Antiquities Preservation Committee," was put into use immediately. The rear courtyard of the Ministry of Interior was selected as the committee's address and reported accordingly. It is noted that this committee, in accordance with the provisions of the Central Antiquities Preservation Law, is the legally competent authority for the preservation of historical sites and antiquities throughout the country. Hereafter, all matters concerning the preservation of historical sites and antiquities throughout the country shall be carried out by this committee in accordance with the Antiquities Preservation Law and its implementing regulations, item by item. The main points are summarized as follows: (1) To supervise and improve the completeness and improvement of the preservation methods of legally established preservation organizations; (2) To cooperate with local governments to protect and repair historical sites and antiquities not yet under government preservation; (3) To approve or reject applications for excavation from academic institutions and provide appropriate assistance and supervision; (4) To severely punish private excavations by unscrupulous merchants and local ruffians; (5) To protect antiquities in private collections by conducting detailed investigations and registrations of important items; (6) To determine the preservation organization for newly discovered antiquities in various localities after the committee assesses their value; (7) To hold local governments responsible for the protection of local historical sites and antiquities; (8) For antiquities related to academic culture, to allocate them to central cultural and academic institutions for research; (9) To register and properly plan preservation methods for other discovered antiquities and historical sites; (10) To strictly supervise the excavation of undiscovered antiquities. The above ten points are the outline of this committee's work. However, the preservation of antiquities is of utmost importance and is closely related to research in history and academics and improvements in art and industry. All members of this committee will work diligently, fearing that they may not be up to the task. It is hoped that all ministries and councils, provincial and municipal governments, military organizations, universities, and public and private academic organizations will thoroughly implement the Antiquities Preservation Law and its implementing regulations promulgated by the central government. If there are those with specialized research on antiquities preservation methods, those who carefully examine antiquities, or those who have definite identification, it is hoped that all will express their great opinions and jointly assist in this grand undertaking, so as to benefit cultural revival, provide a basis for the spirit of history, promote national consciousness, and enhance the beautification of education, so as not to fail the government's intention to specially establish the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee. Now, we specially send one copy each of the Central Antiquities Preservation Law, the Implementing Regulations of the Antiquities Preservation Law, and the Organizational Regulations of the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee for your perusal. Respectfully, Fu Rulin, Chairman of the Standing Committee of the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee; Standing Committee Members Teng Gu, Li Ji, Ye Gongchuo, Jiang Fuchong, bowing in unison.

Italy to Rescue the Bank

The Roman Cabinet Approved a Case Today Stipulating That the Italian People Must Notify the Italian Bank of the Amount of All Investments in Foreign Bonds or Italian Bonds Issued Abroad Before December 31. Failure to Comply with the Order Will Result in a Fine Equal to the Amount of the Unreported Bonds and May Be Sentenced to Imprisonment. All Banks, Bankers, and Businesses Must Submit Foreign Loans to the National Foreign Exchange Administration, Which Will Purchase Them at the Current Exchange Rate. No Official Reason Has Been Published as to Why the Government Passed This Case. However, Domestic and Foreign Banking Circles Are Not Surprised by This. They Said That the Case Is Clearly to Rescue the Recent Losses Suffered by the Italian Bank Because the Bank's Cash Reserve Has Fallen Below the Legal 40% (National Telegram on the 8th).
