Temperature at Seventy Degrees Below Zero

Barthels, India, America, Says One-Eyed Aviator Bushd Completed Second Stratospheric Experiment Here Today, Reaching 50,000 Feet, Measuring Air Temperature There at Seventy Degrees Below Zero Fahrenheit (National Telegram on the 7th).

Full Text of Guo Taiqi's Speech at the 15th Session of the League of Nations General Assembly (Continued from the 8th)

Statement on China's Position on the Northeast Issue

When the League of Nations General Assembly Passed Its Report Eighteen Months Ago, the Lytton Commission of Inquiry Had Already Submitted a Report with the Results of Its Investigation to the General Assembly, Detailing the Tragic Situation Caused by the Japanese Military Invasion, Ending with the Statement, "Manchuria Has Been in Turmoil in the Past Year, and the People of This Vast and Fertile Land Have Experienced a Situation and Suffering Almost Unprecedented." Today's Situation Has Deteriorated Further, as Can Be Proven by Independent and Irreproachable News. On August 23, the London Times Published a Message from Its Shenyang Correspondent Stating, "Since August 6, Bandits Have Attacked an Average of Twice a Day. The Newspapers of 'Manchukuo' Also Publish a Table Today Listing 31 Bridges Destroyed, 31 Train Derailments, and 91 Station Attacks Along the Eastern Section of the Central-Cambodian Railway. According to News Obtained by Foreigners Here, the Danger of Foreigners Being Attacked by Bandits Is Increasing Day by Day When Traveling Outside the Trunk Lines." The Next Day, August 24, the Times Also Published a Maritime Electric Message Stating, "Many Announcements Regarding 'Manchukuo' Are Often Preceded by Statements That Public Security and Order Have Now Been Restored. Such Familiar Words Are Difficult to Believe Based on the Bandit Police News Obtained in a Single Day. On Saturday, Thirty-Six Koreans Residing in a Village Northwest of Shahezi Were Massacred by Bandits Near Beiling in Shenyang, Killing Thirty-Three. On Wednesday, Three Japanese Workers Were Killed by Bandits on the Jitu Railway. On Tuesday, A Train of Armored Vehicles Traveling on the Eastern Section of the Northern Manchuria Railway Was Attacked by Bandits After the Locomotive and Four Train Cars Derailed." The Tragedies Cited Above All Occurred on the Trunk Lines, and the Situation in the Rest of Manchuria Can Be Imagined. Recently, the Residence of the Pseudo-Emperor in the So-Called Capital Was Also Burned Down, and One of the Largest Japanese Airfields Outside the So-Called Capital Was Burned to the Ground for the Second Time in April, with Losses Reaching Millions of Dollars. All of This Is Sufficient to Show That the Scattered War Is Large in Scale and Is Referred to as "Bandits" for the Convenience of Spreading Evil Plans. Of Course, There Are Lawless Elements in Manchuria Who Make a Living as Bandits, but in Terms of Burning Down Palaces and Airfields, Destroying Railways, and Attacking Troops and Troop Trains, It Is Actually a Major Illegal Movement of the Oppressed People Resisting the Army. These People Persist in Their Doctrine and Are Not Discouraged, So They Fight Anytime and Anywhere, and When the Opportunity Arrives, They Will Launch a Final Liberation. The Situation in Manchuria Today Is Roughly the Same as When the September 18 Incident Occurred, That Is, the Japanese Army Is Still Occupying Major Cities and Sending Troops to Punish Residents at All Times to Show Their Might. Under the Occupation of Foreign Troops, There Is a Possibility of Restoring Law and Order and Allowing People to Achieve Prosperity. This Kind of Ideal Has Been Dispelled by Facts and Actually Despises the Lessons of History. The Reaction to the Destruction of Treaties and the Occupation of Our Country's Northeastern Provinces Is Not Limited to the Far East. All European Countries That Care About Their National Borders or National Security Have Been Harmed Because the Countries of the League of Nations and China Are Still Unable to Do Anything, or Have Done Something, but Are Too Cowardly to Support the Decisions Announced by the League of Nations. The Spreading Consequences Are Not Purely Negative. The Soviet Union's Accession to the League of Nations and the Closer Cooperation Between the League of Nations and the United States Can Be Said to Be at Least Partly Due to the Urgency of the Far East Incident. Furthermore, the Far East Is Becoming Increasingly Important in World Affairs and Has Now Received More Vivid and Broader Recognition. It May Be an Overstatement to Say That the Center of Gravity of World Politics Has Shifted from Europe to the Far East, but It Is Indeed a Sad Fact That the Pacific Ocean Is Gradually Becoming the Center of World Affairs. Unfortunately, the Continued Military Occupation of Our Country's Northeastern Provinces Has Become the Most Urgent Danger of the Second World War in Today's World. There Is Absolutely No Doubt About This. The Danger of War in the Far East Is Closely and Inseparably Related to the Future of Peace in Europe, and This Is Also Becoming Increasingly Clear.

The Chinese Representative at the World Economic Conference Once Asked Everyone to Pay Attention to the Potential of the Chinese Market and the Grand Program of National Reconstruction That the Chinese Government Has Implemented Through the Technical Cooperation of the League of Nations. This Program, as You Can See in the Report of the League of Nations Technical Experts, "Includes Various Aspects of National Reconstruction, Such as the Construction of Roads, the Improvement of Silk, Tea, and Cotton, and Cultural Education and Health. Currently, There Are Only a Few League of Nations Experts in China Who Are Specializing in Investigation and Making Technical Designs That Are Completely Unrelated to Political Disputes. The Government Is Currently Carrying Out the Development of Sky and Railway Transportation, and the Strict Movement to Reject Drugs, and Other Reconstruction Undertakings, Although Not Receiving the Technical Cooperation of the League of Nations, Are All Within the Scope of the Overall National Reconstruction Plan. As for What Methods Are Used to Seek the Most Beneficial Results from This Kind of Work, This Is Clearly a Matter of Purely Internal Policy, Which Should Be Decided and Implemented by Sovereign China. Other Countries Have No Reason or Any Right to Interfere in This Kind of Policy. China Is Comforted by the Fact That China's Position on This Matter Has Been Fully Supported by All Countries Concerned with the Policy of East-West Cooperation, as Can Be Proved by the Actions Taken by the Powers After the Tokyo Declaration Was Issued in April. The Chinese Government Is Still Engaged in Struggle to Resist Major Difficulties, and the Work to Be Established Is Also Very Arduous, but We Now Feel That We Have Gained a Foothold and Are Moving Forward in the Right Direction. Given Time, We Will Surely Succeed. If International Peace Can Be Maintained, China's Progress Will Be Solid and Rapid.

I Have Now Strived to Be Concise and, in the Spirit of Plain Realism, Have Stated to You the Prominent Points That the Chinese Government Considers to Be Related to the World Situation, the Far East Issue, and the Purpose of the League of Nations. China Regards Itself as the Vanguard of the League of Nations and the Entire Plan of East-West Cooperation. This Kind of Feeling Has Been Strengthened by the Situation That We Do Not Wish to Have but Makes Us the Main Victim, Because China Has Become the Only Representative of the Far East in the League of Nations Executive Council in the Past Eighteen Months. We Are Willing to Consolidate All Our Chains with the League of Nations in the Technical and Political Scope to Resist the Pressure Exerted by Those Who Will Force Us to Turn Our Backs to the West and Force Us to Join a Purely Unequal Combination in the Name of "Asia for Asians." We Do Not Believe That the World Should Be Divided Into Several Impermeable Parts According to Continents and Races. We Firmly Believe That Peace Can Only Be Maintained Through the League of Nations. The League of Nations Is Universal, and Its Organization Is Not Divided by Major Geographical Regions of the World, So It Can Stand on an Unshakable Position. The Chinese People Have Always Trusted International Justice, Which Is Why, Despite Experiencing All Kinds of Disappointments and Setbacks, Their Loyalty to the League of Nations Has Not Diminished Slightly, and They Are Determined to Exert All Their Powers to Support the League of Nations Covenant and Adhere to the Path of Peace.

I Will Now Make a Conclusion to Strengthen the Power of the League of Nations and Show Future Hopes. China Is the Foundation of Asia. If So, Then Russia Should Be the Arch of the Union of Europe and Asia. China Eagerly Welcomes Russia's Hope to Join the League of Nations Immediately. Russia's Hard Work in the Disarmament Conference Is a Good Sign of the Power It Will Occupy When It Joins the League of Nations. Russia Has Contributed the Most Explicit Definition of Aggressors. China and Russia Have Always Been Neighbors, and the Distance of Their Border Lines Is the Crown of Europe and Asia. We Have a Common Relationship in Maintaining Peace in the Far East and the Pacific Ocean. From Now On, We Are Extremely Happy That Our Joint Efforts to Manage Peace Can Be Carried Out Within the League of Nations Organization. (End)

Military and Political Report Compiled by the Nanchang Headquarters

- Report Submitted to the Fifth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee -

Nanchang Correspondence: The Fifth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee Is About to Open. The Nanchang Headquarters of the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission Has Specially Compiled Reports on the Military, Political, and Facility Measures of the Past Year, Respectively. Regarding the Military Aspect, the First Office Has Compiled a Report on the Military Course of Suppressing Bandits in Jiangxi Province and Submitted It to the Military Affairs Commission, and It Will Be Compiled into a Booklet with Military Reports on Suppressing Bandits in Other Provinces. Regarding the Political Aspect, the Second Office Is Currently Working Hard to Compile It and Will Complete It Within Days and Send It to the Capital by Plane and Submit It to the Fifth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee at That Time. The Items of the Political Report Are Recorded as Follows:

First, General Remarks

Second, Matters Concerning the Local Administrative System (Attached to the Reorganization of Guangze and Wuyuan): A. Promulgation of the Method of Joint Office of the Provincial Government; B. Promotion of the Commissioner System and the Division of Its Responsibilities; C. Promulgation of the Method of Reorganizing the County Government by Abolishing Bureaus and Changing Them into Sections; D. Formulation of the Outline of the Method of Establishing Offices in District Divisions of Each County; E. Establishment of Political Bureaus in Each Special District; F. Reorganization of Guangze and Wuyuan.

Third, Matters Concerning Local Administrative Examination and Inquiry: A. Meeting of Senior Administrative Personnel of Ten Provinces; B. Holding of Security Meeting; C. Organization of Inspection Group.

Fourth, Matters Concerning Civil Affairs: A. Establishment of People's Training Committees in Each Jurisdiction; B. Planning for Flood and Drought Prevention; C. Rectification of Grain Storage in Each Province; D. Harmonization of People's Food in Each Province; E. Establishment of Training Courses.

Fifth, Matters Concerning Finance: A. Examination and Approval of the Budget of Financial Revenue and Expenditure of Each Province; B. Overall Planning of Team Expenses; C. Raising and Allocating Post-War Rehabilitation Expenses.

Sixth, Matters Concerning Education: A. Handling People's Education in Each County in the Bandit Suppression Area; B. Handling People's Education in the Provincial Capital of Jiangxi; C. Handling Special Education in Five Provinces, Jiangxi, Fujian, Anhui, Hubei, and Henan.

Seventh, Matters Concerning Construction: A. Supervising the Construction of Roads in Each Province; B. Pilot Implementation of Immigration and Reclamation; C. Preventing Labor Strikes in Each Province.

Eighth, Matters Concerning Security: A. Improvement of the Security System; B. Unification of Security Organs; C. Compilation of Team Textbooks.

Ninth, Matters Concerning Post-War Rehabilitation in Rural Areas: A. Promoting Rural Cooperation, Establishing Main Organizers, and the Status of Operations in Each Province; B. Relieving Rural Financial Agricultural Loans, Raising Loan Amounts, the Situation of Group Society Lending, and Supplementing Agricultural Tools and Cattle Breeds; C. Handling Rural Land, Establishing Land Handling Training Courses, a Summary of Land Handling, Handling of Rent and Debt Arrears in Recovered County Areas, and Rewarding Officers and Soldiers for Assisting People in Farming; D. Preparing for Rural Revitalization Work.

Tenth, Matters Concerning Justice: A. Promulgation of Regulations on Punishing Local Tyrants and Bad Gentry; B. Promulgation of Methods for Clearing Prisoners; C. Promulgation of Methods for Handling Marriage in Bandit Areas.

Eleventh, Matters Concerning Blocking the Economy of Bandit Areas: A. The Reason for Blocking Bandit Areas; B. The Situation of Handling the Blockade; C. The Effects of the Blockade.

Twelfth, Matters Concerning Prohibition of Opium and Drugs: A. Promulgation of the Method of Strictly Prohibiting Opium; B. Promulgation of Regulations on Strictly Prohibiting Highly Addictive Drugs.

Thirteenth, Matters Concerning the Disposal of Surrendered Prisoners and Scattered Soldiers: A. Disposal of Surrendered Prisoners; B. Reception of Scattered Soldiers; C. Planning for the Establishment of Factories for Disabled Soldiers and Civilians in Each Province.

Fourteenth, Matters Concerning the Collection and Discussion of the Actual Situation of the Bandit Party and Government: A. Research on the Politics of the Red Bandits.

Fifteenth, Matters Concerning the Punishment and Rewards of Civil and Military Officers and Soldiers: A. Punishment and Rewards of Civil and Military Officers and Soldiers; B. Statistical Table of Rewards and Punishments; C. Statistical Table of Pensions and Rewards.

Sixteenth, Matters Concerning the New Life Movement (Central News Agency).

Huang Fu Expresses Willingness to Take on the New Position of Minister of Interior

Huang Fu Cables the Central Government and Will Travel to the Capital Soon

Wartime Zone Cleanup Work to Be Implemented

Peiping Correspondence: Huang Fu, Chairman of the Political Reorganization Committee, Suffered from Anemia in the Middle of Last Month. After Treatment by Chinese and Western Doctors, He Has Now Recovered. Huang Fu Has Agreed to Concurrently Serve as Minister of Interior, but the Time He Will Travel to the Capital Is Still Undecided. Huang Fu's Attitude Toward Concurrently Serving as Minister of Interior and the Current Status of the Political Reorganization Committee's Work Are Described in Detail Below:

The Morning After the Executive Yuan's Decision to Appoint Huang Fu Concurrently as Minister of Interior Reached Peiping, Huang Fu Issued a Written Statement to Visitors in the Evening, Expressing That the North and South Are Remotely Separated and Difficult to Take Care Of Simultaneously, and Said That Northern Political Affairs Are Being Gradually Promoted. On That Day, Huang Fu Received a Telegram from President Wang, In Addition to Asking About Huang Fu's Illness, He Also Told Him That the Central Government Had Great Expectations and Asked Him Not to Humbly Refuse the Position of Minister of Interior and Hoped That He Would Immediately Travel to the Capital to Take Office. Huang Fu Then Replied by Telegram on the Evening of the (7th), First Stating That His Illness Had Recovered, Then Expressing His Gratitude for the Central Government's Favors, and Finally Stating That There Were Hundreds of Matters to Be Dealt With Here in Political Affairs, and Each Part That Had Been Promoted Needed to Be Personally Presided Over. Once Everything Was Sorted Out, He Would Travel to the Capital Soon to Receive Guidance, Etc. Therefore, Although the Date of Huang Fu's Trip South Has Not Yet Been Determined, He Has Agreed to Take on the New Position of Minister of Interior. As for Huang Fu's Illness, After Diagnosis by Chinese and Western Doctors, It Was Considered to Be Anemia. The Left Arm Could Not Be Extended, and the Brain Nerves Also Felt Twinges From Time to Time. After More Than Ten Days of Diagnosis and Treatment, Chinese Medicine Used Moxibustion, and Western Medicine Used Electrical Treatment. Until Today (the 8th), the Left Arm Has Been Able to Extend Freely, and the Headaches Have Also Stopped. Today (the 8th), Huang Fu Went Downstairs to Inspect Various Places and Met with Yu Xuezhong in the Afternoon.

The Most Recent Work of the Political Reorganization Committee Concerning Internal Affairs Is Currently Handling the Examination Matters of the Training Institute for Local Administrative Personnel and the Training Institute for Rural Enterprise Talents, and Classes Can Be Started Soon. Regarding the Wartime Zone Cleanup Issue, the Wartime Zone Cleanup Committee Is Being Ordered to Work Hard to Proceed. The Preparation Procedures of Our Side for the Wartime Zone Cleanup Work Have Been Completed, and the Implementation Steps Will First Be Handled by the Commissioners of the Chan-Yu-Ji-Mi Two Regions Separately, but There Are Many Items and They Need to Be Done Step by Step (the 8th).

Jinan Japanese Pawnshops Are Depressed

- Opening Night Pawnshop to Reduce Interest -

Jinan Correspondence: Since Wang San, Japanese pawnshops have sprung up, Exploiting Heavily, and the Poor Have Had No Choice but to Be Oppressed in Order to Seek Relief. According to Statistics, the Capital of Japanese Pawnshops Has Reached One Million Yuan. The Provincial Government Began to Establish Yulu Pawnshops the Year Before Last, and Now Business Is Extremely Developed. On the 2nd of This Month, Yulu Branch Pawnshops Were Also Established in the Commercial Port, with a Term of 12 Months, an Interest Rate of 2%, and a Storage Fee of 0.5%, So Japanese Pawnshops Have Gradually Been Affected, and They Have Tried to Change Their Previous Methods. Starting Yesterday (the 5th), the Term Will Be Six Months, the Monthly Interest Rate for Those with 20 Yuan Is 5%, the Monthly Interest Rate for Those with Less Than 50 Yuan Is 4%, and the Monthly Interest Rate for Those with More Than 50 Yuan Is 3%. Also, Considering the Psychology of Those Who Pawn Items, Most People Do Not Want to Be Seen by Others, So Night Pawnshops Are Being Planned Again, and Pawning and Redemption Can Also Be Done at Night, Which Can Be Said to Be Good at Speculation.

Qingdao Private Shipping Industry's Appeal Amidst the Sound of Longqing Intermodal Transport

If Intermodal Transport Is Implemented, Freight Transport Will Be Taken Away

Please Ask the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to Plead with the Municipal Government for Relief

Qingdao Correspondence: The Maritime Transportation Between Qingdao and Haizhou, Shijiusuo, and Other Places Has Always Been Carried Out by More Than Ten Private Shipping Companies in This City, Such as Xiaogang Changji Line, Which Navigate Back and Forth and Carry Goods, and Business Is Still Considered to Be Developed. A Total of More Than 30 Small Vessels Navigate the Small Wheel of Haizhou Shijiusuo Xiangshui Kou. In Order to Implement Cooperation, the Industry Has Also Formed a Xiaogang Joint Office to Seek Common Interests. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Is Now Cooperating with the Longhai Railway to Handle Water and Land Intermodal Transport. The Intermodal Transport Route Between Shanghai, Qingdao, and Lianyungang Has Been Added and Officially Started on the 5th of This Month. After This Is Implemented, Almost All the Freight Transport of the Private Shipping Industry in the Xiaogang Area Will Be Taken Away. The Industry Is Greatly Panicked and Specially Convened an Emergency Meeting of Various Private Shipping Companies the Day Before Yesterday. It Was Decided to Submit a Request to the Shipping Association to Quickly Find a Way to Maintain It. The Shipping Association Submitted the Request, Saying That the Matter Is of Great Importance to the Future of Private Shipping and Specially Sent a Letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to Request the Municipal Government for Assistance and Relief. The Original Letter Is Recorded as Follows: "A Request to Plead for a Way to Maintain It in Order to Save the Shipping Merchants from the Emergency. It Is Secretly Based on the Joint Name of More Than Ten Businesses, Such As Changji Line, Tongfuchang, and Yutai Line, Members of Our Association, Who Claim That the Businesses Have Been Operating the Wheelboat Business Between Xiaogang, Qingdao, and Haizhou Along the Coast for Several Years. During This Period, Affected by the World's Economic Depression and Business Recession, Water Power Has Fallen Miserably and Business Has Been Depressed. Therefore, Years of Losses Have Been Hard to Say. This Winter's Freight Transport Has Improved Slightly, and I Am Fortunate to Have the Opportunity to Make Up for It. However, the State-Owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Does Not Care About the Hardships of Private Wheelboats and Has Undertaken the Intermodal Transport of Longqing. I Heard That the Preparations Have Been Completed and Implementation Is Imminent. Its Organizational Scale Is Large, Its Situation Is Superior, and All Expenses Have Been Given Preferential Treatment by the Government. It Is Difficult for Private Wheelboats to Compete with It. In the Future, All Freight Transport Between Haizhou and Xiaogang Will Be Absorbed. Moreover, the Largest Wheelboat in Xiaogang Is Only About 500 Tons, and the Smallest Is Only 50 or 60 Tons. In Addition to Navigating Between Haizhou and Qingdao, There Is No Other Route That Can Be Changed. It Is Different from the Wheelboats That Navigate Between Haizhou and Shanghai. It Has No Competitive Power and Can Only Sit and Wait for Death. The Maritime Administration Once Had an Order to Limit the Addition of Ships on Each Route in Order to Maintain the Shipping Industry, and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Did Not Use All Its Strength to Compete with Foreign Merchants to Recover Lost Interests. It Only Engaged in Destroying the Private Shipping Industry and Was Determined to Put Them to Death and Then Quickly. It Lost the Original Intention of Our Government to Protect the Shipping Industry. It Can Be Seen That More Than 30 Small Wheelboats Are All Placed in Useless Places, and More Than 3,000 Seamen Have Lost Their Way to Make a Living. It Is Also a Plan That Is Abandoned Due to Improper Gains and Losses. In Short, the Intermodal Transport Business Is Convenient for National Economy and People's Livelihood, but the Existing Wheelboats Have Been Serving the Society for a Long Time, and There Are No Achievements to Speak Of. Slight Labor Is Worth Recording. If Intermodal Transport Is Carried Out Suddenly, the Livelihood of the Existing Wheelboats Should Also Be Taken Care Of. We Should Plan for Relief Measures Before We Can Proceed Smoothly and Avoid Involving the Destruction Stage. We Can Either Invest in Buying Up Each Wheelboat, or Lease It at a Reasonable Price, or Allow Them to Join the Intermodal Transport to Serve Together. We Hope That the Public and Private Sectors Will Be Consistent and Maintain Each Other. Otherwise, at the Critical Moment of Survival, It Is Inevitable to Compete to the Death, Resulting in No End. I Think the Government Cannot Bear to See This Situation and Does Not Plan for a Solution for the Businesses' Survival and for the Future of the Private Shipping Industry. I Only Have to Ask Your Association to Quickly Find a Way to Maintain It to Relieve the Difficulties. I Can't Say How Much I Hope So. According to This, the Existing Wheelboats Sailing Between Qingdao and Haizhou Rely on This Line as a Way of Management. In the Past, They Have Served the Society and Have Achieved Some Success. If the Intermodal Transport of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Is Implemented, the Scope Will Be Wide and the Strength Will Be Great. The Business Will Naturally Be Incomparable to the Existing Wheelboats in the Future. If We Do Not Seek Appropriate Relief Measures for the Private Shipping Industry, It Will Be Impossible to Survive, Which Is No Different from Adding to Its Destruction. The Grievances It Holds Are a Definite Fact. In This Autumn of Economic Decline, Regardless of Whether It Is State-Owned or Privately Owned, They Should All Be Maintained Uniformly. The Future of the Country Will Benefit. The Difficulties and Difficulties of the Members Have Been Discussed at the General Assembly, and It Has Been Decided That the Matter Is Related to the Danger of Shipping and We Have to Plead With Your Association to Plead With the Municipal Government to Understand the Situation and Provide Assistance and Relief to Relieve the Difficulties. I Am Grateful for Your Kindness. I Am Respectfully Submitting It to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce," (the 8th).

Suzhou

Discovery of Bandits in Yangcheng Lake

Zhou Weilie, the district chief of the Second Water Police District, and Yin Suichou, the former chief of the Tenth Autonomous District of Wu County, sent an urgent telegram stating that bandits had been discovered in Cheng Lake, intending to cause unrest. Chief Zhou immediately arranged a meeting with the Zhejiang Seventh Water Police Team and ordered all subordinate teams, including the Seventh, Eighth, Fifth, and Special Task Teams, as well as the war junks "Peirong," "Baosu," and "Anjing," to encircle and suppress the lake bandits in nine routes. After starting mobilization on the 7th, the commander of the Seventh Team of the Third Route, Xu Boying, led dozens of water police officers on a motorized sampan, from Zhangyadang Beiku to Sanbaitang. Six bandit boats were spotted, three of which escaped upon hearing the alarm. The remaining three were engaged by Commander Xu and his team, who opened fire and suppressed them, forcing the bandits to flee. As a result, one bandit boat and six bandits, including Wang A'si, Wang A'da, and Chen Guangfu, were captured. They are scheduled to be sent to the Suzhou District Office today (the 9th) for investigation.

Wuxi

Appeal for Exemption of Business Tax for Merchants

The local county chamber of commerce recently received a notice from the Business Tax Bureau to various guilds of rice, beans, miscellaneous grains, and mountain products, instructing all brokers to collect business tax from merchants on their behalf. Since brokers pay license fees and operate by acting as agents for buyers and sellers, they already pay brokerage tax and business tax, which feels like an unnecessary burden. Collecting business tax on behalf of merchants would essentially turn rice shops into a disguised likin station, still taxing goods. This would inevitably deter merchants from coming. Moreover, the Second National Financial Conference this year, in reviewing local financial reforms, generally agreed that commissioned collection and proxy collection were essentially taxes on goods and should be abolished. Brokering in Jiangsu Province, especially in rice and grains, is vital, especially as this year has been marked by famine and food shortages in Jiangnan. Reliable distribution from distant places is essential to alleviate the situation. If rice shops in various regions are required to collect business tax on behalf of merchants, it would be highly inappropriate for the current distribution of food. The central government clearly ordered the localities to abolish likin in the 20th year of the Republic to reduce harassment, which is not in accordance with this order. After consulting with neighboring counties such as Wu County and Wujin, their feedback was consistent. Yesterday, they urgently telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of the Interior, and the Provincial Finance Department, requesting a special exemption to facilitate commerce and benefit the local economy.

Changshu

Interception of Smuggled Rice Boats at Hupu Estuary

Due to severe disasters in the county this summer, rice production has sharply declined, and rice prices have soared since the beginning of winter. The provincial government previously issued a clear order to prohibit the leakage of rice from the mainland. The county government, in conjunction with various agencies, organized a Food Management Committee, headed by Wu Yu, to manage affairs. However, it was repeatedly reported to the government that Fushan was exporting rice for sale to Jiangbei. Because Wu failed in his duties, he was dismissed by the county. A rice merchant from Nantong, Chen Yunsheng, brought an official letter from his county to Changshu to purchase 1,500 dan of japonica rice and requested the county government to issue a passport. The rice was processed on the 7th and loaded onto eleven boats for export at the Hupu estuary. However, the plan was leaked and discovered by the local people, who intercepted and inspected it at the sea mouth. While the passport stated 1,500 dan, the actual amount loaded was over 3,000 dan, a significant discrepancy. The rice boats were therefore detained and placed in the custody of Ren Fei'an of the Hupu Fishermen's Association. The county government was notified by telegram to handle the matter.

Two Steamships Race and One Sinks

Donglai Town in this county is close to Xiyi. Someone there has established the Northeast Steamship Company, operating daily trips between Xiyi and Changshu, which is convenient and prosperous. Seeing that the company is quite profitable, Qian Yuesheng, a merchant in Luyuan, also organized the Datong Steamship Company, running a steamship between Wuxi and Luyuan in this county. This resulted in fierce competition between the two companies. On the 8th of this month, the Northeast Steamship Company's regular steamship was passing near Langan Bridge on its way from Xiyi to Changshu when it suddenly collided with the Hongfei steamship of the Datong Company. The Northeast steamship was holed and flooded, and soon sank. Many passengers also fell into the water. Negotiations between the two parties were ineffective, and a lawsuit has now been filed in the county.

Mother-in-Law and Daughter-in-Law's Conflict Leads to Tragedy in the Middle of the Night

Wu Fulin, of Xishabin, Dongtang City, Third District, has a son named Yongsheng, who married Wang Xiuying from the same village as his wife. They have been married for less than a year, but the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law are at odds and seem irreconcilable. They even engaged in a mutual knife fight, resulting in one death and one injury. This case occurred on the 6th of this month. Due to the distance between the city and the countryside and the lack of telephone communication, it was not until the afternoon of the next day that the case was brought to the city, causing a sensation. Such a murder case between a mother-in-law and a daughter-in-law is truly bizarre and unprecedented. The details are as follows: Xishabin, about three miles from Dongtang City, is inhabited by people all named Wu, hence the name Wu Family Homestead. Wu Fulin, a farmer, lives there with his son Wu A'si and grandson Agou. Fulin is forty years old and has been widowed for nine years. He has a son named Yongsheng, who is now seventeen and helps with the family business. Two years ago, Fulin married Xiuying, the daughter of Wang Zhangquan, from across the river, to his son Yongsheng after being introduced by someone, and the wedding was held in October last year. Unexpectedly, Yongsheng was not fully developed and did not understand romance, so Xiuying often felt that her youth was wasted and was unhappy. Agou, the son of Wu A'si, although from a farming family, was handsome and often tempted Xiuying, taking the opportunity to spread slander about Wang Zhangquan, hoping to alienate Yongsheng and Xiuying and take her for himself. However, due to their uncle-nephew relationship, it never erupted. Since then, Xiuying often returned to her mother's house, neglecting her father-in-law and husband. This summer, Xiuying suddenly fell ill at her husband's house. Yongsheng was inexperienced, so Fulin personally took care of her, bringing her medicine and showing great concern. After Xiuying recovered, Fulin had inappropriate thoughts and even made advances to his daughter-in-law, repeatedly behaving improperly. Xiuying firmly refused and returned to her mother's house for several months. Now that the autumn harvest is in full swing and farming is busy, Fulin plans to bring his daughter-in-law back to help with the work. Unexpectedly, upon returning, the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law quarreled as soon as they met and soon went back to her mother's home. Later, Fulin blamed Wu A'si and his son for instigating his daughter-in-law's departure, leading to another conflict. A'si, in anger, hired a boat to Wang's place that night (the 6th) to bring Xiuying back. Unexpectedly, the tragedy occurred deeper in the night. After Xiuying returned, the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law quarreled more and more fiercely, not stopping until midnight. Later, for some unknown reason, a fight broke out, causing the situation to escalate. Fulin took a kitchen knife and went straight in, slashing his daughter-in-law wildly. Yongsheng saw this and called for help. When neighbors Zhu Xubao and others arrived, they saw the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law lying in a pool of blood. Xiuying's head had been slashed five times, bleeding profusely, and her left hand had three knife wounds, with her index finger falling to the ground. Fulin had cut his throat and was barely alive. They then reported to the woman's father, Wang Zhangquan, and others, who arrived to find the scene extremely tragic. They sent both to the trauma clinic for help, but Fulin had cut his throat and died before dawn, and Xiuying was also in critical condition. After discussion, it was believed that Wu A'si and his son were suspected of instigation. Therefore, Wu Yongsheng and Wang Zhangquan came forward to accuse Wu A'si and Wu Agou of inciting murder and brought them to the county government on the evening of the 7th. After detailed interrogation, they claimed that there was no instigation, implying that Fulin committed suicide by slitting his throat after slashing his daughter-in-law. Both defendants have been detained. The next day, the county sent examiner He Cheng down to the village to investigate.

Nantong

Completion of Baojia System in Six Counties Under District

The Baojia system in the six counties of Tong, Ru, Jing, Chong, Hai, and Qi under the Nantong district has now been completed. After inspection by Jia Zongfu, dispatched by the special commissioner's office, and Sun Yunxia, the general inspector of the Baojia system of the Department of Civil Affairs, the results were deemed satisfactory. Each county is using the Baojia system to investigate and ban opium and drugs and to collect outstanding grain. At the same time, training sessions on the Baojia system for townships and districts are being held to make the general public understand the meaning of the Baojia system.

All Opium Paste Shops Open for Business

All opium paste shops in Tongyi have not yet opened because they need to purchase paste from the Zhenjiang branch, which is very inconvenient. It has now been approved by the provincial authorities that since the Nantong branch has been established, purchases can be made nearby. Therefore, all shops are now open for business.

Haimen

Bandits Attempt to Rob Miaojiao Town but Fail

On the afternoon of the previous day, a group of bandits speaking various dialects suddenly appeared on the streets of Miaojiao Town, Second District of Qidong, intending to rob it. The town's self-defense corps discovered them and immediately dispatched corps members to search and arrest them, capturing eight bandits and seizing items such as box guns, candles, flashlights, and hemp ropes. The remaining bandits fled. Yesterday, the corps sent the bandits and their loot to the county government for interrogation.

Jiashan

Robbery and Injury in Dongjiang Village

Dongjiang Village, about six li from Xitang Town, is a place where bandits often appear. A resident named Jiang Liuguan, whose family is fairly well-off, was suddenly visited on the evening of the 6th by a group of masked bandits wielding knives and sticks who broke into his house, overturning chests and ransacking everything. They also stabbed Jiang Liuguan's son, Linsheng, several times, causing him to bleed profusely and putting his life in danger.

Murder Case in Dayunsi Town

In Fangjiabang, Dayunsi Town, a resident named Zhu Along, who is elderly, has an only son named Axiong, who married a Zhang woman as his wife two years ago. After she married into the family, her husband died. Zhu Zhengxiang, a member of the clan, took the opportunity to encourage Ye Yinlin, a villager, to live with Zhu's wife so that she could continue the family line. For several months, they lived in peace. However, Lin behaved poorly and indulged in gambling, often asking the old man for money to waste. Zhu Along, distressed by the constant harassment, often thought of ending his life. Yesterday, when Zhang went elsewhere, only the old man was at home. Ye Yinlin again asked for money, and the two quarreled. Lin then beat Zhu Along with his fists and feet, causing him to die from his injuries. Seeing that he had caused a disaster, Ye Yinlin took all the money and belongings and fled without a trace. The local police reported the incident to the county court, which dispatched officials to the village for investigation.

Jiaxing

Disaster Relief Association Distributes Flour

The disaster-stricken farmers in the Fifth District of Jiaxing are waiting to be fed. The All-Zhejiang Jiasu Relief Association and the Zhejiang Provincial Relief Affairs Association sent Gu Zongkuang and others to the villages to investigate and compile a list of disaster-stricken households, which was completed early. The list of disaster victims will be sent to the association. It is now learned that over 8,000 bags of relief flour have been shipped from Shanghai to Wangdian. Director Gu has scheduled the relief distribution from the 11th to the 14th in Wangdian. In addition to notifying local gentry and party and government agencies to send representatives to assist in the distribution, the county chamber of commerce has also appointed Qian Xingqiao to assist in Wangdian at that time. Disaster-stricken households in Yunnan, Yunbei, Baosheng, Guojie, Wangyun, Qing Si, Yinbei, Taibei, Tainan, Qixing, Daqiao, Mahuang, Yangqi, Dongzhen, Sizhen, Zhongzhen, Baofu, Zhengu, Xin'an, Fantian, Guanxing, and other townships and towns are required to gather at the Sun Yat-sen Hall in Wangdian on the designated dates to receive the relief flour with their tickets.

Hangzhou

Automobile Ferry Implemented on Qiantang River

The Qiantang River Transportation Committee, in conjunction with the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau, is preparing for an automobile ferry and has drafted regulations and various equipment. The fee for this automobile ferry is two yuan, and the fee for small package cars is one yuan each time. The proceeds from this collection will be used to subsidize the equipment expenses for crossing the river. It is scheduled to be implemented on New Year's Day of the 24th year of the Republic.

Local News

Suppression of Bandits Victory, Fifth Plenary Session Opens, All Circles in This City Celebrate Today

Meeting in the Morning, Parade in the Afternoon

Flags Fly Throughout the City to Mark the Celebration

Sailors Celebrate Simultaneously on Two Routes

All circles in this city are celebrating the victory in suppressing bandits and the opening of the Fifth Plenary Session of the Central Supervisory Committee. Preparations were made some days ago, and it was decided that a celebration meeting would be held this morning in the assembly hall of the municipal chamber of commerce, with a car parade in the afternoon. The details are as follows:

Arrangement of the Venue: The venue is the assembly hall of the municipal chamber of commerce at Tianhougong Bridge. A large colorful archway has been erected in front of the gate to the municipal chamber of commerce facing the Beisu Fu River. A white cloth banner is hung with the words "Shanghai Municipal Circles Celebrate the Victory of Bandits Suppression Representative Meeting". In the center of the hall, the party flag, the national flag, and the late Premier's portrait are hung. Order slogans are posted on both sides, and the four walls are covered with slogans, creating a solemn scene.

Meeting Order: (1) Music, (2) All stand at attention, (3) Sing the Party Song, (4) Pay the highest respect to the Party flag, the national flag, and the late Premier's portrait, (5) The chairman respectfully reads the late Premier's testament, (6) Silence, (7) Chairman's report, (8) Speeches, (9) Slogans, (10) Adjournment with music.

Scheduled Officials: Presidium: Municipal Party Department, Municipal Government, Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Municipal Farmers' Association, General Labor Union, Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Municipal Education Association, Municipal Women's Association. Records: Tong Muge, Zhu Xiaochun. Master of Ceremonies: Zhang Hanyun. Reception Director: Huang Xianggu. Reception: Huang E, Li Erbai, He Yuanming, Fan Mingyao, Lai Zhiwen, Lin Kecong, Wu Di, Wang Guoping, Cao Runshen, Du Mengsen, Bao Huizhong, etc. Inspection Director: Zhang Yingzeng. Inspectors: Xia Weiqing, Yu Yaoqiu, Yang De'an, Ren Bin, etc. The Public Security Bureau band will participate in the music.

Car Parade: The car parade measures and route have been reported previously. According to the preparatory committee, in addition to the 120 vehicles from various agencies and groups decided upon by the preparatory committee, there are reportedly more than 30 vehicles that have voluntarily registered with the committee to participate, totaling about 200 vehicles of various types.

Aircraft Celebration: To draw special attention from the city, the preparatory committee has printed millions of small colorful slogans and requested the Aviation Commission to send three aircraft to Shanghai this morning to distribute small slogans and perform for the celebration.

Citywide Flag Hanging: For a warm celebration, the preparatory committee has published a notice in the newspaper to all agencies, groups, schools, factories, shops, and residents in the city to hang flags today to celebrate. The Nanshi Huashang Tram Company and the Nanshi Zhabei Public Bus Company have plastered slogans and are flying the national flag.

Slogans Flutter: The large white bamboo cloth street-spanning slogans made by the preparatory committee have been hung in the main thoroughfares of Nanshi and Zhabei, fluttering in the wind and attracting the attention of passersby.

Sailors Hold Meeting: The Special Party Department of the China Seamen's Union at Laoximen, in addition to participating in the celebration meeting and car parade of the municipal chamber of commerce, has also scheduled to convene comrades from various districts and branches at 8:00 am today in the assembly hall of the department to celebrate the opening of the Fifth Plenary Session and the victory of bandits suppression, and to hold a grand sea parade.

Celebration on Two Routes: The Special Party Departments of the Jinghu and Huhangyong Railways, in order to celebrate the opening of the Fifth Plenary Session and the victory of bandits suppression, in addition to sending representatives to participate in the citywide celebration meeting, will also convene employees in Shanghai at 10:00 am today in the assembly hall of the North Station to hold a celebration meeting. Celebration ceremonies will be held along the various stations of the two routes to express their congratulations.

Additional News on Urgent Disaster Relief Donation

Scout Council Has Received Over 8,000 Yuan

According to the Central News Agency, since the mobilization of over 5,000 scouts on the 8th, they have been collecting donations along the streets for urgent disaster relief. Due to the urgency of the matter, the Scout Council was unable to prepare adequately, so only over 80 groups participated in the general donation, with over 30 groups unable to participate.

The results of the scouts' general donation along the streets are still being tallied and finalized as of yesterday. Over 80 groups have submitted their donations to the Scout Council, totaling over 8,000 yuan. In addition to sending them to the general directorate of the committees for general donations for urgent relief to disaster areas, other groups were unable to submit them all to the council for forwarding to the general donation for urgent relief committee due to the Sunday holiday yesterday, so they must be submitted to the council today. During this general donation, young students ran around all day soliciting donations, and their enthusiasm for disaster relief is commendable. People in the community were very moved.

Since the city launched a general donation for urgent relief to disaster areas, Mr. Du Yuesheng, a community leader, and the Yiyuan Dog Racing Track agreed to hold dog races for two days to raise funds for the general donation for urgent relief. It is reported that over 16,000 yuan has been delivered some days ago, and the second installment will be delivered soon, estimated at over 30,000 yuan. Mr. Du Yuesheng has also written to the Huili Ball Park, requesting two days to be set aside for the general donation for urgent disaster relief, which is expected to be held soon. As for performing charity shows for urgent relief, Mr. Du Yuesheng has already arranged everything separately. Mr. Du's enthusiasm for urgent relief is a model for the community and is highly admired.

The Shanghai Fourth District Shipbuilding Industry Labor Union, because its employers are British merchants, found it difficult to implement the General Labor Union's regulations for deducting wages, so they plan to voluntarily solicit donations from workers and have issued 3,000 receipts in three denominations: two jiao, four jiao, and one yuan.

The general directorate received 2,000 yuan in silver dollars and 40,000 jiao in small coins from the Scout Council yesterday. Due to the large amount, they have not yet been counted. The Shanghai Private Middle School Scout donated 233 yuan in silver dollars, over 4,900 jiao in small coins, and over 12,000 copper coins. The Sisheng Scout donated 18 yuan in silver dollars, over 1,100 jiao in small coins, and 15,008 copper coins. The Chongshi Scout donated 37 yuan in silver dollars and over 800 jiao in small coins.

The general directorate received 10,000 large slogans from the Zhongnan Printing Company and others. Various Circles Prepare for Memorial Service for Mr. Shi

Date of Meeting Set by Various Public Organizations for the 23rd; "Shen Bao" Affiliated Organizations Today

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce and Other Organizations Set a Date for a Meeting. Mr. Shi Liangcai, after returning to Shanghai from Hangzhou on the 13th of last month, was killed by bandits. Public organizations in this city, considering Mr. Shi's lifelong dedication to culture and social enterprises and his great achievements, initiated a memorial service through the Shanghai Provisional Municipal Council, the Shanghai Newspaper Association, and the Shanghai Local Association. Since the announcement was published in the newspaper, various public organizations and cultural and industrial institutions have joined enthusiastically. As of recently, there are more than fifty organizations, including the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, the Newspaper Workers' Union, the Bankers' Association, and the Chinese Students' Christian Association. It was initially proposed to hold the memorial service on the 12th of this month at the Hu She club, but as more organizations joined, a larger venue was needed for the occasion. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, considering that Mr. Shi had served as the Speaker of the Municipal Council and was a representative of the city's legal organizations, made an exception and offered the use of its venue. Due to the complexity of the preparations, the memorial service was rescheduled to the 23rd of this month. It is expected that the event will be solemn and mournful.

"Shen Bao" Affiliated Organizations to Hold Memorial Service. It is now known that the preparatory office sent personnel last night to arrange everything, with memorial banners displayed everywhere, creating a solemn atmosphere. The program for today's meeting is as follows: (1) Ringing the bell to begin the meeting, (2) Chairman's report, (3) Playing mourning music, (4) Standing in silence, (5) Silent tribute (end of silence), (6) Playing mourning music, (7) Laying wreaths, (8) Reading the eulogy, (9) Playing mourning music, (10) Bowing deeply to Mr. Shi's portrait, (11) Reciting his deeds, (12) Guest speeches, (13) Condolences, (14) Family thanks, (15) Taking photographs, (16) Playing mourning music, (17) End of ceremony.

Supplement to the Memorial Service Held the Day Before Yesterday. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Third New Ship, "Haili" Arrives at Songkou Last Night

Entering Port This Morning, Berthing at Gaochang Temple

Teng Shibiao Arrives Together, Will Inspect and Take Over

Of the four ocean-going vessels built in England with funds borrowed by the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Refund, the third ship, the "Haili," arrived in Songkou last night and is scheduled to enter port this morning for inspection and handover. Details are as follows:

Arriving and Berthing. After completion, the "Haili" set sail for China from the shipyard in Glasgow at the end of October. It passed through Gibraltar, Marseille, the Suez Canal, Aden, Colombo, Singapore, Hong Kong, and Xiamen. Due to encountering wind in the waters off Fujian and Zhejiang, the speed was reduced, resulting in a delay until about 8:00 PM last night, when it finally arrived at the Wusongkou. Due to the late hour, it anchored outside Wusongkou overnight and is scheduled to enter port today, berthing at the Jiangnan Shipyard wharf at Gaochang Temple.

Entering Port This Morning. The Shanghai representative of the shipyard, Jardine Matheson & Co., received a telegram from the "Haili" beforehand, stating that it would arrive in Shanghai in the afternoon yesterday. Until 4:00 PM yesterday afternoon, the families and relatives of Teng Shibiao and others who were arriving together welcomed them at the naval wharf at Gaochang Temple. As the ship was due to arrive late in the evening, they returned home. After entering port this morning, it is scheduled to enter the dry dock of the Jiangnan Shipyard. The style, size, and equipment of the ship are the same as the first ship, "Haiyuan," and the second ship, "Haiheng."

Inspection and Handover. After the "Haili" enters port, Jardine Matheson & Co. will jointly inspect it with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. If it is in good condition, the Jiangnan Shipyard will be ordered to paint it. After the work is completed, it will be taken over. It is reported that the designated shipowner is Teng Shibiao, and it will operate on the North and South Ocean routes in the future. As for the fourth ship, "Haizhen," which was also built by the Glasgow shipyard, it has been completed and is sailing to China, scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at the end of this month.

After the Ministry of Finance Revised Import Taxes, Sales of Domestically Produced Coal are Thriving

Imports of Foreign Coal Reduced by Half This Year

Our country's coal industry, previously affected by the dumping of foreign merchants, experienced extreme panic. It is now learned that since the Ministry of Finance revised import taxes, the domestic coal industry has become quite active. The "New News Agency" reporter specially inquired about the situation from the coal industry yesterday and recorded the details as follows:

Sales of Domestic Coal are Brisk This Year. Our country's coal industry was previously affected by the dumping of foreign coal, and sales gradually became sluggish. After the Ministry of Finance revised import taxes, it was calculated that various types of foreign coal, such as Haiphong, Hongay, MacKay, and Kailan, had to pay an additional tax of about six yuan per ton, plus an additional one yuan for water freight. The cost of foreign coal increased, resulting in brisk sales of domestic coal. According to the Coal Industry Association yesterday, sales of domestic coal in this city totaled 427,929 tons in the first half of the year, while sales in October alone in the second half of the year reached as many as 122,278 tons. It is expected that sales in November and this month will be even higher than this figure. It can be seen that after the increase in import taxes, the sales of domestic coal are booming. Therefore, they are very optimistic about the future of the industry.

Imports of Foreign Coal are Gradually Decreasing. In peacetime, the most imports of foreign coal are from French Hongay, Haiphong, MacKay, British Kailan, and Japanese Fushun, among others. In the first half of the year in this city, imports of foreign coal totaled 591,009 tons, while imports are gradually decreasing. According to a report from the National Trade Bureau, as of the end of October this year, foreign coal statistics are: Annam 1.3 million tons, Japan 1.17 million tons, India 480,000 tons, and the remaining Dutch East Indies, etc., 460,000 tons, totaling about 4.76 million tons, a decrease of more than half compared to last year.

Export of Chinese Tea to Russia

Value Increased, But Green Tea Decreased Sharply

According to the China Council for the Promotion of International Trade, the annual consumption of tea in the Soviet Union is very large. Through years of efforts in planting, domestic production has continued to increase. The area under tea cultivation has now expanded to 35,000 hectares, and the production of green tea this year reached 6,560 tons. Twenty-one new tea factories were built last year, producing 748 tons of tea, while this year it was 1,480 tons, an increase of about one-fold compared to before. The value of our country's tea exports to Russia in the first ten months of this year totaled 5,608,956 gold units, an increase compared to 4,235,124 gold units in the same period last year. However, the green tea item has decreased from 1,074,595 gold units to 407,937 gold units, a decrease of more than one and a half times. In addition to the increase in domestic production in the Soviet Union, it is also due to the competition and squeeze from Japanese tea.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Abolition of Jiangxi Province Porcelain Tax

The Other Five Categories Have Been Suspended

How Can the Porcelain Tax Exist Alone?

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday submitted a petition to the Ministry of Finance, stating: "Regarding the petition, according to the Shanghai Porcelain Industry Association, when the Jiangxi Porcelain Production and Sales Tax was changed to the Porcelain Special Business Tax in the 21st year of the Republic of China, Zhao Zijiang and other representatives of Jingdezhen porcelain merchants submitted a petition to the Jiangxi Department of Finance, stating that this temporary alternative measure, when the Jiangxi Special Goods Production and Sales Bandit Suppression Post-Disaster Tax is abolished in the future, the Porcelain Special Business Tax recognized this time should also be abolished at the same time. On November 21 of that year, the Jiangxi Department of Finance issued Approval No. 2243, approving that when the aforementioned Bandit Suppression Post-Disaster Tax is abolished, the Special Business Tax recognized by the industry will enjoy the same treatment as other industries. At that time, there were six categories of Bandit Suppression Post-Disaster Taxes, and the other five categories have been abolished and suspended on July 1 of this year. However, the Jiangxi Provincial Department of Finance still approves the annual tax amount for the porcelain industry and invites merchants to contract it, changing the temporary production and sales tax into a permanent nature, which is inconsistent with the established case of approving equal treatment for merchants. It violates the order to abolish Likin and also conflicts with the sixth item of the scope of abolishing exorbitant taxes and levies set by this year's National Finance Conference, which states that taxes and levies that hinder transportation and are levied on goods or vehicles passing through are all exorbitant and should be abolished. It is requested that it be forwarded for abolition. The association has checked the attached photograph of the approval from the Jiangxi Department of Finance, and the submitted information is all true. The industry has borne the temporary Bandit Suppression Post-Disaster Tax for nearly two years, and it has been eager to help the public and has not lagged behind. Now that other industries have been exempted, the industry's burden remains the same. How can it be fair and show great faith to the porcelain merchants? The association should submit the same photograph of the approval, requesting your department to review and approve it, and instruct Jiangxi Province to abolish the bureau and suspend the tax in accordance with the original agreement, which would be a public convenience."

Settlement of the Case of the "Songpu" Collision with the French Warship

The Three North Company's Yangtze River ship "Songpu" collided with a French warship in the Huangpu River when it set sail from Shanghai to Hankou. It is learned that the case has been settled, with the Three North Company paying the repair costs.

Cause of the Collision. The "Songpu" ship was loaded with goods and passengers in Shanghai last Friday and set sail from the Hongsheng wharf in Pudong. When the ship reached the Huangpu River, the French gunboat "Savorgnan de Brazza" was moored there, but because it was at night and the French warship did not have its lights on, it could not be seen, causing the bow of the "Songpu" to collide with the French warship. The outer hull of the French warship was damaged by the collision, and the iron plate was damaged. The "Songpu" quickly reversed, so it was not seriously damaged itself.

Joint Inspection by Both Parties. After the incident, the shipowner of the "Songpu" reported it to the company, and the French warship also reported it to the customs. The shipowner and captain inspected the damage on the spot. The "Songpu" continued to sail to the Yangtze River as usual. The next day, the Three North Company, together with the French warship, sent impartial personnel to the ship to inspect the collision damage and then discussed the handling method. They also invited impartial personnel to estimate the amount of the damage for repairs.

Settlement of the Negotiation. Yesterday, the Three North Company reached a settlement with the French warship. The Three North Company will pay the repair costs for the damage to the ship caused by the collision of the "Songpu," according to the actual estimated repair costs. The case was satisfactorily resolved. The "Songpu" has peace insurance, so it is reported that the insurance company will pay the compensation.

Report on Disaster Relief in Haining by the Bodhi Society

Chen Meiqing of the local Bodhi Dharma Assembly was sent to Haining to investigate and release the first district's emergency relief. His report states that the disaster situation in the 18 villages and towns of the first district of Haining County is detailed as follows: Since November 4, the society began to investigate and issue relief tickets to each household. It was observed that the farmers in the villages and towns of the district were in dire straits. The reason is that in previous years, silk cocoons were abundant, and the economy was prosperous, which inevitably led to waste and no savings on weekdays. The disaster of Renshen (1932) was still bearable for the farmers. In recent years, silk cocoon farmers have gone bankrupt one after another, coupled with the economic downturn, high rice prices, and high living costs, as well as successive natural disasters. This autumn, there has been a severe drought, with no water at all, and the scorching sun has raged, turning the drought into a disaster. There has been no harvest. Farmers are destitute. The association conducted a village investigation and witnessed withered rice stalks, only a foot tall, remaining in the fields. Those that looked promising were all empty husks and white water. There was no hope of a harvest. Farmers had no savings, and all mortgages had been exhausted. We also saw village women and children with hunger and yellowing faces. Their suffering is difficult to describe. In the blink of an eye, winter will arrive, and it is unknown how they will survive. The society's relief funds are limited and are a drop in the bucket, making it difficult to provide comprehensive coverage. Only the extremely poor, elderly, young, orphans, and widows among the farmers were given relief. The society is unable to cope and is helpless. It is hoped that the national government and philanthropists at home and abroad will quickly provide post-disaster winter relief so that the farmers who are waiting to be fed can overcome the difficulties of this year and seek social stability. This is a deep hope and prayer. May the country be fortunate, and may the farmers be fortunate.

Official Land in County to be Paid for and Upgraded to Taxable Land

Methods Resolved at Land Consolidation Discussion Meeting

The Shanghai County Government recently received an order from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, stating that the Shangbao Shatian Official Property Bureau had requested that Shangbao counties jointly measure the excess land and land occupied for planting without grain, and that the people should pay for them according to regulations, issue certificates, and upgrade them to taxable land. Based on this, it ordered to comply with and handle it. After receiving the order, the county magistrate convened the sixth meeting of the Land Consolidation Discussion Committee yesterday and specially submitted it for discussion at the meeting. The following methods were resolved immediately: (1) For land that is measured and found to have no documents and no grain and is proven to be official wasteland occupied by the people for planting, the people should pay for it according to regulations. (2) For land with grain and documents, or originally with documents that have been lost, but still have grain registers and registers to check, it belongs to private property. If the measured excess is small, the measures for handling the measured excess land interpreted by the Judicial Yuan ordered by the Provincial Land Bureau should be followed, and grain should be levied on the actual land. If the measured land is insufficient, shorter than the original document, the tax amount should be corrected. (3) The village land recorded in the register, originally divided into one mu of land or two or three mu as one mu to pay grain, the land obtained according to the allowable number is the actual land that the allowable land should have and cannot be referred to as land without documents and no grain and treated as official property. Whether it should be canceled in the future, the allowable conversion method or the change of the allowable land tax rules, the actual land should be upgraded to taxable land, and a report should be submitted to the department for approval, as it involves changing the amount of land tax. If there is still a small excess outside the allowable number, it should be handled according to the measures resolved in Article 2. (4) Newly formed beaches along the river and coast that have not been paid for should be paid for according to regulations. Those that have been paid for but have not been upgraded to taxable land should be upgraded to taxable land uniformly. (5) Inland river water beaches have been silted up for many years, and the original river width is mostly vague. Staff should be sent to measure and determine the river width and report to the Construction Department for approval. Then, the silted land outside the river width without documents and no grain should be paid for and upgraded to taxable land according to regulations.

Bylaws of the French Concession Council on Self-Owned Rickshaw Licenses

The French Consulate General in Shanghai has issued the bylaws of the French Municipal Council regarding the management of licenses for self-owned rickshaws in the Shanghai French Concession. (Article 1) All rickshaw pullers of self-owned rickshaws must obtain a special rickshaw license issued by the municipal authorities or police station in the area where the rickshaw registration owner resides. (Article 2) Applicants for a rickshaw license must complete an application form provided free of charge by the Municipal Council, stating the applicant's name, address, date and place of birth, and the registration number of the rickshaw. The application must be signed by the rickshaw registration owner. The applicant must personally submit the application to the Vehicle Affairs Office. Rickshaw licenses will only be issued to applicants who are physically strong and fully aware of traffic regulations. The license fee is "as per the Bureau's tax schedule." (Article 3) Rickshaw licenses are strictly for personal use only and cannot be lent or transferred. They must be renewed annually between January 1st and March 1st. These licenses are valid in both the French and International Concessions. (Article 4) The license number of the self-owned rickshaw and the owner's name must be clearly stated on the rickshaw puller's license. Any change of owner must be detailed on the license. Furthermore, the rickshaw puller must submit the license to the police station within three days of leaving the employment. If the rickshaw puller temporarily or permanently leaves the rickshaw pulling job, the license must be returned to the Vehicle Affairs Office within three days. (Article 5) All rickshaw pullers must, during their working hours, visibly wear the armband issued with the rickshaw license on their left arm, and must always carry the rickshaw license for inspection by police officers. (Article 6) Rickshaw pullers are strictly prohibited from using their owner's rickshaw for public use or rental, and are not allowed to pull vehicles other than those owned by their employer. (Article 7) All rickshaw pullers must comply with current police regulations regarding traffic. (Article 8) All rickshaw pullers must be vaccinated regularly and must comply with all other epidemic prevention measures stipulated by the Municipal Council. (Article 9) Violators of these bylaws will be subject to a fine of between five cents and twenty dollars. Those who violate the bylaws may immediately pay the fine to the arresting officer in exchange for a receipt to avoid subsequent prosecution. Otherwise, the police station will prosecute the case in court. In cases of serious violations, the rickshaw license may be confiscated or revoked by the arresting officer, and the violator may still be prosecuted.

Investigation and Prohibition of Cigarette Premium Incidents

Tobacco Factory Representatives Explain

Authorities Agree to Reconsider

Since the Ministry of Finance issued an order to all provinces and cities to investigate and prohibit cigarette premium coupons, tobacco factory operators, fearing the impact on their businesses and potential local disputes, specially appointed representatives Shen Weiting, Bao Gengsheng, and Jing Yimeng to meet with Minister Kong to explain the difference between premium coupons and sales promotion coupons, noting that the latter had already been ordered to cease, and to request a delay in the prohibition to allow for proper arrangements with the Tax Bureau for a smooth transition. Minister Kong agreed to reconsider, stating that the deadline would be discussed with the Tax Bureau, setting a date based on when the products left the factory, and allowing for the sale of cigarettes with premiums already in circulation, so that the tobacco industry across various regions would not suffer significant losses.

Exhibition of Ancient Coins of Past Dynasties Closed Yesterday

The Municipal Education Association Seeks to Make Exhibition Permanent

The China Rare Gold, Silver, and Copper Coin Exhibition, held at No. 324 Xinshijie Hotel on Nanjing Road, has received enthusiastic welcome from both Chinese and Western visitors since its opening. Yesterday was the second day. In addition to the original collection of over 2,700 types of precious coins from past dynasties on display, a valuable silver ingot from the Song Dynasty was added, encased in a redwood glass box for viewing. Mr. Wang of the exhibition said that the silver ingot weighs over fifty taels and one mace and one fen, with a value of over ten thousand yuan. However, they are committed to preserving ancient artifacts and are not willing to easily sell these precious treasures of China. The exhibition is scheduled to close today (yesterday) at 8 PM and will not be extended. After a suitable period, another exhibition will be held to allow numismatists to study the collection. In the future, they also plan to solicit contributions from collectors of ancient coins to participate. As for the Municipal Education Association's request to continue the exhibition, it will be held as soon as a suitable location is selected.

The bustling marketplace is seen as a thorny path

Thugs hold up travelers in the early morning

Ningbo Fellow Association Sends Letter Requesting Investigation

The 16th Pier in this city is where ships dock and merchants gather. Common thugs take advantage of the time when ships arrive and positions have not been restored in the early morning, forming groups of three or five to hold up travelers. Women from our hometown are eager to get home and hire vehicles to travel to Xiaodongmen, Minguo Road, and Xinkaihe, where they are often held up by groups of thugs. Cries for help are often heard. Under broad daylight, such robberies occur along the way. The bustling marketplace is seen as a thorny path. We are requesting that you forward this letter to the Municipal Public Security Bureau and ask them to quickly take preventative measures. Our Association has previously reported similar incidents to your Bureau and requested that you take measures to stop them. However, these unfortunate events continue to occur, which is deeply regrettable. Perhaps it is because the police have not yet taken their posts in the early morning that the thugs are able to take advantage and harm merchants. Our humble opinion is that your Bureau should dispatch a team of police officers to patrol that section of the road every morning to prevent these incidents. If this suggestion is adopted, not only will the people of our hometown benefit greatly, but the future of public safety will also be greatly enhanced. We await your response.

Police Officer Saves a Life

Wei Xiangxue's plight is pitiful

Yesterday morning at 2:30 AM, a young man was found hanging himself with an electric wire from a tree next to the residence of the owner of Yu Liangxin Pharmacy on Dong Maqiao in the city. A Woman in Her Prime Gives Birth to a Monstrous Fetus

Flat and Level Above the Eyebrows

With No Forehead or Hair

Shen Cangfu, from Shaoxing, works at a silk shop in this city. He married a woman named Yuan, and they rent a place at No. 131 Sanyuanfang, Yangshupu. Mrs. Yuan, who is nearing her prime, gave birth to a daughter after marrying Shen, but the child died at the age of three. This spring, she became pregnant again. On the morning of the 5th of this month, she suddenly felt abdominal pain and knew that she was about to give birth. She hired Mrs. Wang Yu, a fellow villager who lived nearby, as a midwife, agreeing to pay her ten yuan for one month of service. Mrs. Yuan suffered until 2:30 AM that night before finally giving birth. The infant, a girl, landed in the basin, but made no sound. When illuminated by candlelight, the child's facial features and limbs were fully formed, but the head was markedly different from normal. Above the eyebrows, it was flat and level, with no forehead or hair, covered only by a thin layer of skin. A person without a brain has no hope of agility, so the child died as soon as it was born, like a flash in the pan. Mr. and Mrs. Shen believed that the child's death was due to Mrs. Wang Yu's failure to perform the delivery properly, causing the child's head to hit the basin, resulting in the condition. They refused to honor the service agreement and did not pay the midwife any fee. However, the midwife firmly stated that she was not responsible for any negligence and insisted on receiving her due payment. They argued and clashed. Shen then took the dead child and dragged the midwife to the Yangqiao Police Station. After questioning by the police chief, Mrs. Wang Yu was told to leave, and the child's body was sent to the Philen Road mortuary. Yesterday, a report was made to the First Special District District Court Prosecutor's Office, which appointed Prosecutor Song to lead a forensic doctor to the mortuary to examine the body. After questioning Shen and Mrs. Wang Yu, they determined that the child was indeed a deformed fetus, which had great significance for physiological research. They ordered the child's body to be temporarily stored in the mortuary for research. It is truly a monstrous fetus.

Luring Women to Qingdao for Trafficking

Zhang A'mei Almost Falls into a Trap

Zhang Caiyun Still Being Solicited

- One Case Leads to Another -

Zhang A'mei, a woman from Suzhou, is 18 years old and used to work as a hostess at the New World Amusement Park. She is slightly attractive and very romantic. She became acquainted with Zhou A'si and had an affair. Later, when the New World Amusement Park closed, Zhang lived with her sister, Zhang A'jin, at the Wang Yuanchang Electric Shop on Guling Road, but secretly continued her affair with Zhou A'si. Little did she know that Zhou was a rogue. Seeing that Zhang's money was running out, he had evil intentions. Not only did he abandon his former love, but he also wanted to traffic her to another location to get a huge price for her, which he would waste. He secretly discussed this matter with Chen Shouming (also known as Zhang Shouming), a Hubei native living at No. 34 Santai Lane. Chen often went to Qingdao, and his mistress, Chen Zhu, from Tongzhou, whose nickname was Da Mai, was quite familiar with local thugs in the Qingdao area. Zhu colluded with Mu Gu, a woman from Songjiang, to make arrangements with someone surnamed in Qingdao. Zhou A'si falsely told Zhang that he had found her a factory job in Qingdao with a monthly salary of 30 yuan, and asked her to go there. Zhang believed him and went to Chen Shouming's house at No. 34 Santai Lane on the 4th to stay temporarily. Chen bought five boat tickets, preparing to leave for Qingdao in two batches yesterday. Chen and Zhou were in the first batch, and Chen Zhu, Mu Gu, and Zhang A'mei were in the second batch. Zhu and A'mei pretended to be sisters to avoid scrutiny along the way. Everything was ready, but the plan was not kept secret. The detectives from the Huishi Police Station, Liang Yuliang, Bao Wenbin, and Chen Kezhang, learned of the plan and secretly went to No. 34 Santai Lane at 11:50 PM the day before yesterday, arresting Chen Shouming, Chen Zhu, Mu Gu, Chen's brother Chen Shouyu, Chen's sister-in-law Chen Xu, Chen's younger brother Chen Fufu, and Zhang A'mei. Zhou A'si was not present and escaped the arrest. The detectives found three boat tickets on Chen Shouming and two boat tickets and two letters on Chen Zhu. The letters generally stated when the goods (referring to the person) would arrive. A photo of a woman was also found on Mu Gu. Based on the photo and the statements of the arrested, another case arose. The woman in the photo was Zhang Caiyun from Wuxi, 17 years old, tall, and beautiful. Three days ago, she was lured by Chen Xiuying, a woman from the same hometown, and traveled to Shanghai with Lu Zizhen by car. They first stayed at Room 17 of the Sutai Hotel on Sima Road, and then moved to No. 111 Taianli on Tiantong Road. It was also learned that Mu Gu was an experienced trafficker, and had sent Zhang Caiyun's photo to Qingdao to solicit customers. If a buyer was found, she would be informed by letter to bring her there. The detectives then went to No. 111 Taianli and arrested Chen Xiuying, Lu Zizhen, and their accomplices Gu Agen and Fang Fuzhang, along with Zhang Caiyun, and detained them separately. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special Court. The police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the above situation and requested permission to detain the arrested. After questioning by Judge Wu Tingqi, Chen Shouyu, Chen Xu, Chen Fufu, and Gu Agen were allowed to be released on bail, subject to immediate recall. The remaining persons were detained and the trial was postponed for seven days. Zhang A'mei was taken back by her sister, Zhang A'jin, and Zhang Caiyun was sent to a relief organization for temporary shelter.
