Liu Zhongying Discusses the Preparation Process for the Jiangxi Provincial National Products Exhibition

The Shanghai Chinese Domestic Manufacturers Association led member manufacturers to participate in the Jiangxi Provincial Capital National Products Exhibition. Due to misunderstandings among the business community in that province, the exhibition was repeatedly postponed, and the preparation time reached three months. It is now known that the exhibition officially opened on the 8th of this month. Yesterday, Standing Committee member Liu Zhongying of the Association gave a detailed account of the participation in the Jiangxi exhibition, which is specially recorded as follows:

Initiation and Organization: It is said that the Jiangxi National Products Exhibition was originally initiated by the Association, which had sent letters and telegrams to various party and government agencies in Jiangxi Province, and received their agreement. The province then vigorously supported and welcomed the exhibition with repeated telegrams (as reported in the newspapers). The Association then sent personnel to Jiangxi to prepare for the exhibition together with various sectors of Jiangxi society. First, the Jiangxi Provincial Party Department and Provincial Government convened a joint meeting of representatives from various Jiangxi agencies and the Association to resolve the holding of the exhibition, and established the Jiangxi National Products Exhibition Preparatory Committee. Regarding the expenses of manufacturers, such as booth construction and electricity costs, all were to be provided by the Association, while the Jiangxi side was responsible for the preparatory expenses. Both parties aimed to promote domestic products and recover rights and interests, and worked together.

Beginning Preparations: Liu also said that after the Association's representatives resolved to hold the exhibition at the joint meeting, they returned to Shanghai to report on the negotiation process and the joint meeting's proposals. The Association believed that since all sectors of Jiangxi Province were willing to provide such support, for the sake of the future of domestic products, it should make efforts to proceed. Therefore, on September 20, the Association's Standing Committee meeting resolved to announce the start of preparations and notified member manufacturers to register for participation. Because Jiangxi is the birthplace of the New Life Movement, and its publicity for the promotion of domestic products would definitely be more effective, the members all readily supported and actively participated. Within a week, the quota of 150 industries was filled.

Midway Obstacles: It is also said that after the Association started preparations, because it received support from various agencies in Jiangxi, the members also actively participated, and it was decided that the National Products Exhibition would open on Double Tenth Day (October 10th). A representative was specially sent to Jiangxi again to build the venue and actively make arrangements. Unexpectedly, while preparations were in full swing, the Jiangxi City Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations suddenly raised concerns about dumping and sent telegrams to the party and government agencies in Shanghai and Jiangxi, requesting the cancellation of the proposal and preventing the holding of the exhibition. The Association believed that although the Jiangxi exhibition was initiated by the Association, it had received the support of various agencies in Jiangxi. Moreover, the organizers were the Jiangxi Provincial Party Department and the Provincial Government, which convened a joint meeting of representatives from various agencies. The Jiangxi City Chamber of Commerce also sent a representative, Mr. Zhou Zishi, to attend and participate in the meeting. During the meeting, the representatives not only had no words of opposition, but also did their best to support the initiative. Now that the City Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations suddenly opposed the exhibition when the Association's preparations were about to be completed, was this not childish? Therefore, based on reason, telegrams were sent to various relevant agencies to strive for the exhibition, and the opening of the National Products Exhibition was therefore repeatedly postponed until it was finally implemented on the 8th of this month.

Negotiation Process: It is also said that after the Jiangxi City Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations opposed the exhibition, the Jiangxi party and government agencies rejected the opposition of the City Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations after the Association protested. However, the Jiangxi side was still unwilling to accept this, and demanded the collection of public welfare donations (10% of the value) and demanded that manufacturers subsidize the Jiangxi side's office expenses (2% of the value), using various unreasonable conditions as a threat and deliberately making things difficult. The Association believed that the exhibition of domestic products, according to the regulations of the Ministry of Industry, did not impose taxes or donations, and could also be exempt from state-owned vehicle transportation fees. As for the Jiangxi side's office expenses, the representatives had resolved that the Jiangxi side would be responsible. Now the Jiangxi Province was inventing various names, obscuringly requesting harsh taxes and levies, and not complying with the resolutions, which violated the original purpose of the central government's domestic product movement. Therefore, based on the Ministry's orders and regulations, and according to the precedents of national exhibitions in various places, it requested exemption. However, the Jiangxi side still insisted on a subsidy of 1,000 for office expenses, which remained unresolved. This is truly an unfortunate phenomenon that has never occurred in the domestic product movement.

Opening Situation: It is also said that after the misunderstanding occurred in Jiangxi Province and the exhibition was suspended midway, the opening day was repeatedly postponed. This time it was determined to open on the 8th of this month. Because it was approaching the end of the year, it was really impossible to postpone it any further. Therefore, the Association decided to first open the exhibition as scheduled, and at the same time, according to the resolution of the representatives' meeting, continue to protest to the relevant agencies. According to a telegram from the Association's Jiangxi representative, Mrs. Xiong, the chairman's wife, cut the ribbon at the opening ceremony of the Jiangxi exhibition. Chairman Xiong and hundreds of leaders from all walks of life and manufacturer representatives attended the meeting to deliver speeches. The ceremony was very grand, and the people of Jiangxi who came to the meeting to visit and purchase goods were also very enthusiastic.

Three Organizations Held a Meeting Yesterday to Commemorate Mr. He Caitang

The Commercial Bank of China, the Ningbo Native Place Association in Shanghai, and the Dinghai Native Place Association in Shanghai held a memorial service yesterday at the Dinghai Guild Hall on Pingjili Road in the French Concession for the late Mr. He Caitang, the Assistant Manager of the Commercial Bank of China. The venue was filled with elegiac couplets and poems, and the scene was unusually solemn. More than 400 people, including Mr. Yu Qiaqing, Yu Zuoting, Fu Xiaoan, Zhang Shenzhi, Fang Jiaobo, Wu Zhihao, Zhu Qixiang, and relatives and friends Zhu Zikui, Zhang Zixiang, etc., arrived. At 2:00 p.m., the bell rang, mourning music was played, and the meeting began. Mr. Chen Liangyu chaired the meeting and reported on the purpose of the meeting. Then, Mr. Chen Yiting described Mr. He's deeds, and Mr. Hu Yinong read the eulogy by Mr. Liu Hongsheng, the chairman of the Dinghai Native Place Association. Two classes of male and female primary school students from the Dinghai Native Place Association performed ceremonies in turn and sang a memorial song. Then, Mr. Fu Xiaoan described Mr. He's relationship with the Commercial Bank of China and his personal friendship with him, and proposed that Mr. He be posthumously given the title "Tong Zhong," which was unanimously approved on the spot. Later, Mr. Fang Jiaobo, Mr. Wu Zhihao, Mr. Yuan Ludeng, Mr. Hong Yanbin, Mr. Xu Tingzuo, Mr. Zhang Xiaogeng, Mr. Wu Yaqin, and others delivered speeches successively, describing Mr. He's internal conduct, his literary talent, his enthusiasm for public welfare, his loyalty to his duties, his respect and love for his friends, his filial piety to his old mother, and his brotherly love in great detail. Mr. Wu Zhihao also advocated collecting Mr. He's manuscripts to prevent them from being lost, and to seek commercial assistance for his younger siblings. The audience applauded unanimously. Finally, Mr. He Qiliang, a family member, gave a speech of thanks. The meeting ended at around 4:00 p.m.

Zheng Tangsheng and Others' Conspiracy to Escape from Prison Concluded

Sentencing scheduled for the 15th

The notorious kidnapper Zheng Tangsheng, a local, was arrested in Tianjin by detectives sent by the French Concession Police Station in the autumn of last year and brought to Shanghai. He was sent to the Second Special District Court and prosecuted in accordance with the Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits. During the trial, Zheng once attempted suicide in the police station detention center out of fear of his crime, but was rescued and recovered. Later, he was sentenced to death. Zheng refused to accept the verdict and petitioned the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval to send the case back for retrial. Because the case was not finalized, Zheng was detained in the detention center of the Second Special District Court. Unexpectedly, in the past month, Zheng colluded with Liu Ruiqing, a guard from Yangzhou, and sent a letter to his friend Li Quangen, asking him to procure pistols, gunpowder, and strong water, hoping to set a date to escape from prison. Because the matter was not kept secret, it was leaked out and detected by the French police, who arrested Li Quangen and notified the detention center to transfer Zheng and the guard Liu Ruiqing to the prosecutor for investigation and prosecution. The police also transferred Li Quangen to the Second Special District Court for prosecution. After the case was first tried by the preliminary court, it was transferred to the local court for trial due to the importance of the case. After the presiding judge of the criminal court, Wang Gangxu, and the chief prosecutor, Chen Beisan, held a court session and briefly interrogated the defendants, they ordered the witnesses Zhang Asi, Wu Shaoting, Liu Guibao, and others, who were also detained in the same place, to be brought in, and summoned Mr. Wu, the staff member of the detention center who was in charge of inspecting the prisoners' correspondence, to the case. After interrogating them, they ordered the start of the debate. First, the prosecutor stood up and stated that the defendants had committed the crime of escaping under Article 171, Paragraph 3, and the crime of bribery under Article 128 of the Criminal Law, and requested that they be punished according to the law. Then, the police lawyer Gu Shouxi argued that the circumstances of the defendants' attempt to escape had been thoroughly investigated and clarified by the court. Regarding the Criminal Law, the prosecutor had already stated that the defendants intended to damage the detention center and attempted to escape from prison by using violent coercion. The facts were obvious, and they should be severely punished according to the law. The defendant Li Quangen was defended by lawyer Shen Xingxia, who argued that, after examining the letters sent by Zheng Tangsheng to Li Quangen, there was the phrase "(If you don't find a way, I am determined to hang myself)," which showed that although Li Quangen's reply to Zheng's letter contained the words "(The things will be ready in about two or three days)," regardless of whether he was forced by Zheng Tangsheng's suicide threat and was giving comfort out of private feelings, he still said "(about)," which was difficult to recognize as a determination to help procure the items. Also, it was found that the attempt crimes in each paragraph of Article 171 of the Criminal Law were based on the act of failure to carry out the crime, not on the intention to commit the crime. This can be seen from the fact that the words "(intention)" were not added to other legal articles. Assuming that the items mentioned in Li Quangen's letter were indeed pistols, and had already been procured and prepared for delivery, which would be enough to help Zheng Tangsheng gather a crowd to violently coerce an escape, then before Zheng Tangsheng received them, it could only be recognized that Li Quangen had agreed to prepare to help Zheng Tangsheng commit a crime, but had not completed it, and had not reached the extent of facilitating Zheng's escape, and had not carried out the attempted act. What's more, the items had not been procured, and it was difficult to determine whether they would be procured. According to the law, it was difficult to recognize that he had formed an attempted escape. Also, it was found that Article 39 of the Criminal Law stated that "(an attempted crime is one that has begun to carry out the crime but has not succeeded)." In this case, Li Quangen only had the intention to help commit a crime (preparation) but did not succeed, and had not reached the stage of starting to help commit the crime (implementation). Since the preparation of the criminal intent cannot be separated from the stage of implementation, it can directly help others cause a certain result of committing a crime. According to the above-mentioned legal articles, it is even more difficult to make him bear the responsibility for attempted crime. Citing the so-called pre-event preparatory act in the judgments of the Supreme Court of the 21st year, Feizi Xin No. 9, No. 97, it should not be regarded as a precedent for starting the crime. Then, the part of Zheng Tangsheng, Li Quangen, and others' conspiracy to escape from prison, even the most important law, does not constitute a crime, etc. Zheng Tangsheng was defended by lawyer Ding Yuanpu, whose words were roughly the same as before. After verifying the statements in court, the court announced the end of the debate, and scheduled the sentencing for 9:00 a.m. on the 15th. The defendants were still returned to custody separately.

A New Ghost in the Dafang Hotel

The deceased claimed to be Wu Jialin

A traveler came to the Dafang Hotel on Zhengjia Muqiao Street in the French Concession at around 5:00 p.m. the day before yesterday. He was wearing a Western-style suit and claimed to be Wu Jialin from Nanjing, 19 years old, who worked in hardware. He was greeted and led to the fourth floor, Room 431. He went out once at around 10:00 p.m., and soon returned to bed. At 12:00 a.m. the next morning, the tea boy saw that he had not gotten up, so he knocked on the door several times, but there was no response. He then tried to pry open the door and went inside to check, and saw that he had died. Later, an empty cigarette case was found under the bed, and it was known that he had died of poisoning. He then reported it to the police station, who sent detectives to the scene to transport the body to the Tongren Fuyuantang Mortuary to examine the body, pending a report to the court for an inspection.

Li Boliang Invented the Boliang Stove

Li Boliang, the director of the workshop of the Dagong Vocational School, graduated from the Department of Mechanical Engineering of the Osaka Higher Technical School in Japan. After returning to China, he successively served as the factory director of the Pudong Hengda Yarn Factory and the director of the Department of Mechanical Engineering of the Jiangsu Provincial First Industrial College for more than ten years. He has specialized knowledge of various machines, and has spared no effort in research on weekdays. Recently, seeing the wood chips piled up like a mountain in the school's woodworking workshop, making it difficult to find a suitable outlet, he used waste to invent a wood chip-saving stove for heating in the cold weather. The advantages of this stove are superior to various coal-burning stoves: first, it saves money. The cost for the whole day is less than half that of a coal stove, and the firepower is greater; second, it is convenient to light. Only one match is needed, and the entire stove can be completely lit within half a minute; third, the firepower can be increased or decreased freely; fourth, regardless of size, there is no need to add fuel or remove ashes within twelve hours; fifth, you can safely go to bed and sleep at night, without any danger; sixth, it is smokeless, non-toxic, odorless, and dust-free, and is exceptionally clean; seventh, the top of the stove can be used for cooking, which can be said to kill many birds with one stone. After Mr. Li's operation, this stove has been improved again and again. The results of the public trial on Thursday this week at the school were excellent and convenient for the public. Because it is the crystallization of Mr. Li's scientific research, it is named the Boliang Stove. As for its exquisite structure and beautiful style, it is just a matter of course. It is reported that it has been submitted to the Ministry for registration and application for a patent. It is believed that once this stove becomes popular, those who need to keep warm will rush to buy it.

Appeal in Counterfeit Case Scheduled for Sentencing

The Defu Foreign Company at No. 261 Sichuan Road sells various pigments. One type of red pigment used for candles is produced by the German Dada Pigment Factory. The Defu Foreign Company registered the red candlestick as a trademark with the Trademark Office of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the National Government, and it is widely sold. In October of this year, it was discovered that the Tongrenhe Pigment Store at No. 80 Minguo Road in the French Concession was counterfeiting the red candlestick trademark and selling it on the market, which affected sales. The manager of the company, an Englishman named Li Anha (transliteration), reported it to the French police station, who sent detectives to search Tongrenhe and seized ten cans of counterfeit pigments and 3,500 counterfeit trademark papers. It was found that they were printed by the Xinmin Printing House at No. 49 Xinxin Street in the Nanshi. The owner of the store, Xu Chengxun (Zi Huiping, 35 years old, Shanghai native), was taken to the police station along with the evidence, and the police lawyer filed a public lawsuit with the Second Special District Court on the charge of obstructing agriculture, industry, and commerce. After the trial was concluded, Xu Chengxun was sentenced to two months of imprisonment and a fine of 300 yuan for counterfeiting a registered trademark with the intention of deceiving others. During the appeal period, he was ordered to provide reliable shop guarantees. Xu refused to accept the original judgment and filed an appeal with the collegiate panel of the Second Special District Court. After an investigation was concluded, Wang Gangxu, the presiding judge of the criminal court, and two judges, Li Changnian and Qiu Huanqing, opened a court session to hear the case the day before yesterday. Fei Xizhen, a lawyer from the Police Department, appeared in court. The appellant and his defense lawyer appeared in court. The original plaintiff, Li Anha, also appeared in court with an interpreter. According to the appellant's statement, since the eighteenth year, he had been trading with the Aodefu Foreign Company. In order to facilitate the payment of tariffs, he purchased large barrels of pigments and took them to Shanghai. In order to facilitate sales, he repackaged them into small cans and sold them with the original brand. He mistakenly violated the law because he was not familiar with the law. Although it was a counterfeit brand, it was different from other counterfeit situations in general. The original sentence was too severe, so he filed an appeal, requesting a change of the sentence to a lighter one. Then, after mutual debate by the two lawyers, the court announced the end of the debate and listened to the scheduled sentencing. The appellant was still released on bail by the original guarantor.

Victims of Private Gravesites Being Confiscated as Government Property Seek Relief from the Ningbo Native Place Association

The Ningbo Native Place Association in Shanghai received a letter yesterday from Fan Yunqing and other fellow villagers from Yin County, stating: "Since the Old Ningbo Official Property Clearance Office began clearing official property, local thugs and vagrants have taken the opportunity to covet ancestral gravesites owned by others, falsely reporting them to the Official Property Office as unclaimed land and introducing them for sale. The Official Property Office then issues notices, setting deadlines for the descendants to dismantle and relocate the graves on the land. The descendants of the affected gravesites have specifically submitted genealogies and deeds, or, in cases where deeds are temporarily unavailable, requested the Official Property Office to waive the demolition and valuation. However, these requests have not been granted. Moreover, most of these graves date back to the Qianlong era, or there are deeds without genealogies, or genealogies without deeds. Although we cannot say that the evidence is completely sufficient, some of it can be proven. Furthermore, the government has issued orders protecting ancient tombs and cemeteries, and the Official Property Office disregards merchants and accepts bribes. We request you to find a way to provide relief, etc." It is reported that the association, based on the information, sent a letter to County Magistrate Chen of the neighboring county, requesting him to negotiate with the Official Property Office and asking them to handle the matter with caution.

Xu Wancheng Solicits Answers to the "How Do I Get Rich?" Plan

Mr. Xu Wancheng telegraphed to the authorities of major secondary and high schools nationwide: "In this time of poverty, lack of food and clothing, malnutrition, illness, spiritual depression, and stagnation in all areas, the inferior roots of narrow-mindedness, deceit, hypocrisy, and indifference are becoming increasingly apparent. As Guanzi said, 'When food and clothing are sufficient, then one knows etiquette and righteousness.' In the future, education must focus on material construction before national rejuvenation can be achieved. Therefore, I am soliciting answers to the 'How Do I Get Rich?' plan, in other words, what are the legitimate ways for everyone to seek a livelihood, work hard, and become rich? It is definitely not buying aviation lottery tickets, gambling, pimping, or selling opium, etc., or having unrealistic thoughts of getting rich quick. I request the authorities of major secondary and high schools nationwide to solicit answers from students, so that a special collection can be published to guide each other, which will greatly benefit the youth." Mr. Xu also hopes that people from all walks of life will actively respond to this question, so that we can gather wisdom and build together to make everyone rich. Manuscripts should be sent to Xu Wancheng, Editorial Department, Longwen Bookstore, Dananmen, Shanghai. All respondents will receive a framed saying inscribed by more than forty people, including Cai Yuanpei, Ma Junwu, Huang Renzhi, Jiang Menglin, and Jiang Kanghu. Mr. Xu has a great interest in studying life's problems. His recently compiled "Discussion Collection on Life's Problems" has been widely read. The book "My Outlook on Life," soliciting the opinions of more than a thousand people nationwide, will also be published next spring.

Spring and Autumn

Little Western Paradise

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter Five: Fawning and Flattering with a Lit Lamp to Illuminate a Withered Hungry Stomach - Displaying Frivolity

These last few words seemed to touch Yueying's heart, and she remained silent. Sister-in-law Hu saw her opportunity and picked up the hot water kettle to pour into the basin. She grabbed a towel and was about to wipe his face. Yueying took the towel, stood up, and sighed, "Oh! Let me do it." She was indeed a clever girl. Ready-made cosmetics were available here, and with Sister-in-law Hu's guidance, she spent thirty minutes re-touching her face. As soon as she put on a floral Western-style qipao, Xiao Ji pushed open the door and came in. Such a coincidence, he must have been peeking outside, making Yueying so ashamed that she immediately turned her back. Xiao Ji smiled at Sister-in-law Hu and said, "This move works. If you do this in front of Old Master Jia, he's sure to like it." Yueying couldn't bear it and turned around, putting on a stern face. Xiao Ji ignored her, looked her up and down, and smiled, "It's okay, but the powder on your nose isn't evenly applied. Watch me." As he spoke, he held up a small mirror in his left hand, picked up a powder puff from the powder box with his right hand, and randomly dabbed it on her face and nose. While applying the powder, he twisted his head left and right in front of the mirror. Although Yueying was very upset, she couldn't help but laugh. He didn't care, handing the mirror and powder puff to Yueying, and said with a smile, "Here, you do it." He casually wiped his face with the towel Yueying had used. Yueying held the powder puff in her hand, dumbfounded. Xiao Ji said, "What's wrong? Even out the powder on your face, and we can go!" Yueying looked back at Sister-in-law Hu, remaining silent. She thought, since she had applied the powder, she should apply it well. Be frivolous, be vulgar, it's better than starving to death anyway. So she learned from Xiao Ji, dipped the powder puff in powder, and dabbed it on her cheeks and the tip of her nose in front of the mirror. Xiao Ji nodded secretly and praised her. However, Yueying's heart was more painful than being cut by a knife. Perhaps not all women with faces full of rouge and powder are happy. (85)

Bits and Pieces

— (Xiong Yu)

Everyone knows the principle that being able to laugh out loud once a day is good for health. I alone say that being able to cry out loud once a day is even better than laughing.

For suppressed and magnanimous feelings that have no way to vent, and for those who want to laugh but cannot, a good cry will dispel all the pent-up emotions.

Wang's Head and Feng's Arm

— Holding Buddha

During the Spring Festival of the second year of the Republic, our principal, Feng Bingsou, along with Mr. Feng Sigong, Mr. Feng Fufu, and others, went to a desolate mound outside Beiguo in our hometown to pay their respects. I asked if this mound belonged to a talented but unappreciated scholar or a chaste woman of ice and jade, why did it inspire the local gentlemen to come and mourn?

It turned out that the mound did not contain an entire body, only an arm and a head. The head belonged to Mr. Wang, and the arm belonged to Mr. Feng. That's what my friend said.

Oh! So they are the tombs of two national heroes! Mr. Wang's name was Du'an, and Mr. Feng's name was Tanxi. They both followed Zhang Cangshui in resisting the Qing army and died for their country. Later generations only found an arm of Mr. Feng and a head of Mr. Wang. Pitying their loyalty and righteousness, they buried them together as a memorial. My friend said again, and then I understood.

When the Southern Capital was overthrown, Zhang Cangshui and Qian Sule, among others in our hometown, supported Prince Lu as regent. The loyal and righteous people's army repeatedly resisted the Qing army, which greatly frightened the Qing court. Later, Zhang Gong advised Zheng Yanping to take Nanjing, entering the river from Chongming, and they were victorious everywhere. Zhang Gong first moved his troops upstream, directly capturing Jiujiang, and the military power was very strong. Later, Yanping was defeated, and Prince Lu also died. Wang Du'an, who initiated the righteous cause with Zhang Gong, suddenly had a quarrel with his wife one day, scolding and arguing, causing a great uproar. As a result, he sent his wife back to her parents' home, severing their relationship forever. The neighbors were very surprised to see this, thinking that Mr. Wang was a righteous man, so why was he so unrighteous to his wife? They were all suspicious in their hearts.

Later, Zhang Cangshui scattered his troops and lived in seclusion on Zhoushan Island, where he was discovered by Qing soldiers and died unyielding. The two gentlemen, Wang and Feng, must have also died for their country, unlike Hong Chengchou and Qian Muzhai, who willingly became second-rate officials! After Mr. Wang was killed by the Qing army, his reason for resolutely divorcing his wife was finally understood.

Wild Ducks

— Zhu Shaofei

In the early winter evening, wild ducks flew in flocks across the gray and vast sky, their voices so clear and loud, resembling airplanes arranged in formation and moving forward.

The weather is getting colder, and they feel that the northern lands are harsh, cold, and hungry, so they have to laboriously flap their wings, hoping to survive. However, their lives are still lost in the hands of southern fishermen.

Wild ducks are on the market again. Fishermen's faces are filled with smiles, and even those who are not used to eating game want to taste some.

In my hometown of Dongshan, this season is the peak time for fishermen to catch wild ducks. There are hawkers who specialize in selling ducks. They buy at low prices and sell them to Suzhou and Shanghai. In Dongshan, they cost only a thousand or so cash per pair, but when sold outside, they are worth about a yuan per pair. The hawkers earn more profit than the fishermen with a single turnover.

In the reed ponds and shallow waters by Taihu Lake, fishermen each guard their territory, setting nets, pulling bows, and releasing a few wild ducks as "decoys." They stare with sharp eyes, gazing intently at the sky, waiting, waiting. When the flock of wild ducks arrives, they jerk the "decoy ducks" to make them call. The flying ducks hear the calls below and will fly down, throwing themselves into the net.

The nets are laid in the reed ponds. When the ducks fly into the net, the rope is pulled in, and they are rolled into the net one by one. The bow pullers insert a half bamboo pole into the mud, with each pole a zhang apart. The rope is tightly tied to the top of the pole, and the rope is tied in a loose circle. Another rope is used to pull the bamboo pole down. When the time comes, the rope that pulls the bamboo pole down is released, and the bamboo pole stands upright, trapping the heads, feet, and wings of the wild ducks. That's why only Dongshan has live wild ducks for sale.

There is also a type of wild duck called "Yangtze cargo." Most of the wild game sold in Shanghai comes from the Yangtze River. It is said that "Yangtze cargo" is not caught like Dongshan ducks. They use hunting guns to shoot them, or they mix poisonous powder with food and spread it on the beach. When the wild ducks fly to the beach to find food, they eat this poisonous food and die. Fishermen just go and pick them up in the morning. That's why they are not as fresh and delicious as Dongshan cargo.

Resist!

— Shi Ying

Temple Foundation and Field Frog

— Ma Fosheng

Dried tofu, also known as fragrant dried tofu, is exceptionally delicious when eaten with peanuts, so it is also called vegetarian ham, and the price is very cheap. But the most exquisite production method belongs to Keqiao in Shaoxing. If you happen to pass by the stations of the Shao-Xiao Highway or the Hang-Jiang Railway, you will surely hear vendors shouting to sell Keqiao dried tofu. This can truly be worthy of the eight characters "cheap and good, famous all over the world" without any shame.

Speaking of Keqiao dried tofu, there is also a very funny anecdote, that is, the misunderstanding between "temple foundation" and "field frog." Originally, there was more than one store selling dried tofu in Keqiao, but among them, the most famous was the tofu shop in Dianji Lane. Therefore, out-of-town customers only knew about the dried tofu in Dianji Lane when they came to buy dried tofu, but forgot the name of the shop. Tracing back to the name of Dianji Lane, it was because there was originally a Zhang Shen Temple here. Later, it was unknown when the Zhang Shen Temple was destroyed, leaving only a temple foundation, so this lane was called Dianji Lane. (Now, not only is there no trace of the temple foundation, but even Dianji Lane is gone.) However, outsiders do not know the truth and mistakenly recognize "temple foundation" as "field frog"; moreover, they also embellish it with a rumor, saying: Keqiao Field Frog Lane is famous because there are many field frogs. This tofu shop catches the field frogs in the lane and boils them in soup as the juice for the dried tofu, so its dried tofu is particularly delicious, causing vegetarian old ladies to be suspicious and dare not eat it. Don't you think this is ridiculous?

Records of Lingering Fragrance from the Imperial Palace

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling, translated by Qin Shouou

After the Empress Dowager entered this palace courtyard, she suddenly seemed to lose consciousness. Her eyes were always staring straight ahead, and her walking was also very unnatural, as stiff as someone walking in a dream. But there were no tears on her cheeks. She just walked to a glass box on the left to look at it like she had lost her mind, and then turned to a box on the right to look at it; or she looked at it again once, twice, three times, even countless times. What made her especially embarrassed was that Xianfeng's relics were particularly few, not only could they not compare with Qianlong's, but they were also far behind those of other emperors of previous dynasties. It can be said to be the smallest part! Simply pitifully few! What is the reason for this? It's very simple to say. We people can be said to know everything. Or among the readers of this book, there are also many who understand. To put it simply, it is because this great emperor only knew how to enjoy himself during his lifetime. Gambling, drinking, almost all of them were his daily routines; in addition, in addition, there is no need to hide it, he also had a fondness for lust. If a person has so many bad habits, of course he can no longer be proficient in literary or martial arts; and the court affairs that he should handle are also completely abandoned. Strictly speaking, the reason why the Qing Dynasty declined and eventually perished, the first seed, may as well be said to have been sown by him. At least, no one can defend him, saying that he is not a昏君 (昏君: a fatuous and incompetent ruler) who has done nothing!

When we were visiting from the two palace courtyards in front, because we saw that the Empress Dowager was pointing east and west and talking very happily, everyone unconsciously forgot to be afraid and asked various questions, either directly asking her, or the two of them discussing with each other. The situation was very lively; but when we arrived here, we secretly glanced at her complexion and realized it was wrong, and quickly became aware of the situation. Everyone tried their best to endure and did not dare to say a word (195).

Small Gardening

Hibiscus and Papaya

— Zheng Yimei

(1) Hibiscus

"Having a woman in the same carriage, her face is like the hibiscus flower," which means that the hibiscus flower is a metaphor for the beauty of a woman. The hibiscus is a deciduous shrub, six or seven feet tall, with lush branches and leaves. It blooms from the turn of summer and autumn, and does not stop in winter. Therefore, Xu Ning has the sentence "Who says the hibiscus flower is born with a sense of haste, it is pitiful to count half a year of red." The flowers have several colors of red, white, purple and yellow, with five petals and short stalks like hollyhocks. The sunlight is shining, and it is suspected that flames are born, so it has the name of morning fungus. Other nicknames, such as Buddha Sang, Hibiscus, Jade Steaming, and Mu Ji are all. Or it is said that Shun Ying is a pure white and uninterrupted flower.

Flowers with double petals are better, single petals are only suitable for weaving into hedges, so they are named Hedge Hibiscus, the lowest of the flowers. It is said that when weaving a hedge, it must be inserted continuously without stopping. If it is done intermittently, it will be difficult to live. I don't know if it is true, it is really incomprehensible.

Hibiscus tender leaves can be used as a tea substitute. Tingzhou people in Min fry hibiscus flowers with noodles, so they call it noodle flowers. Also, Yu Chongzhi said: Pick red hibiscus, wrap yellow plums in leaves, pickle them in salt and dry them in the sun to recommend wine, so it is named Jade Xiu.

The red hibiscus in Lingnan blooms often from January to December, see Lingnan Exotic Objects, it is charming all year round, it is indeed lovely, is it because of the warm climate in the south?

There are not many hibiscus poems. Cui Daorong said: Hibiscus flowers are rarely seen, a new one every day. Yang Lingyun said: Towards the evening, they compete to dismiss the stamens, and the flowers bloom in the morning. Li Shangyin said: Deep red and fresh are mixed together, it is difficult to tell whether to cry or laugh. Yang Wanli said: The hedges are sparse along the road and piled up like brocade, blooming in the morning and falling in the evening and blooming again in the morning. What I have recorded is only this.

(2) Papaya

In addition to fragrant citron and Buddha's hand, papaya is also a clear offering in the study. Papaya is a deciduous shrub, six or seven feet tall, with flowers before leaves. The flowers are divided into red and white, which are beautiful and unusual. The fruit is elliptical in shape, the skin is yellow and looks like it is powdered, smaller than zhen 𣚛, and the fragrance is very strong.

Papaya is also called Mao, also called Iron Foot Plow. Fang and Sheng Lan said: When the papaya flowers are in bloom, there are snakes coiled around them. When the fruit falls, it is offered to the great bodhisattva and then they leave, so it is called the Guardian Holy Melon.

Xuanzhou is famous for producing papaya. Therefore, Qiu Jun's poem thanking for the gift of papaya has the sentence "The jade branches are sparse after frost and rain, except for Xuan City, there is nothing better." The ground is full of melon plants, and every time the fruit is formed, the good people carve paper flowers and stick them on the melon. The night dew and sunlight shine on them, and the flower patterns are vivid, named embroidered melon, also known as flower papaya. In the imperial era, it was often used as a tribute. In the past, Wang Yanzhang and Wang Fu were classmates in the Imperial College. Wang Fu was beautiful but empty, and Yanzhang called him flower papaya, which was a mockery.

Papaya can be planted or grafted, or pressed. Flowers bloom in late spring. If you transplant them, it is better to do it before and after the Autumn Festival. It is afraid of the sun and likes fertilizer, and if it is fertilized with dog dung, it will naturally flourish. The straight branches can be used as crutches. The elderly hold them, which is beneficial to the muscles and veins.

The method of storing papaya is to dry the papaya in the sun and put it in a sealed bottle, so that it can be fragrant for a long time without decay. Papaya tastes sour and astringent, but it can also be eaten. Miscellaneous Records of Emperor Ming: Empress Yuanxian thought of eating sour food, so Zhang Shuo offered a papaya in his sleeve. Cut the papaya raw and remove the skin, boil it thoroughly, change the water several times to soak it, so that the sour and astringent taste is removed, and then fry it with honey to make candied papaya. Also, papaya soaked in wine is also a good product.

If you roast the papaya into ash, the fish will die if they eat it. Abridged History of the Three Kingdoms: Qi Xiaozhao of the Northern Dynasty attacked Kumo Xi and reached Tianchi, using papaya ash to poison the fish.

Education News

National Vocational Education Conference Closed Yesterday

Three Plenary Sessions with a Total of Fourteen Resolutions

Promotion of Vocational Education and Students' Career Paths Were Discussed

Opening of the Third Plenary Session

(Nanjing, 9th) At 8:00 a.m. at the National Vocational Education Conference, He Qingru was invited to give a lecture on various scientific methods of vocational guidance. At 9:00 a.m., the Third Plenary Session continued to be held. Chairman Gu Shulin reported on the two proposals that had not been discussed at the Second Plenary Session, reviewed the results, and then submitted them for discussion.

Discussion of Various Proposals

(1) Regarding the Career Paths of Graduates

(Resolution) The methods are as follows: 1. This Association should suggest to the Ministry of Education to forward it to the National Government, ordering the National Economic Commission and the Ministry of Industry to pay attention to the local products of various provinces and cities and establish factories, farms, and ranches to enrich people's lives. 2. This Association should propose to the National Government to order the National Economic Commission, the Construction Commission, and the four ministries of Industry, Transportation, Education to jointly form a central vocational introduction agency, or this agency should be attached to the National Academic Work Advisory Office to jointly plan the career paths of vocational students. 3. This Association should propose to the National Government to order all public and private production agencies and administrative agencies related to production to give priority to employing vocational school graduates, especially paying attention to the production agencies in the northwestern provinces, and should give priority to allowing students from schools of the same nature to intern. 4. Consult with the Construction, Education, and Finance Bureaus of various provinces to jointly organize loan committees and vocational introduction agencies, and vocational education and production guidance should be carried out simultaneously. The original proposal is for reference for various provinces to organize this agency.

(2) Regarding the Vocational School Curriculum

(Resolution) 1. The industrial department should add a general overview of the industry and factory equipment. Adopt the opinions of the original proposal and pay attention to the third item of the general explanation of vocational education laws and regulations. 2. Please ask the Ministry of Education to collect the current textbooks of vocational schools across the country, and then entrust the Ministry to research vocational education institutions or experts to review and compile temporary textbooks and civic education textbooks for vocational schools. 3. Determine the teaching material outline for vocational subjects in private schools and labor schools, and submit it to the Ministry for reference. The remaining proposals were passed according to the review report.

(3) Regarding the Promotion of Vocational Supplementary Education

(Resolution) 1. The Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Industry should find ways to promote labor education laws and regulations, and order various provinces and cities to order local industrial and commercial groups to set up vocational supplementary education institutions within a time limit, so that apprentices in factories and shops can enroll in supplementary education. 2. Local educational administrative agencies should contact local industrial and commercial sectors to set up various vocational schools or supplementary schools within a time limit. 3. Local educational administrative agencies may contact local agricultural, industrial, and commercial sectors to organize a vocational supplementary education design committee. 4. Please ask the Ministry of Education to issue a notice to various provinces and cities, paying attention to running vocational supplementary schools under a portion of the social education funds.

(4) Vocational Guidance Should Be Strictly Implemented in Primary and Secondary Schools

(Resolution) 1. The personnel in charge of vocational guidance in primary and secondary schools in various provinces and cities should supervise the principals of primary and secondary schools throughout the province and city to strictly implement vocational guidance within one year before graduation. 2. The educational administrative agencies in various provinces should hire experts and leaders from various industries to organize a vocational guidance committee and advisory board. 3. Educational administrative agencies in various provinces and cities should hold regular vocational guidance regular seminars. 4. Local educational administrative agencies should conduct a survey of vocational conditions throughout the province and city, and publish a booklet on vocational classification and distribution to various schools. 5. Local educational administrative agencies should set up vocational guidance centers and vocational introduction centers in the shortest possible time. 6. For the above five items, please ask the Ministry of Education to issue a notice to the educational administrative agencies in various provinces and cities to strictly comply with it. 7. Please ask the Ministry of Education to set up a summer vocational guidance seminar to convene personnel in charge of vocational guidance in various provinces and cities to participate. The original proposal was passed as recorded.

(5) Temporary Proposal: Jiang Wenyu proposed to order the formulation of methods for vocational education and moral cultivation in primary schools.

(Resolution) This case is sent to the Ministry for reference. Please ask the Ministry of Education to formulate detailed methods separately and issue a notice for implementation.

Chairman's Final Report

At this point, all the proposals have been discussed. Finally, the chairman reported that this vocational education discussion meeting lasted for two and a half days. There were a total of nine proposals from the Ministry of Education and fifty-two proposals from representatives from various provinces and cities. As a result of the discussion, most of them were merged into the proposals from the Ministry of Education and discussed together. A total of fourteen proposals were resolved: 1. Vocational education administrative personnel, 2. Vocational education funding, 3. Vocational education laws and regulations, 4. Vocational education departments, 5. Inspection and reorganization of vocational schools, 6. Methods for awarding and subsidizing vocational schools, 7. Vocational school teachers and treatment, 8. Vocational supplementary education, 9. Vocational guidance, 10. Vocational subjects and internships, 11. Career paths for vocational school students, 12. Short-term vocational training classes, 13. Military training, 14. Vocational moral cultivation methods. The remaining six pieces were sent to the Ministry of Education for reference. This is the general situation of the results of the conference.

The Conference Closed at Noon

After the chairman finished the report, it was already twelve o'clock, and the meeting was adjourned immediately. After the representatives had lunch at the Ministry, they left Beijing separately in the afternoon.

He Qingru's Lecture Yesterday

Titled "Scientific Methods of Vocational Guidance"

At the conference on the 9th, He Qingru was invited to give a lecture on scientific methods of vocational guidance. The outline of his lecture is as follows:

1. The basis of vocational guidance, A. Research on people, B. Analysis of things, 2. Individual differences, A. Physiological differences, B. Intelligence differences, C. Mechanical ability differences, D. Social ability differences, E. Interest differences, F. Personality differences, G. Educational differences, H. Environmental differences, 3. Methods of studying individuals, A. Testing, (1) Types of tests, (2) Value of tests, B. Investigation, (1) Academic performance, (2) Conduct, (3) Physical condition, (4) Interests, (5) Family background, C. Face-to-face interview, (1) Importance of face-to-face interview, (2) Content of face-to-face interview, 1. Questions, 2. Personal situation, 3. Vocational status, 4. Disposal plan, (3) Personality observation, 4. Differences in affairs, A. Nature of work, B. Working environment, C. Work needs, D. Work treatment, 5. Methods of analyzing affairs, A. The Text of the Proposal Formally Announced at the First Plenary Session

The National Vocational Education Discussion Meeting was held at the first plenary session on the 7th. The proposals passed have been recorded in this newspaper. Now, the text of the proposal formally announced at the conference is recorded below for reference.

1. Regarding how to supervise the implementation of vocational education laws and regulations and what suggestions are there.

The Fujian Education Bureau proposed "Please order various provinces and cities to pay special attention to agricultural teaching and practice in rural areas and rural primary schools as a supplement to promoting agricultural education."

The Shanghai Education Bureau proposed, "It is proposed to reduce the burden on vocational school students and clearly stipulate the amount of fees paid by vocational school students."

The Anhui Education Bureau proposed, "The division of subjects in junior vocational schools should be as simple as possible in order to facilitate implementation and meet practical needs." The above three proposals were incorporated into this proposal for discussion.

Resolution: 1. It is hoped that various provinces and cities will supervise the implementation of the provisions on the establishment of departments, funding, equipment, and internships in vocational education laws and regulations.

2. If there are still vocational departments set up in existing middle schools, and if there is considerable equipment, teachers, and achievements, and it has been specially approved by the Ministry of Education, it can continue to exist and be regarded as a kind of experimental school. If the existing junior vocational schools are reorganized from junior high schools, and it is necessary to retain the junior high school class in fact, and it has been approved by the Ministry of Education, it may be temporarily allowed to set up a middle school class. As for the strengthening of agricultural subjects in rural normal schools and the increase of junior vocational schools, the education subjects are changed, and a small part of the curriculum should be accommodated.

3. The establishment of vocational schools should be based on a single subject. Departments of the same nature can set up more than two departments. If the school's economic, personnel, and equipment are all capable of setting up multiple departments, and it is necessary to set up them in fact, and it has been approved by the Ministry of Education, it can be established.

4. The fees paid by vocational school students should still be handled in accordance with the regulations. It is hoped that various provinces and cities will find ways to reward or subsidize private vocational schools with excellent results. Before private vocational schools receive public subsidies, and the fees paid by students exceed the number specified in the regulations, it may be accommodated after approval by the主管敎育行政機關 (zhǔ guǎn jiào yù xíng zhèng jī guān: responsible education administrative authority).

2. The case of short-term vocational training classes attached to senior vocational schools.

The Fujian Education Bureau proposed, "Please approve the establishment of special vocational courses attached to senior vocational schools in accordance with the methods of special normal courses attached to normal schools."

The Sichuan Education Bureau proposed, "Please ask the Ministry of Education to issue a notice to various provinces to set up agricultural instructor training classes as soon as possible to relieve rural areas and enrich production."

Representatives from Henan Province proposed, "Simple vocational schools should be established in the capital and various provinces and cities."

Representatives from Nanjing City proposed, "Vocational schools should be jointly run by junior and senior levels to suit the national conditions of our country, so as to enhance students' technical ability and forge them into sound vocational talents."

The above four proposals are attached to this proposal for discussion.

Resolution: 1. Various provinces and cities, depending on the needs of the local area, set up short-term vocational training classes attached to senior vocational schools for the sake of graduates' career paths. However, the agricultural and industrial departments should not be set up. For detailed methods, please ask the Ministry of Education to formulate and announce them separately.

2. The conference recommends that the Ministry of Education consult with various ministries and committees to order the agencies under the jurisdiction of various provinces and cities to consult with the local主管敎育行政機關 (zhǔ guǎn jiào yù xíng zhèng jī guān: responsible education administrative authority) when they need to run short-term training classes or seminars.

3. Various provinces and cities should consult with the local construction departments, finance departments, and other agencies before deciding to set up departments in vocational schools.

4. Industrial vocational schools should be jointly run by junior and senior levels.

The Locations of Two Vocational Schools in Anhui Have Been Found

Anqing Senior Sericulture School is Outside the East Gate

Huizhou Agriculture and Forestry School is in Jixi

(Anhui News) Anhui Province plans to increase the number of vocational schools immediately, one is Anqing Senior Sericulture Vocational School, and the other is Huizhou Agriculture and Forestry School. After many investigations and studies on the location of the two schools, the location of Anqing Senior Sericulture Vocational School has been decided to use an old agricultural school site outside the East Gate of Anqing. The original school buildings are dilapidated and unbearable. The school principal Wu Kuomin has taken over the repairs. The school can be opened and enrolled in the first and second months of next year. The Huizhou Agriculture and Forestry Vocational School was surveyed and determined to be at Konglin, Jixi by local gentry. A branch road will be divided from the Xiong Road Station of the Wu-Tun Road to facilitate transportation. The education department can raise 4,000 yuan for the construction cost of the school. The education department will bear two-thirds of the operating and regular expenses, and the remaining one-third will be raised locally.

Joint Exhibition of Children's Toys by Shanghai Branch of Scientific Games and Others

Solicitation of Items from Schools and Manufacturers Begins Today

Collection Point Temporarily at Wuben Girls' Middle School

The Shanghai branch of the China Scientific Games and the Shanghai branch of the China Cultural Construction Association, in order to use toys to guide children to explore scientific principles and increase scientific knowledge, are jointly holding a children's toy exhibition. The exhibition will rotate between Hangzhou, Shanghai, Tianjin, Nanjing, and other places. Letters have been sent to manufacturers, stores, and schools to solicit exhibits, and Wuben Girls' Middle School has been entrusted to collect and manage them. The deadline for submissions is the 20th of this month, and the exhibition will first be held in Hangzhou on New Year's Day next year, and then rotate between Shanghai, Nanjing, and other places. The following is a summary of the exhibition's regulations: (1) The purpose of this exhibition is to use toys to guide children to explore scientific principles, increase scientific knowledge, arouse curiosity, and stimulate their interest and desire to create and invent new things, in order to promote the progress of science in China. (2) Types of items solicited: A. Various children's toys; B. Portraits and short biographies of scientific inventors. (3) Places to solicit items: A. Schools; B. Toy stores; C. Toy manufacturers; D. Individuals with special toys. (4) The principles of manufacture of the exhibited toys should be briefly explained. (5) If the toys sent to the exhibition need to be returned, it should be stated before sending them. (6) The toys for the exhibition are entrusted to the Office of Wuben Girls' Middle School, Huangjia Que Road, Ximen, to collect.

Outline of Criminology by Xu Pengfei

Since its opening this spring, the University Bookstore has been thriving. Today, it is publishing the Outline of Criminology, which is still rare in our country's academic circles. It is the product of the dedicated teaching of Xu Pengfei, a Master of Laws from the University of Dijon in France and a graduate of Criminal Studies from the University of Barney, currently a professor at the Shanghai Law School and the College of Political Science. The entire book is exquisitely printed in 300 pages and is divided into four parts: Part 1: Introduction; Part 2: Etiology; Part 3: Impact Theory; Part 4: Remediation. Each part is further divided into chapters that provide detailed descriptions with clear organization and lively language. The systematization of the compilation and the practical application of the materials are the hallmarks of this book, making it suitable for use as a textbook and reference book for universities. It is also heard that the sales of the Outline of Labor Problems by Chen Zhenlu and the Original Theory of Public Finance by Yao Qingsan, which were also published by the bookstore, have been extremely strong this semester.

Unexpectedly, Youyou Lost to French Merchants

Inaccurate Shooting Leads to Adverse Consequences

Result: One to Two

Youyou, who once defeated French merchants with a score of five to three, unexpectedly lost to French merchants by a score of one to two yesterday. This was completely unexpected. Youyou was very promising in the Scottish Cup, but unexpectedly lost it yesterday, which is deeply regrettable.

Missed Opportunities Lead to Defeat

If one were to predict the outcome based on the situation of the day, one would have said that Youyou had a 60-70% chance of winning. Especially in the first half, for 45 minutes, Youyou's cavalry roamed around the enemy's goal for quite a while. However, because the shots were inaccurate, they often returned empty-handed despite having the mountain in sight. Fortunately, Sun Jinshun scored a goal in the 15th minute, allowing them to take the lead by one goal. In the second half, Youyou suffered misfortune from the start. The goal they conceded was almost inexplicable. Towards the end, when the game was about to end, Ma Shan'er, who had initially served as an inside defender and was later switched to left inside, deflected the ball into the net, which was especially saddening. It was a situation where victory was within reach, but they suffered defeat. This is a case of the one who could have won losing, and the one who could have lost winning.

Youyou Gains Possession Amidst Strong Momentum

Relying on a surge of energy, Youyou's five riders advanced together. The French merchants were not as strong as in the past, and did not have the imposing manner of rejecting people from a thousand miles away. In the blink of an eye, they passed three levels in a row, with the enemy's goal in sight. However, the shooting line was often blocked and forced to retreat. In the 15th minute, Sun Jinshun, Youyou's only accurate shooter, with the help of his teammates, avoided the opponent's obstruction and kicked the ball into the goal. Once the record was opened, the momentum became even stronger. However, there were still many opportunities lost, and the fault lies with Mei Hongbao. Youyou's failure to create a foundation for victory at that time was a foreshadowing of their later defeat. The first half ended with a score of one to zero in their favor.

Changing Strategy Leads to French Merchants' Victory

Youyou's misfortune seemed to come with the whistle that started the second half. Less than three minutes into the game, center Chen Zhenxiang suddenly touched the ball with his hand outside the penalty area, causing a great disaster. Remy was ordered to execute the penalty. In front of Youyou's goal, both sides, enemy and friend, monitored each other. The ball went towards the goal, and it is unknown who's back it hit, but it bounced into the net, creating a 1-1 tie. The French merchants, realizing that Youyou's attack was gradually weakening, suddenly changed their strategy, focusing on impact. Ma Shan'er had already switched positions with Da Wate, personally leading the three armies. As expected, in the last four minutes, Ma Shan'er fulfilled his wish and deflected the ball into the goal, and Youyou lost by a score of one to two. Their chances in the Scottish Cup ended from then on.

French Merchants

W. Wate, Ma Shan'er, Aigutuo, Ding Baosuotuo, Parker, Remy, Xiao Wate, Da Wate, R. Baosuotuo, Jiesu Fafanqie

Youyou

Tang Ji, Wang Shusen, Jiang Shan Jing, Liang Shutang, Chen Zhenxiang, Li Shengguan, Wang Nanzhen, Sun Jinshun, Luo Haiguang, Zhong Yongshen, Mei Hongbao

Teachers and Students of Zhirenyong Girls' Middle School Celebrate Volleyball Victory

Zhirenyong Girls' Middle School in West Shanghai defeated the Rose Team, which had attended the Far Eastern Games, the night before last, winning the Dahua Cup championship of the Middle School and Youth Volleyball Tournament, taking the lead in women's volleyball in the city. Everything has been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. It is heard that the school is scheduled to convene all teachers and students today to hold a celebration meeting. The principal and sports instructors will each give speeches to encourage the girls to pay attention to sports, and the volleyball team will be photographed to commemorate the occasion permanently. Classes will be suspended this afternoon from 12:30 PM to 6:00 PM, and a dinner will be held for teachers and students at the Hangzhou Restaurant on Edward Road. It is expected that there will be a lively scene at that time.

Jianmei Basketball Team Won Against Post Office Workers Yesterday

Score Close: 32 to 27

The Jianmei Sports Association of this city, at the invitation of the Sports Section of the Shanghai Postal Workers' Union, held a friendly basketball match at the City First Sports Field at 10:00 AM yesterday, officiated by referee Hua Yulin. Jianmei had Xue Jianqiu, Cui Xilin, Qin Jiapeng, Zhao Qingxiang, and other generals, and their skills were quite commendable. They took the lead all the way, seemingly effortlessly. The Post Office Workers team, led by Ma Zelong, Sun Shouqi, Zheng Qilong, Tang Daren, Zhang Youhua, and Pu Cunhong, took turns on the field. Although their coordination was commendable yesterday, they were unable to catch up and lost 32-27. However, the score was still close.
