Free Talk

"Of all things useless, a scholar is the most"

— Cao Juren

Huang Zhongze, a poet from Changzhou, had two lines of poetry expressing his complaints: "Nine out of ten people deserve scorn, of all things useless, a scholar is the most." The latter sentence may carry a hint of humility amidst the complaints, but the uselessness of scholars is true. Emperor Xuan of Han used legalist officials, and the Crown Prince (Emperor Yuan) said that the punishments were too severe and that Confucian scholars should be used. Emperor Xuan was displeased and said, "The Han family has its own system, originally combining the ways of the hegemon and the king. How can we rely solely on moral teachings and have the governance of the Zhou dynasty? Moreover, vulgar scholars do not understand the times, they like the old and dislike the new, confusing people with names and realities, not knowing what to adhere to, how can they be entrusted with responsibilities?" It is said that the emperors of the Han dynasty respected Confucianism, but look at what kind of useless things scholars were in their eyes!

At the same time, in another kind of community, scholars were also looked down upon. In the 71st chapter of Water Margin, after setting up new banners and assigning duties on Liangshan Marsh, there is a passage that describes the advantages of Liangshan Marsh:

"The eight directions share a city, different surnames are one family. Heaven and earth reveal the essence of the stellar fiends, the human realm combines the beauty of heroes. Thousands of miles away, they see each other morning and evening, a single heart shares life and death. Appearances and languages, north and south, east and west, though different; feelings, livers, and gallbladders, loyalty, sincerity, and righteousness are the same. Among them are imperial descendants, wealthy officials and generals, and people from all three teachings and nine streams, even hunters, fishermen, butchers, and executioners, all call each other brothers, without distinction between noble and base; and there are also siblings, married couples, uncles, nephews, in-laws, and followers, even enemies, all enjoy wine and feasts together, without regard to kinship. Whether clever or crude, rustic or romantic, they do not hinder each other, indeed sharing the same understanding; whether with pen and tongue, or knives and spears, or running and stealing, each has their own strengths, truly employing talents according to their abilities. What is hateful is the fake writing, reluctantly keeping a 'sacred-handed scholar' to preserve elegance; what is most annoying is the big turban, fortunately killing the 'white-robed scholar' first, washing away the sour stinginess. The area is four or five hundred miles, with one hundred and eight heroes; in the past, it was often said that the name was heard on the rivers and lakes, like the sound of an ancient tower bell spreading; today we know that surnames are listed among the stars, like beads on a rosary, each linked together. Chao Gai was afraid of daring to proclaim himself king, and returned to heaven early; only Song Jiang was willing to call on the crowd to protect righteousness, taking the stronghold as his head. Let's not talk about gathering in the mountains and forests, but wish to look up to the corridors and temples."

— Page 57 of chapter 71 of the 120-chapter version. The author of Water Margin was so at odds with scholars that he actually said: "What is hateful is the fake writing, reluctantly keeping a 'sacred-handed scholar' to preserve elegance; what is most annoying is the big turban, fortunately killing the 'white-robed scholar' first, washing away the sour stinginess." At first glance, one is quite indignant; but upon reflection, it is also the truth; in the eyes of the heroes of the rivers and lakes, the chivalrous men in the green forests, who puts scholars in their eyes!

Therefore, I picked up Wu Jingzi's The Scholars again and looked through it carefully; it is a book that most sincerely depicts the decline of scholars. If we link The Scholars with Water Margin, these two worlds have such an insurmountable wall! For example, Pan Sanye in The Scholars is not a particularly lovable or respectable character; but compared to Kuang Chaoren, he seems very great. When Kuang Chaoren was wandering in a foreign land with nowhere to return, Pan San did indeed make some money in the tricks of soliciting lawsuits, abducting women, and impersonating examinees, and even completed his marriage. When Kuang Chaoren passed the exam and became a tutor and son-in-law in the mansion of Li Gejian, Pan San hoped that he could help him out in prison; but Kuang Chaoren said with a stern face, "... I should have gone to see him in prison, but I am not like when I was a student; since I am doing things for the imperial court, I must abide by the court's rewards and punishments; if I go to such a place to see people, then the rewards and punishments will be unclear. ... What Pan Sange has done is what I would arrest him for if I were a local official; now I am going to see him in prison, am I saying that the court's punishment of him is wrong? This is not the way to be a subject." When we read Kuang Chaoren's corrupt words, it really gives us a headache. The most poignant thing in The Scholars is the old Mr. Ni who repairs musical instruments. He raised six sons, one died, and four were sold. He was even preparing to sell the youngest one. He complained to the actor Bao Wenqing, "... It's hard to tell you about the time! I entered school at the age of twenty, and now I have been a scholar for thirty-seven years. It's all because I read these dead books, unable to take light things and unable to bear heavy things; I become poorer day by day, and I have many children, so I have to make a living by this skill, which is a helpless thing. - To tell you the truth, I have six sons, one died, and now I only have the sixth youngest son at home; those four sons were all sold to other states and prefectures because there was nothing to eat! ... This youngest one will not be able to stay in the future, and will also be sold to others!" Only this kind of useless thing can create such a weak life. A young Russian woman, after reading Chekhov's novels, couldn't help but cry. She said: Are all these bleak lives and weak souls in Russia? The characters in The Scholars also make us feel this way. Wu Jingzi mentioned four ideal characters at the end of The Scholars: one who can write, one who sells firecracker tubes, one who runs a teahouse, and one who is a tailor; the tailor is the most perfect. He uses Jing Yuan's mouth to express his ideal proposition:

"I don't want to be a refined person, but I often study because my temperament is similar. As for our humble profession, it was left by my grandfather, does reading and writing and being a tailor become tainted? Moreover, those friends in the schools have different opinions, how can they associate with us? Now I earn six or seven cents of silver every day, eat my fill, and can play the zither and write, everything is up to me; I don't covet people's wealth, and I don't serve people's faces, heaven doesn't collect, and the earth doesn't care, isn't that happy?"

But this ideal character is still reclusive and fragile, only worthy of wearing a painted face and performing comedies. On Liangshan, at most it is just "reluctantly" and "to preserve elegance."

In Turgenev's famous work Rudin, Rudin leaves Natalia and leaves a self-blaming letter, saying: "My talent does not seem to be too thin, but my ability is insufficient, so I cannot achieve anything. Even if there is talent, it is useless, even if you sow seeds, there is no guarantee that there will be results. In me, there is no ability to move people, especially no ability to attract women. Relying on a little wisdom alone is useless. I want to stand up and do things enthusiastically, but in fact I cannot realize it at all; my destiny is truly pitiful and ridiculous!" Alas: "Of all things useless, a scholar is the most!"

Calculation

The Red Light in Tangsang Cave

— Shao Guanhua

Rain threads entwine mountain shadows,

Mountain shadows add to the grayness,

Mountain winds cut off sorrow,

Red lights blow up a smiling face.

Travelers feel joy, happiness;

However, the season has reached autumn,

Bearing fatigue, when

A wave of cold air throws up peach blossoms.

Vera

— Feier

Behind a row of old wooden houses arranged in a line, a long row of towering coconut trees cast shadows, making the houses unusually dark even during the day. In front is a flat dirt road. In dry weather, dust constantly rises; and in rainy weather, the mud sucks at people's footsteps.

Vera, this primitive village market, is connected to the Vera wilderness area in the back and lies horizontally in front of the Vera estuary. In the equatorial night world, gales carrying torrential rain constantly shake between the forests behind the houses, causing wild birds and beasts to wail and roar, and the wooden houses shake like an earthquake. During the daytime under the scorching sun, the Vera estuary constantly rises and falls with the tide, and the river rolls with the sound of the tide. Occasionally one or two small steamers pass through the river, the sound of the engines echoes on the riverbank, or the message of the arrival and departure of the steamer comes from the opposite side of Banian Port, the rest of the time Vera quietly lies in the silent breath of the countryside.

On this monotonous dirt road, Chinese people sit in small shops half-dozing doing business, Malays are gambling and chatting, children are playing foreign games, and workers are sunning "copra" all day long.

In front of the road, near the river bank, is a dirt square. Chinese people use bamboo woven things to buy coconuts from the hands of Malays, shell them and take the meat, and spread the coconut meat piece by piece on this place, ready to be dried into "copra". When the weather is good, Chinese workers squat on the square in the morning, patiently spreading the coconut meat in one or two hours. Under the scorching sun, when the tide rises, the riverbank echoes with the sound of Chinese and Malay natives calculating the number of coconuts, the sound of axes hitting coconuts, and the sound of hard objects shattering vibrates in the air.

The workers silently sweat working under a piece of leaves.

"Damn!" The worker uses a sharp digger to dig up the flesh in the shell. If he is careless, the digger hits his hand, and a small piece of flesh and a pile of blood fall from his hand, so the curse comes.

However, after the curse, he wraps a cloth around his hand, picks up the digger and continues to work.

What should be cursed most is rainy days. At that time, a black cloud flies over the sky, and the workers on the square are in turmoil, busy packing up their work. The "atta" leaves just cover the coconut meat, and their bodies have been soaked like they just came out of the river. Only when the coconut meat is dried into "dry" and loaded by the Royal Dutch Steamship Company, the work is considered to have been harvested, but at the same time other work products are piled up again. - Chinese people are always like this to make a small profit.

However, Vera suffocated in the price drop of "copra". The bosses shook their heads and sighed, but the workers were in the tide of unemployment, packing their bags under the wooden sticks of the police to return home. The Guangzhou craftsmen in the gold shops had already put away the shrines and incense burners written with red paper in front of the shops, and my Hehe Liang had to drop out of school and move with his gold-making father. Vera was locked in rows of shops, and the rats took the opportunity to breed and make noise in the houses.

As early as forty years ago, Vera was the location of the "palace" of the Vera chief and also the anchorage of ships. When the price of rubber rose, Banian Port, the estuary of the Banian River basin, which was rich in rubber, was established, so the ships changed their anchoring place, and the Vera king was forced to relocate. Today, the price of rubber has plummeted, and Banian and Vera are listlessly facing each other across the river, shrinking their hands in the recession.

No time is the rise and fall of the economy as fast as Nanyang, and no place is the rise and fall as unexpected as Vera. Vera, this quiet coast of the South China Sea, is a representative of a special example of the change in a deformed economic geography.

The last time I passed Vera, I saw that Vera City was about to die under the scorching sun. When I thought of He Liang leaving this birth place and crying to me in a foreign land, I felt a faint nostalgia for this gray old village city and a pathetic indignation towards the laborious and bleeding workers as if fighting against this world.

A Process in My Creation

— Li Huiying

Counting from the beginning of writing novels, it has been five or six years.

In the past, I was fascinated by the idea that "literary works are for people to pass the time," so what I wrote always revolved around fine wine, women - in a word, "enjoyment." However, immediately following the "September 18th" Incident, the Japanese imperialist army trampled on my hometown, and the artillery fire of the Japanese imperialists in the "January 28th" Shanghai War destroyed the school I was studying in. This not only forced me to remotely receive the title of a slave of a lost province, but also lost my place to study and live in Shanghai. I was wandering, I was panicking, I was sad, I was angry, and finally, it aroused my emotions of resisting violence! "Wake up, can't you change the direction of your writing?" I woke up, I woke myself up from a drowsy dream and asked myself. "You should turn that kind of writing about leisure and elegance into a weapon to resist your enemies! For example: exposing the oppression, slaughter, and deception of our small nations by Japanese imperialism in the Northeast. At the same time, you should also grasp a certain point or level of the current society and say something that should be said."

Harvest Year - the three novels in this collection are the harvest after I woke up from my dream. They were written after I returned to the Northeast from Shanghai in September 1933 and returned to Shanghai in September, and were published successively in "New China" in 1934. The reason why I wanted to return to the Northeast was very simple, I just wanted to see if the ruined mountains and rivers of my hometown and the suffering of my compatriots under the iron hoofs of imperialism were the same as what we had heard in Shanghai. The facts later proved to me that they were different! Therefore, if there is anything commendable in the three pieces of things in this collection, the most important thing is their "truth." This is also the main theme of the content of the article.

Secondly, regarding the writing aspect, I was careful from the beginning, guarding against writing things that people could not understand. Because I myself am a victim of literary works of the kind that are deeply affected by the awkwardness of writing.

Saying that this is a preface is better than saying that it is a process in my creation over the years, but without this process, how can this collection be written. Then, this may not be a waste of words.

Tomorrow (12)

— (Joseph Conrad) translated by Wu Xiangyu

She exclaimed suddenly: "It's you! You yourself he's waiting for. It's you who's coming tomorrow."

He murmured. "Oh! It's me?" Completely stunned, they both seemed to stop breathing. Clearly he was pondering what he heard; then, though without anger, but very puzzled, he said: "I don't understand. I haven't written any letters or anything, it was my companion, he saw the newspaper, told me—just this morning ... oh, what else?"

He inclined his ear to her; she whispered quickly to him, he listened for a while, murmuring "yes," sometimes saying "I know," at last he asked "but why not today?"

"You don't understand me!" she said impatiently. The line of light in the west beneath the clouds was vanishing. He bent himself a little more forward to hear clearly, the darkening night covering up all of the whispering woman and the attentive man, except their faces brought intimately close, with an air of secret and tenderness.

He shrugged his shoulders; the black shadow of a broad-brimmed hat sat picturesquely on his head. "These are so unpleasant, oh?" he complained to her. "Tomorrow?" Igh! igh! never heard such a thing spoken of. Why, all, so far as I can know, is tomorrow, and nothing has to do with today."

She still remained motionless, and did not speak a word.

"You perhaps encourage such ridiculous notions," he said.

"I have never gone against him."

"Why do you not?"

"Why should I?" she defended himself. "It would but make him unhappy. He perhaps would become out of his mind."

"Out of his mind!" he murmured, and heard a little nervous laugh from her.

"Where is the hurt done? Is it that I had a quarrel with the old fellow formerly? This I can easily believe to half extent."

"Oi, oi," he thought intelligently, "I fancy the old chap does deal always in his eloquent words with you. You are a good-hearted person."

Her two hands moved upward helplessly in the darkness. "That is perhaps all true. That is already true. That is already come. It is here. It is, we have been waiting for it, the tomorrow."

Correction: The article "On the Dian-Yue Road" published by this journal the day before yesterday has been completed. The "上" character in the title was mistakenly added with (), which may lead readers to believe that it has not been completed. This is a special correction, and readers are requested to pay attention.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Small Talk

The Morbidity of Society

— Home For

No one would deny it, right? In the historical process of continuous human evolution, various social organizations are produced. This is precisely because of the objective material and economic relations that affect and dominate, and present different social forms.

Take the law as an example: it is precisely one of the life forms in every society. Indeed, its purpose is to protect human beings, but it is created by human beings themselves; at the same time, it must vary with each different social and economic organization. However, if you violate or destroy the laws of the then-existing society, that is "committing a crime" and must be judged by the court.

However, the occurrence of various "criminal" events can essentially reflect the general form of social organization at that time.

Here, we must be convinced: the giant wheel of the times has turned to the teeth of this 20th century, and everything is unprecedented progress. However, we cannot fail to see that even in today's "civilized countries," the increasing complexity and surge of various "criminal" cases has become one of the serious morbidities in society, which is worrying and distressing many "sociologists" and even those specialized "criminologists."

As for Shanghai, which is known as the "New York of the East"—its appearance is so solemn and magnificent! Its progress is so rapid (!)—it is indeed worthy of our ordinary people's praise and nostalgia, right? However, it cannot be an exception, regardless of elegance or vulgarity. According to the recently published "October Crime Statistics" of the Public Concession's Bureau of Works, it is disappointing and alarming enough.

Look: the statistics of "criminal cases" in the Public Concession in October alone amounted to as many as 1,399 cases, an increase of 149 cases compared to September. Compared with the same period last year, there was a sudden increase of 204 cases. Among these cases, there were 877 theft cases, an increase of 176 cases compared to September. Compared with the same period last year, there was an increase of 171 cases. There has also been a sharp increase in various other cases.

Here, it is also reminiscent of a terrible thing: that is, the university student who graduated from XX University actually went to do that kind of sneaky, "shameless" business. But after all, "the law" is inescapable, "sentenced to four months in prison as a warning" (see the newspapers of November 21).

This time, the issue of the university student's crime has indeed attracted the attention of the general public in society, and various opinions have been expressed and the rights and wrongs have been examined.

However, it is a fact that students from prestigious universities have committed crimes by stealing. To put it more precisely: that is precisely a more powerful reflection of our general way of life today, and a more serious and concrete manifestation of the morbidity in this society!

Originally, the causes of various human criminal problems are very complex and detailed. If classified by those "criminology experts," there are objective, subjective, congenital, instinctive, accidental, professional, and so on. However, we can all see that in today's situation of "market depression" and "rural bankruptcy," coupled with unprecedented natural disasters and man-made calamities... then, the increasing surge of criminal cases and the increasing seriousness of social morbidity will never be so accidental and simple. It should be known that every social problem must first be affected and dominated by its objective material and economic relations! Nothing can be an exception!

Page 20

Anti-"Anti-Flattery"

— Ma

"Anti-Flattery" are those who oppose "flattery," and Anti-"Anti-Flattery" are those who oppose "Anti-Flattery," and thus write about Anti-"Anti-Flattery." The other day I read Mr. Pi's article "Anti-Flattery" in Tan Yan, which on the surface seems agreeable, but in fact I strongly oppose it. This is because those who are good at "flattering" must be more agreeable and useful than those who are not good at "flattering." This is because those who are good at "flattering" can "anticipate the will," "report information," "shrug and smile flatteringly," and "pretend to be diligent," making it easy to win the master's favor. Therefore, as the saying goes, "a thousand wears and ten thousand wears, flattery never wears out." There is great truth in this.

Tang Wusansi often said, "I don't know what the world calls good people or bad people, but those who are good to me are good people, and those who are bad to me are bad people." These words are very straightforward, very easy to listen to, and very reasonable. Unfortunately, I don't have the qualifications to be a master, but if I did, I would be determined to use such people, because I hate strong-headed people who don't listen to gossip as soon as I see them. Therefore, "hawks and hounds," "slanderers," "claws and teeth," and "petty people" are the most necessary figures for the master's heart and soul.

Flattery is not only popular now, but also a very important historical trace in history. Let me give a few examples from history! There are many such historical traces in history, and I will give a few prominent examples:

During the Han Dynasty, the capital city asked Ping'en Marquis Xu Bo to enter the mansion, and when the wine was at its peak and the music was playing, Tan Changqing, the Shaofu of Changxin, got up and danced, performing a monkey fighting with a dog, which made everyone laugh.

During the Tang Dynasty, Lu Juan was a slave in the treasury, and when they gathered, they all held spittoons. Only Ku Rongguan spat into Juan's mouth, and he swallowed it all, saying, "I wish that the wisdom and fortune of the Lord would all enter my belly."

When Yang Zaisi was prime minister, he specialized in flattery to please the emperor. Zhang Tongxiu, the brother of Zhang Zhizhi, the Shaoqing of the ceremonial department, once teased Zaisi at a banquet, saying, "Yang Neishi's face looks like a Korean." Zaisi was delighted, cut paper and attached a turban, turned his purple robe backwards, and performed a Korean dance, which made everyone laugh.

When Duke Wei of Tang was ill, an official who was always flattering him came to the mansion to inquire about his health. He saw a chamber pot in front of the bed, picked it up and drank it. Duke Wei frowned and said, "Why do you do this?" He replied, "If the excrement is sweet, the disease is difficult to cure. Your excrement is not sweet, so it is easy to cure."

During the Song Dynasty, Han Tuozhou once toured the South Garden with a group of guests, passed by a mountain village, and wished for bamboo fences and thatched huts, saying, "This is truly the atmosphere of the countryside, but it lacks the crowing of chickens and the barking of dogs." Suddenly, he heard a dog barking in the thicket, and when he looked, it was Shi Duo. Tuozhou laughed loudly.

During the Song Dynasty, when Qin Hui was in power, Wang Lun presented a chamber pot made of seven treasures, engraved his name on the side, and wrote on the note, "Wang Lun respectfully presents this. In the past, the Han Emperor never forgot Ju Lu under every meal. I follow this intention and respectfully present a chamber pot, also wanting you to not forget it at all times."

During the Ming Dynasty, when the eunuch Wang Zhen was in power, Wang You, the right vice minister of the Ministry of Works, was beautiful and beardless, and was good at observing Zhen's expression. One day, Wang Zhen asked, "Why does Minister Wang have no beard?" He replied, "How dare the son have what the master does not have."

After Yan Song was stripped of his office during the Ming Dynasty, his family was confiscated, and a white jade chamber pot was found, which was very exquisite. A gold medal was attached to the top, with the inscription "Zhao Wenhua respectfully presents." Later, Wenhua was impeached, and Wenhua said, "He wants to slander me, so he attached a gold medal to it." His flattery and cunning were like this.

The above are all historical traces of "flattery." No matter who you are, if you encounter characters like Tan Changqing, Yang Zaisi, Zhao Shiduo, Wang Lun, and Zhao Wenhua, and their "flattery" is applied completely, I ask you, is it comforting or not, is it pleasant or not? Therefore, I firmly and greatly oppose Mr. Pi's article on "flattery." This is because Mr. Pi may not have thought about the master at all? As for the intention of "flattery," I do not know, and should ask a few good flatterers.

Sympathizer

— Snow

White Face

— Rui

In the jail, the whole day is filled with dullness in the dark atmosphere. More than a dozen people all feel suffocated and hope to run to the open space outside to take a breath of fresh air. Although the air in that open space may not be that good, it is filled with black coal smoke everywhere. However, to the people in the jail, the air there is simply better than the seaside in the morning. It is more joyful than being an immortal to be able to take a deep breath there.

Old Zhou, the big guy with the strange beard covering his lower cheeks, was the last one to come to this jail. But because he has too much beard, in just a few days, he has become more fierce than those who have lived here for more than ten days. He really looks like a prisoner. Because he is new here, the dark world and the dull air here simply suffocate him. All day long, he walks by the iron fence that is less than a丈 wide, like an old tiger that is accustomed to running in the deep mountains and is trapped in an iron cage for the first time. He sighs uncomfortably, frowning and not saying a word.

Today, the weather is a little warmer. Everyone got up early in the morning, and everyone rushed to the iron fence, reaching out to the bucket to fetch towels to wash their faces. Old Zhou got up a little late, and there was only half a bucket of water left in the bucket, and it had all turned black. He had no choice but to hold his towel and curse in a low voice:

"Damn, is this still water for washing your face? It's simply sewage from the gutter!"

"Sewage, isn't it good? This is still considered preferential treatment! Otherwise, there wouldn't even be this bit of sewage. Not to mention anything else, look at the more than a hundred people across the way! Aren't they still using the same bucket?"

Everyone in the jail knew that Old Tang liked to talk. Although he was already in his forties, he didn't feel anything because he was used to this kind of life. Every day, he just played around, told jokes, and talked happily. He was the only one doing it, as if he was the oldest person outside, but the youngest child when he came here. At this time, he looked at Old Zhou's situation and knew that he was feeling sad again, so he chimed in and said a few words.

Actually, he can't be blamed. People like Old Zhou, although they are already twenty-five or six years old this year, have never suffered a bit. They don't read much, and they always stay at home every day, playing with their big and small wives. He never dreamed that there would be such a place in the world, or that there would be people living this kind of life. Even for himself, he never dreamed that there would be a day when he would live in this kind of place. This time, entering this iron cage, he felt very strange, as if he was dreaming.

Today, the north wind is blowing very fiercely. In the iron cage, it is icy cold and there is not a bit of heat. More than a dozen people

Page 21

are huddled together in a circle in the corner, with their heads tucked in. They can't see the morning sun. Only the biting cold wind blows on their faces, piercing the flesh inside their thin clothes. Their hands and feet are as cold as ice.

Tired, spiritless eyes are rolling in the dark corner, especially Old Zhou's big eyes, which are constantly rolling up and down.

"Hey! We are really too stupid. Look, isn't the sunlight shining into this cage? Let's go stand in the sunlight and see who is whiter.

It was about nine o'clock, and a ray of red sunlight was shining through the skylight. Although it was separated by a layer of iron bars, it seemed particularly bright in this dark jail. Old Tang seemed to have discovered something and became happy, calling everyone to stand in the sunlight and look at their bloodless faces.

More than a dozen people locked in the jail have not seen sunlight for ten or twenty days. Today, everyone is excited that the sunlight is shining into the cage, and everyone is standing in the sunlight to shine on themselves. However, the white faces that were not discovered in the darkness are now even paler in the sunlight.

Originally, everyone was happy, but now, everyone's brows are furrowed. Everyone is worried that their blood will dry up day by day, and when they leave the cage, they may not even have a trace of color left, leaving only a white face and a corpse-like body.

Talk about Renting a House

— Song Yuan

Once you arrive in this metropolis of the Orient - Shanghai, you think that there are new houses everywhere, and there are houses for rent in every alley. It doesn't matter, as long as there are enough banknotes in your wallet. In fact, finding a house is enough to make you angry. In other words, the problem of housing in the city is not so easy to solve.

Are you alone? A bachelor, that's even more troublesome. When you have chosen a clean and quiet alley, how comfortable it would be to live here, then you must be determined to rent a house here. However, the cleaner and quieter the alley, the more difficult it is to rent a house. When you look for red paper with black characters for rent everywhere, you will definitely be surprised; why are there no houses for rent here? If you are lucky enough to find a piece of paper for rent, knock on the door according to the address. The grandmothers and wives inside will lead you upstairs to see the house. The house has good light and air and is very clean. You will definitely be satisfied and want to talk to them about the rent. However, the first thing they ask you is, "Are you alone, or do you have a wife with you?" You will be stunned. You want to say "I am alone," then she sees you standing there stunned, and she will say to you first, "We don't rent to people without family members." She will also explain the reason, "There are many bad people in Shanghai..." putting you bachelor as a bad person and sending you out the back door. If you are lucky enough to find a house that says "Those with family members don't ask," it is some kind of club. You must think that you have found a house this time, and not having a wife is not a problem, but they want you to have a reliable shopkeeper to guarantee that you are a good person, not a bad person. If you can't find a reliable shopkeeper in Shanghai, then you have to admit that you are not a good person and don't fit in with what they are talking about.

You have hardened your heart about the houses in clean alleys, and you don't want to patronize them, then it will be easier to succeed. The easiest alleys to rent in are those where there are peddlers hawking, and it seems that the landlords are competing to pull in tenants. As soon as you enter the door, as long as the price is right, they are warm and kind, and even the children will call you uncle. However, as soon as you move your luggage and furniture in, the trouble will immediately come to you. Before your bed and table are arranged to your satisfaction, the landlady will immediately come to knock on the door. She is not here to congratulate you on your new home, but to ask you for rent with a smiling face. "There is a rule for renting a house in Shanghai, pay first and then live." If you want to discuss it with her, pay half of the rent first, it is best not to open your mouth, she will definitely not agree. Moreover, she thinks you are a fool who doesn't understand the rules of Shanghai, and she tells you a lot of things about renting a house, as if there have been regulations set long ago, and you don't even know these regulations. If you don't show that you are an old Shanghai person and know the old rules of renting a house, then her renting regulations will immediately change, and according to the rules, tenants should give notice ten days before leaving the house, and landlords should give tenants half a month's notice. She sees that you are an amateur, and she first takes care of you and says, "If you want to move out, you should give notice a month in advance." If you know the rules and argue with her, she will at most give in to half a month in advance, and in the end, she will sell you a favor and say, "Ten days is fine too. It's good for everyone to live here, it's better not to move." After you pay the rent first, she will also tell you, "Our lights are on until twelve o'clock at night, and the main door will be locked." She is not asking for your agreement, she is just notifying you. Also! As if she cares about your business very much, she calls you to go to the Public Security Bureau to report and register immediately, or you will be fined if you are a day late. If you don't understand these rules, or don't believe that there is such a thing, then she will first urge you with a lot of nice words, and later even get angry at you. "If you don't register, the Bureau will fine the landlord, I can't afford it!"

It's really troublesome to rent a house in Shanghai. Believe it or not, it's up to you.

Opening "Bao Yu Visits Xiaoxiang Pavilion at Night"

Severe winter frost forms ice. Moonlight hazy, about to fade. Gusts of north wind penetrate the bones. The Grand View Garden is desolate and deserted. Jia Baoyu walks along the flower street. Footsteps gently and slowly move. He is a lamp. A person. Dark shadows looming, even more melancholy. Alone to Xiaoxiang Pavilion. To see if Sister Lin's illness has lessened. Gently knocking on the copper ring, a rattling sound. Ziyun the maid is busy opening the door. Saying, Second Master, you should be careful in the cold late at night. Sister, I am worried about your girl Lin. Especially came to ask if you are well. Arrived at the right of the sickbed. Only to see her breathing weakly and without a sound. One called Sister Lin. One called Cousin. Her almond eyes slightly opened, tears streaming down. Saying, Brother, my Second Sister-in-law should not treat me like this. Although the Old Ancestor loves me dearly. But alas, she is deaf and blind and not sensitive. My illness cannot be cured. And I cannot ask for leave every day to ask for peace. Brother, my debts from the previous life with you are paid off in this life. Please, noble son, do not care about this ill-fated person. Sister, your life is always full of worries. Why do you think so little of yourself? Think of anything you want to say. You and I are of one mind. I advise you to eat three meals a day. I advise you to add more clothes and be careful. I advise you to take care of yourself by first taking care of your heart. Why bother looking for troubles yourself? I advise you not to listen to the words of the sisters. They are like false and like true. I advise you to rest early and not stay up late. It is not good to grind on till dusk when you are sick. I advise you to put aside all your worries. And don't think about the old Su Zhou wall door. Daiyu nodded secretly. Brother's words I keep in my heart. The heart turns dark. Even more sad. The nemesis is most caring for me. Tears cannot stop flowing. Saturating the fragrant silk scarf. This life may not be too drifting.

National Studies

Ms. Wang Bingmei's Tang Poetry

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Ode to Peonies by Ms. Wang Bingmei

Beside the Peony Pavilion, brocade clouds piled high, peony blossoms set off by verdant moss.

Flowers bloom like brocade, their beauty radiant, a woman leans on carved railings, smiling openly.

The spring light is bright, the spring breeze fragrant, cherishing spring, yet there's the sorrow of Du Wei Niang.

The days are long, with nothing to do but watch the flowers, tiny golden lotuses tap along the corridor.

Murmuring, a pair of swallows, once acquainted, bees and butterflies flutter, vying for the wind.

The fragrance of clothes and flowers intermingle, dark, shiny hair brushes against the clouds.

A celestial maiden scattering flowers, her spirit dancing, her clothes woven with brocade, an embroidered skirt.

The embroidered skirt and silk stockings, a new outfit, a slender waist and snow-white neck, naturally perfect.

Like a flower, like jade, also like a fairy, loving flowers as if her life depended on it, burning candles high.

Instructing the maidservants to carefully protect them, cherishing the flowers, rising early and sleeping late.

Jade branches and jade leaves, covered in golden gauze, light clouds and gentle breezes beside Phoenix Pond.

Wishing the flowers always beautiful, the moon always full, wishing my beauty rivals the flowers.

Wealth and elegance surpassing all others, verdant youth that never changes.

Letters to the Editor

To the esteemed editor, In the Wireless Radio column of the News Evening Post on the 4th of this month, a letter clarifying matters was published by Wu Huilin, Dong Ruiqing, Ji Shiying, Li Dongliang, Mi Mian, Gao Xinzhi, and other gentlemen. After reading it, I was extremely shocked. The Shanghai Feige Society is solely organized and managed by Shou Xun personally, as has been proven by lawyers Wang Yintai and Zheng Wenkai. When Feige Society previously broadcasted singing on radio stations such as Central-West, Fuxinghua, Huamei, and China, Wu Huilin and the others were all employees hired by Shou Xun. Furthermore, Wu and the others have now formed the Xingguang Society, naturally severing all ties with our Feige Society. Now, Shou Xun is also engaged in other occupations, and the broadcasting work of the Feige Society has been temporarily suspended. Apart from Shou Xun personally and Ms. Cang Yinqiu, who are currently collaborating with the Shanghai Wireless Drama Society, there are no other radio broadcasts. Therefore, henceforth, no matter who uses the name of Feige Society to make contact for any matters, it has nothing to do with Shou Xun. For this reason, I am taking advantage of a corner of your esteemed publication to issue a solemn statement. This is to the Radio Editorial Department of Shen Bao. Respectfully submitted, Wang Shou Xun of Shanghai Feige Society (Seal) December 9th

Shen Bao Local Supplement　Movie Special

Carole Lombard's Peculiar Sense of Humor

— Li Bin

The life of Hollywood's beautiful star Carole Lombard is simply a continuous stream of jokes. She was practically born to laugh. Her abundant sense of humor finds its only outlet in teasing people or playing pranks. As the ancients said, "Why not engage in some frivolous activities to spend one's limited life?" Lombard deeply understands this principle. Her daily life and that of her friends are almost entirely devoted to finding jokes and having a good time. As the old saying goes, "Birds of a feather flock together; those of the same mind resonate with each other." Since Carole Lombard is like this, the group of friends who gather around her are naturally of the same kind. If you can't stand her jokes, you simply shouldn't befriend her. If you are too sensitive and can't withstand her teasing, you shouldn't even see her. But if you have a sense of humor equal to hers, then you will find her endlessly amusing and full of laughter.

For example, which Hollywood star would be willing to have someone burst into laughter during the most romantic scene, or have everyone remain silent while watching their comedy, or have several friends laugh and walk away when they are singing their best? The above is what happened to the famous singer Bing Crosby himself. It was at a theater on Catalina Island, during the screening of Bing Crosby's latest musical film, that Carole Lombard suddenly led a group of friends in. She said she was there to congratulate Bing Crosby on his success, but her method of congratulation was too peculiar. But Bing Crosby is also a great guy with a sense of humor no less abundant than Carole's. He knew Carole was there to make fun of him, so when she led a group of friends out with loud laughter, he chased after her, shouting behind her, "Wait for me! I'll go with you!" He also followed Carole to have some fun. Of course, Bing Crosby knew that Carole was making fun of him, but how many Hollywood stars can withstand this kind of public prank?

This was not the first time Carole Lombard and Bing Crosby played pranks on each other. One day, director Norman Taurog led a large group of people on his private yacht to scout locations and take a break. Everyone had agreed beforehand to bring some food to treat their friends. Bing Crosby happened to forget to bring anything and ran to the yacht empty-handed. Everyone knew that Bing Crosby was known for being forgetful. This time, he probably forgot, and they said he was a Jew who wouldn't spend money. She pestered Bing until he had no choice but to promise that he would treat everyone to champagne as soon as the ship docked. But later, when they arrived at Catalina Island, they still didn't have any champagne to drink. Clearly, Bing Crosby had already forgotten again. The next day, while Bing was filming, he suddenly received a telegram. He opened it and saw only the word "Now" written on it. He knew Carole was joking with him again. He just laughed it off. Unexpectedly, fifteen minutes later, while filming was in full swing, he received another telegram. He opened it and it was also the word "Now" written on a blank piece of paper. He just laughed it off again. Ten minutes later, he received another telegram, with the same word "Now" inside. Five minutes later, there was another telegram. From then on, a telegram arrived every minute. This made Bing Crosby flustered and unable to concentrate on filming. Finally, he realized that he hadn't fulfilled his promise of champagne to everyone. So he immediately ordered champagne. Sure enough, as soon as the champagne arrived, the telegrams stopped coming. But he had already received more than fifty telegrams. Of course, the telegram fees were all charged to Bing Crosby's account.

Of course, specializing in teasing people also has its own risks. Carole Lombard herself admitted that she had been tricked by director Norman Taurog. She still laughs when she talks about it. Norman had recently made a film that used a large bear. But the bear's training was not very good. By the time the film was finished, he was covered in sweat. From then on, he not only didn't want to see the bear again, but he didn't want to hear the name of the bear mentioned. Carole Lombard heard this and deliberately got a big bear, put it in a large wooden box, and had someone send it to Norman's house at night when he was about to go to sleep. Norman was very angry when he saw the big bear Carole sent him. Later, he thought, since she wants to trick him, why not think of a way to resist. He thought for a long time, then his brow furrowed, and an idea came to him. He immediately ordered someone to call the animal farm and have the bear put in a car and taken to the animal farm, saying that it was Carole Lombard's treasure and should be carefully cared for. He also had a special and exquisite room built for the bear, and all the expenses were to be paid by Carole. Unexpectedly, the big bear got sick as soon as it arrived at the animal farm, so he specially hired a famous veterinarian and used round-the-clock nursing to treat the bear for several months and cure its illness. He then drove the bear back to Carole's house and attached a bill for rearing and medical expenses. This time, she suffered a loss of several thousand dollars. But Carole laughed out loud when she was tricked herself.

Of course, the above words are not entirely without meaning. Foreigners say that Chinese people have no sense of humor at all. They get angry and lose their temper at the slightest provocation. Theaters and taverns are supposed to be places for fun, but they often encounter scolding and fighting. After reading this article, one will understand the principle of "knowing fun and being happy," and not just making oneself suffer.

Film Review

Review of "Lady by Choice"

— Ling He

Lady by Choice - Cathay

After the old actress May Robson, she performed in this work that was enough to give full play to her acting skills. Coupled with Carole Lombard's strong and individual acting skills, "Lady by Choice" can satisfy people in terms of acting. But it is a pity that the excellent acting skills are built on a fantasy story. Because the story is not a representation of reality, the result is that excellent acting skills are only equal to waste, because everything in the play does not give people a real emotion.

What is the theme of the play? A young girl who disregards morality and often violates criminal laws should be combined with a young man who loves her wholeheartedly. In order to achieve this theme, the playwright makes a wandering old woman become a dignified and noble lady after her life is satisfied, not drinking, not making trouble, and using herself as a model for young girls. Such a persuasive effect is unnecessary to say.

Perhaps people think that a dancer's publicist uses the dancer's arrest or solicitation of a mother as top-notch publicity material; it's quite light and interesting, but this has no other effect other than to combine young boys and girls.

After watching this film, we feel that May Robson's acting is extremely good, but other aspects do not give us a deeper impression. The first half is very light, lively, and interesting. Director David Burton did handle these places very successfully, but in the second half, it gradually fell into stagnation and dullness.

There is nothing else to say.

Audience Opinions

Regarding the performance of "The Goddess"

— Yafei

After I finished watching the film "The Goddess," I felt that this new playwright has great hope for the future. Of course, he has already given us some good impressions in this initial debut work.

Undoubtedly, here we can see that the playwright already has a considerable understanding of the current society, although his subjective views still need to be discussed.

No matter what, "The Goddess" is a very realistic expression in terms of subject matter. Although this is just a simple story, it has very smoothly developed the social and ethical tragedy; a woman sells her body and soul for the sake of her beloved son; and in order to make her child grow up and improve, she is willing to give the money she earns from selling smiles to her child to study; but the snobbish educator wants to investigate the profession of her parents. How can she answer this? In the end, the child cannot get the opportunity to be educated, and the embarrassing mockery makes her very sad!

The rogue forcibly occupies a private prostitute. Due to the control of the environment, she has no choice but to endure the cold treatment and the ruthless trampling and is subdued under the iron hooves of the devil's lust, but in the end, she can no longer bear it and is sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment!

"This is a social problem," I believe no one will deny this. The playwright has correctly grasped this, and under his clever analysis, he emphatically developed it through the old principal's narrative. This subtle technique is really commendable.

Speaking of the director, there are also many new gains, such as (1) taking Ruan Lingyu and Li Keng from Zhang Zhizhi's crotch to express being subdued, (2) the re-shooting of Ruan Lingyu in Zhang Zhizhi's palm, illustrating that she cannot escape his control, (3) Ruan Lingyu's trial in court and the transformation of the prison scene, etc., are all rare successes. In addition, the narration of the whole play is also very concise and clear; however, the blandness of the climax part seems to lack consideration.

In terms of performance, Ruan Lingyu's expression of double personality is very powerful, and Li Keng's acting talent will naturally not disappoint us. Zhang Zhizhi looks like a typical "playboy," and Li Junpan is also quite satisfactory.

Finally, we are looking forward to Mr. Wu making greater contributions in the second time and meeting us.

A Bunch of Tianyi News

— Bai Yun

Set designer Zhou Hekang specially remodeled a prison car with a truck for filming "Model Youth," which is no different from a court prison car.

The sound film "Model Youth" is scheduled to shoot a scene in front of a dance hall today, and the set is extremely grand and magnificent.

"Baihuazhou" is one of Tianyi's new films, starring Chen Yumei, Ye Qiuxin, Yu Guang, and Chen Qixia. It is said that it has been scheduled to be screened at the Carlton Grand Theater this month.

Wang Pingling's "Spring in Zijin Mountain" is now in preparation.

"Red Mansion Spring Deep" has been screened at the Far East Grand Theater in Changsha, Hunan for more than a week, and it is full every day. (Actually)

Correction of Letters

Dear Editor, I read the December 5th

Your publication published a news item about the capital air defense exercise news film produced by Yihua Company, which is quite different from the facts. After investigation, this time, our stock was ordered to rush from Gan to Beijing to shoot various exercise situations to create a public air defense education film for our stock's patrol and projection team to project in the mainland and in the army's rural areas. Because the number of photographers in our stock was insufficient, we specially telegraphed Comrade Yuan Congmei, director of our stock, to temporarily hire. Then, directors Shi Dongshan and Zheng Yingshi and photographers Zhou Ke and Wang Yang of Yihua Company enthusiastically supported and participated in this work together. All materials and reception expenses were borne by our stock. Matters related to national defense are not the same as ordinary news that can be freely obtained. The duty of our stock lies in this, and we specially send a letter to clarify, and hope to correct it. I wish you good health.

Political Training Office of the Chairman of the Military Committee, Nanchang Military Camp, Film Share, December Day

The above news was printed on publicity materials by Yihua Company. Since it is inconsistent with the facts, it is hereby corrected. Editor Bai

Movie Novel

Mother and Daughter's Fate (Lady by Choice) (8)

— Zhong Jia

When Alabama heard Johnny say that he would rather give up his family fortune to marry her, she burst into tears of joy and said, "You are a young man with millions of dollars, and you are willing to give up your family fortune for me, but can you promise me that you will live a poor life in the future?" Johnny laughed and shouted, "We will be as poor as beggars in the future. We earn money and spend it all. When we are old, we will move to a nursing home. This is what comes from my conscience." After he finished speaking, he hugged Alabama and kissed her wildly. At this time, Alabama was already happy and dreamy. She was like going to a fairyland she had visited before, where she had dreamed of when she was a little girl, long before she changed her personality. That dream is now reappearing before her. The next day, Alabama suddenly received a call from Judge Darting to ask her to come. She immediately ran to the judge's place. The judge looked at her and felt a little strange. He had a relationship with this feather fan dance expert, but now the god of fate has brought her to him again. A few months ago, she was arrested for nude dancing and released by her. Now, outside of her duties, she wants to have some negotiations with this woman, because two people have come to ask her to help interfere with this woman's behavior. One is Johnny's mother, and the other is Pansy. After listening to their statements, she felt that their views were correct. Now she saw this woman standing in front of her, and when she mentioned Johnny's name, her eyes were almost tearful. When she advised her not to marry Johnny, her lips trembled in fear. When she told her that she would ruin Johnny's entire future, she could see the pain in her heart. But she also thought that she was an actress, or she might be performing for her. But in the end, she listened to Judge Darting's advice and agreed not to marry Johnny. When Alabama withdrew, she saw Pansy in the room again. When Pansy saw Alabama, she went up and hugged her and kissed her lips. Alabama also became happy. Pansy also knew that Alabama had changed, so when Alabama asked her to go back together, they went together. But from then on, Alabama's eyes and lips no longer showed her smile, and she trembled when the phone rang. She refused to see Johnny and didn't even talk to him. When Pansy saw this scene, she remembered that there was a girl who cried all night for love. She was also so sad, just because she wanted to do a reasonable thing and forget her lover, and the voice and smile of that lover were exactly the same as Johnny now. Where did that girl go then? Later, she became an old and frail Pansy. She remembered everything she had experienced before, how could she bear to watch Alabama repeat her mistakes. Later, Alabama went to her former manager Kendall to restore her feather fan dance life. This time, Pansy couldn't bear it anymore. She ran to Johnny and told him everything that had happened to Alabama recently. So Johnny and Pansy immediately ran to Judge Darting's place again. That night, the place where Alabama was dancing was surrounded by the police again, and Alabama was arrested. After Alabama was arrested, she laughed wildly. Of course, it was not a happy and licentious laugh, but her laughter was filled with the infinite pain in her heart and the hatred for life. She was brought before the judge, and she still laughed coldly. The judge pretended to be calm and said, "Arrested again, right? This time I'm going to execute the previous announcement of the situation. What do you have to say?" Alabama sneered, "Just execute it. No one is stopping you." Johnny heard this and suddenly stepped forward and hugged her and said, "No, baby. There is still one way to go, and that is for you to marry me. Otherwise······" Alabama exclaimed in surprise, "You!" She wanted to persuade him not to be infatuated, so as not to hinder his future, but she couldn't open her mouth, because Johnny's lips had already sealed her mouth, because Pansy and the judge were also looking at them and smiling at each other. (The End)
